AmaLunga Edale (AM-Assembly Members ngesiNgisi) aseWelsh akhathathazekile 'ngokubonakala njengabopopayi'
Amanye amaLunga Edale (AM) asephelelwe ngodaba lokusikisela kokuthi ibizo lawo kumele litshintshwe lithiwe WMP (iLunga leDale lePhalamende yaseWelsh).
Lokhu kubangelwe ngamacebo okutshintsha ibizo ledale libe liDale lePhalamende yaseWelsh.
AmaLunga Edale (AM) asezingxenyeni ezitshiyeneyo zezombusazwe akhathazeka ngokuthi lokhu kungawenza abe yinhlekisa.
Omunye oLilunga leDale (AM) oweQembu Elimela Izisebenzi uthe iqembu lakhe likhathazekile ngokuthi "lokhu kuzwakala angathi ngu-Twp lo-Pwp."
Kubabali abangaphandle kweWales: EWelsh u-twp utsho ubuphukuphuku njalo u-pwp utsho uthuvi.
ILunga leDale (AM) lasePlaid lathi iqembu lilonke nje "lalingathokozi" njalo lisikisela okwehlukileyo.
OweWelsh Oweqembu Elisabambelele Koludala wathi iqembu lakhe "limbono obanzi" ngokutshintshwa kwebizo, kodwa watsho ukuthi kumane kuyikusuka kubala elithi MWP usiya kwelithi Popayi.
Nxa kukhangelwa udaba ngalelicele ibala u-w ngesiWelsh libizwa ngokufananayo lebala lesiNgisi saseYorkshire u-u.
IKhomishini yeDale, esaphakathi kokubona ngokwenziwa kwemithetho yokutshintshwa kwamabizo, yathi: "Isinqumo sokucina salokho okungabe kuchasisa ukuthi amaLunga eDale azabizwa ngokuthini sizakuba yindaba yamalunga ngokwawo."
UMthetho kaHulumende waseWales oka-2017 wapha idale laseWelsh amandla okutshintsha ibizo lalo.
NgoJune, iKhomishini yethula impumela ngemva kokubuza uzulu ngalokho okusikiselwayo kwatholakala ukuthi abanengi basekela ukubiza idale ngokuthi iPhalamende YaseWelsh.
Odabeni lwebizo lamaLunga eDale (AM), iKhomishini yasekela kakhulu ukuthi AmaLunga eDale lePhalamende YaseWelsh kumbe WMP (Welsh Parliament Members ngesiNgisi), kodwa ukuthi MWP yikho okwasekelwa ngabanengi kakhulu ngesikhathi kubuzwa uzulu.
Kukhanya AmaLunga eDale (AM) asikisela okwehlukileyo, kodwa umzamo onzima wokufika esivumelwaneni ungamtshayisa ngekhanda uSibalukhulu u-Elin Jones, olindelwe ukuthi phakathi kwamavikinyana ethule ukuthi ukwenziwa kwemithetho yakhona kuzaba lesimo bani ngotshintsho.
Ukwenziwa kwemithetho ngalokho okumele kuguqulwe kuzagoqela olunye utshintsho endleni yokuthi idale lisebenza njani, okugoqela imiqondiso ngokungafaneleki kwamaLunga eDale (AM) kanye lokuhlela ukusebenza kwekhomithi.
AmaLunga eDale (AM) azavota okokucina ngombuzo wokuthi kumele abizwe ngokuthini kungxoxo-mpikiswano ngokuthi umthetho wakhona uzakwenziwa njani.
Izakhamizi zeMacedonia zenza ukhetho lokutshintsha ibizo lelizwe labo
NgeSonto kuzakhethwa ukuthi ibizo lelizwe litshintshwe yini kube yi "Republic of North Macedonia."
Ukhetho lolu luzaqeda ukungazwanani ngoba sekuleminyaka ilizwe leGreece elingumakhelwane likhonona ngoba lalo lilesabelo okuthiwa yiMacedonia.
Abase-Athens bathi ilizwe elingumakhelwana elisenyakatho kungani libathathela indawo yabo futhi lilwisana lokuthi libe lilunga le-EU le-NATO.
Umongameli weMacedonia uGjorge Ivanov kavumelani lokuthi kube lokhetho lolu njalo uthi kasoze avumelane lokuzakhethwa.
Abanye abasekela utshintsho lolu okugoqela uPrime Minister uZoran Zaev bathi iMacedonia kumele izimisele ukutshintsha ibizo nxa ifuna ukuba lilunga le-EU lele- NATO.
Kuthule Cwaka eSt Martin Ngoba Amasonto eHarlem Athwele Nzima
Umnumzana Adams uthe: "Abantu asebekhulile engikhulume labo bathe wawubona amasonto lamabhawa loba ngaphi ohamba khona."
"Lamuhla, akusekho konke lokhu."
Uthe ukuvalwa kwamabhawa kuyazwisiseka.
Uphinde wathi: "Abantu sebezilibazisa ngezinto ezitshiyeneyo lamuhla."
"Akusajayelekanga kangako ukuthi abantu bayegcwala emabhawa."
Kodwa ukhathazekile ngokuthi nxa izinto ezisemasontweni zingathengiswa, imali leyo iyabe incane kulalokho okukhangelelwe ngabakhokhelayo ngoba "bazasala bengelalutho njengasekuqaliseni."
Uphinde wathi uthe izakhiwo zamasonto lezi zingacina sokuzindawo zokuthi abantu abangalani lokukhonza bacine bezihlalela kuzo.
Uthe, "Kukhanya angani abantu abanengi abazathenga izakhiwo lezi ngabamhlophe, lokhu kuzakwenza ukuthi amasonto lawa avale masinya ngoba bazabe bebalutshwana kakhulu labo abathenge izakhiwo lezi abazaba ngamalunga amasonto lawa."
Amasonto womabili akhiwa ngabamhlophe indawo yaseHarlem ingakabi labantu abansundu abanengi - IMetropolitan Community ngo 1870, iSt Martin’s sekudlule iminyaka elitshumi.
Ibandla lesonto yeMethodist labamhlophe laphuma ngabo-1930.
Ibandla labansundu elalikhonzela duzane khonapho lathatha isakhiwo lesi.
URev. John Howard Johnson nguye owayekhokhela ibandla labansundu elathatha iSt. Martin’s, nguye owakhokhela ukuvukela okwenziwa ngababethengisa endaweni edumileyo u-125 Street eHarlem, njalo wayengafuni lokuthi abantu abansundu baqhatshwe kumbe ukuthi baphiwe izikhundla ezingcono emisebenzini.
Umlilo watshisa isakhiwo lesi ngo 1939 kodwa ngesikhathi abasekeli bakaFather Johnson behlela ukuthi baphinde bakhe, bafaka lamabhera.
Umntaka Father Johnson, uRev. David Johnson nguye owacina esekhokhela eSt Martin’s futhi wathi "amabhera lawa ngawabayanga."
Kodwa eyinye ingcitshi eyatshaya amabhera lawa ngoJuly yayilokunye eyayikucabanga: Yathi "Yinto eligugu" njalo "akula enye into esingayithola edlula amabhera lawa."
Ingcitshi le nguTiffany Ng oweYunivesithi eseMichigan, uphinde wathi uDionisio A. Lind umhlabeleli onsundu nguye owayengowokuqala ukutshaya amabhera lawa amakhulu esontweni eseRiverside eminyakeni engu 18 eyayidlulile.
Umnumzana Merriweather uthe iSt Martin’s ayimthathelanga indawo.
Okwenzakale eSt Martin’s ezinyangeni ezisanda kudlula kunzima ukuzwisisa, kulokungazwanani phakathi kwabadweba amaplani okwakha lalabo abaqhatshwa ukuthi benze lowo msebenzi, ikanti okunye kubangelwa yikungazwanani kwabakhokheli besonto lamaBhishopi.
Abanye abakhokheli ababumba iqula lesonto labhalela amaBhishopi ngoJuly bekhalaza ngokuthi kungani kumele babhadale abantu abadweba amaplani labenza umsebenzi bona babengekho ngesikhathi kusenziwa isinqumo leso ngamaBhishopi.
Abanye abangena isonto le bebesola ukuthi yindaba amaBhishopi esenza izinto ezingacaciyo.

ISainsbury isithengisa ezokuzilungisa lezokubukeka e-UK
ISainsbury isithenge uBoots, iSuperdrug leDebenhams futhi izitolo zayo zigcwele izinto ezinengi ezifunwa ngabantu ukuze bazilungise babebahle.
Kusetshenziswe imali efika amaPound angu 2.8 bhiliyoni ukuze lokhu kuphumelele, phela ezokuzilungisa lokubukeka sezithandwa kakhulu ukwedlula ifeshini lezinto ezisetshenziswa ezindlini, izinto lezi zifakwe zaba zinengi emashelufini amakhulu ezitolo ezingu-11 ezitshiyeneyo futhi kuhlelwa ukuthi zizatholakala lakwezinye izitolo ezinengi ngomnyaka ozayo nxa konke kuhambe kuhle.
Okwenza bacabange ngezokuzilungisa lokubukeka yikuthi izitolo sezisele zilendawo enkulu engelalutho ngemva kokuthi abantu behambise izitolo lezi emithendwandaba ngenxa yamaTV, amamicrowave lezinye impahla zendlini.
ISainsbury isizaphinda kabili inani lezinto zokuzilungisa elizithengisayo, kuzatholakala izinto ezedlula 3,000 okugoqela ezilungiswa yiRevlon, Essie, Tweezerman leDr. Bazaqalisa lokuthengisa okulungiswa yiPawpaw.
Okunye abahlezi belakho okulungiswa yiL’Oreal, Maybelline le Burts’Bees kuzabe sokulendawo enkulu njalo ebhalwe ngendlela efanana laleyo etholakala ezitolo ezinjengoBoots.
Isitolo lesi sizakwenza lotshintsho ezintweni zokuzicomba ukuze ezinengi kube ngezingela mafutha enyamazana kumbe okunye nje okuthethwe enyamazaneni ngoba lokhu kuhambelana lokufunwa ngabanengi abasakhulayo.
AbeFragrance Shop abathengisa ama-perfume bazakhulumisana lezitolo ezimbili zeSainsbury, isitolo sakuqala sivulwe ngeviki ephelileyo eCroydon eningizimu yeLondon, ikanti esesibili sizavulwa eSelly Oak eBirmingham umnyaka lo ungakapheli.
Ukuthenga kusetshenziswa i-internet lokuthenga izinto ezilutshwana ezitolo ezincane eziseduze lalapho abantu abahlala khona, sokusitsho ukuthi izitolo ezinkulu sokumele zenze konke ezikwenelisayo ukuze abantu baye kuzo.
Umphathi omkhulu weSainsbury uMike Coupe uthe ngokuhamba kwesikhathi izitolo zabo lezi zizabe sezilakho konke okufunwa ngabantu okugoqela lezinto ezingadliwayo kodwa ezisethenziswa nsuku zonke ngoba bancintisana lezitolo ezithengisa ngentengo ephansi ezinjenge Aldi le Lidl.
ISainbury yafaka okuyizitolo kwe-Argos okuncane okunengi kakhulu njalo yafaka lezinye ezeHabitats kusukela yathenga izitolo lezi ezimbili eminyakeni emibili edlulileyo, bathi ukwenza njalo kwenze bathengisa izinto ezinengi kakhulu futhi lokhu kubalethele inzozo enengi.
ISainsbury yake yazama ukuthuthukisa ukuthengisa izinto zokuzilungisa lemithi kodwa yehluleka.
ISainsbury leBoots yake yazama ukusebenza ndawonye ekuqaliseni kwabo 2000 kodwa lokhu kwama ngoba kwaba lokungawelelani endabeni yokuthi imali eyayivela ekuthengiseni imithi kwakumele bayabelane njani.
ISainsbury iqalise ibhizimusi le ngemva kokuthengisela umnikazi weLloyds Pharmacy uCelesio ipharmacy yabo elezitezi ezingu 281, ngamaPound angu 125 miliyoni eminyakeni emithathu edlulileyo.
Bathe leli licebo elihle ngoba iLloyds ilamafutha atshiyeneyo njalo amahle kakhulu agoqela iLa Roche-Posay leVichy abazawafaka ezitolo ezines.
Umaqhuzu wezokuthengisa weSainsbury uPaul Mills-Hicks uthe: "Sesitshintshe okunengi kakhulu emashelufini alezinto lezi ezokuzilungisa ngoba sifuna abathengayo bakukholise ukuba lapha.
Siphinde sadinga labantu abazingcitshi emsebenzini lo ukuze bancedise loba ngubani ofuna ukuncediswa.
Loba kuyini abantu abakufunayo ukuze babukeke kuhle silakho, izitolo zethu ziyabukeka okwamagama njalo zitholakala endaweni ezinengi, lokhu kusenza sibedlule khatshana bonke abanye abasadla ngoludala endabeni zokuthengisa."

UPeter Jones owayengumlingiswa ku-Dragons Den usele ‘ezondile’ ngemva kokuthi uHolly Willoughby owenzisa olunye uhlelo ku-TV ethe kasafuni baqhubeke ngebhizimusi yabo yama pound angu 11-miliyoni esithi kafuni kube lolu oluzamphambanisa njengoba esezasebenza le-Marks and Spencer kanye le-ITV
UWilloughby kalasikhathi sebhizimusi yabo yempahla zendlini leyezinto zokucecisa ezilebizo okuthiwa yi-Truly.
Ibhizimusi yalaba ababili ifaniswe lekaGwyneth Paltrow okuthiwa yi-Goop.
Owenzisa uhlelo lwe-This Morning oleminyaka engu-37 ubhale umlayezo ku-Instagram esithi setshiya ibhizimusi le.
UHolly Willoughby utshiye umlingiswa weDragons Den uPeter Jones esidla amalahle ngoba etshiye ibhizimusi yabo ukuze asebenze leMarks and Spencer kanye le-ITV.
Kuthiwa uJones "ubezondile" emhlanganweni ababelawo losisi lo othandwa ngabanengi owenza uhlelo kuTV, babelomhlangano lo ngoLwesibili emawofisini abo amakhulu aseMarlow eBuckinghamshire njalo wathi umsebenzi lo ungamnika imali efika amapound angu 1.5 miliyoni futhi lokhu kumtshiya engaselasikhathi sebhizimusi yabo eye-Truly.
Ibhizimusi le ifaniswe lekaGwyneth Paltrow okuthiwa yi-Goop futhi bekucatshangelwa ukuthi izayiphinda kabili imali kaWilloughby engaba ngamaPound angu-11 miliyoni.
UWilloughby oleminyaka engu 37 uthe ebhala umlayezo wokuthi usetshiya iTruly kuInstagram, uJones yena ubegada indizamtshina esiya eBritain kweyinye yezindlu zakhe ajayele ukuyisebenzisa ukuze aphumule.
Omunye wabika ukuthi: "UHolly ubeyiqakathekisa kakhulu iTruly.
Bekuzakuba yibhizimusi akade ezasebenza kuyo futhi imncede okweminyaka eminengi elandelayo.
Ukukhetha kwakhe ukutshiya ibhizimusi kutshiye abanengi akade besebenza laye bethithibele.
Kwakunzima ukuthi abantu bakukholwe okwenzakala ngoLwesibili, kwasekuseduze ukuthi ibhizimusi iqalise.
Kulempahla ezinengi kakhulu emawofisini amakhulu aseMarlow ezilindele ukuthengiswa."
Izingcitshi zithi ukutshiya kowesifazana lo odume kangaka owenza uhlelo lweThis Morning ibhizimusi le kuzabadlela imali enengi ngoba besekuthengwe amacushion, amakhandlela, izigqoko lempahla zendlini njalo kukhanya angani ibhizimusi le isizaphuza ukuqalisa.
Kukhanya angani lobungane babo osebuleminyaka bukhona bungaphela.
UWilloughby lomkakhe uDan Baldwin balabantwana abathathu njalo sebeleminyaka elitshumi bengabangane bakaJones lonkosikazi wakhe uTara Capp.
UWilloughby loCapp baqalisa iTruly ngo 2016 kwazothi uJones oleminyaka engu-52 waqalisa ukusebenza labo engumgcinisihlalo ngoMarch.
Imuli lezi zombili zijayele ukuzilibazisa ndawonye futhi uJones ule 40 phesenti ekhampanini kaBaldwin ekhipha inhlelo zeTV.
UWilloughby uzabe esemele iMarks and Spencer kwezokubukisa impahla zabo njalo uzathatha indawo ka Ant McPartlin kuhlelo lwe ITV oluthiwa I'm A Celebrity.

ITsunami Lokuzamazama Komhlaba Kubhidlize Isihlenge saseIndonesia, Kwafa Izikhulu Zabantu
Ngemva kokuzamazama komhlaba eLombok, inhlanganiso ezingayisizo zikahulumende zakwamanye amazwe zitsheliwe ukuthi zingabuyi ukuzoncedisa.
Lanxa i10 phesenti yezakhamuzi zeLombok zilahlekelwe yimizi yabo, ilizwe kalizange libizele ukuthi kulomonakalo welizwe, okuyindlela abahlala beyisebenzisa ukuthi bengatholi usizo kwamanye amazwe.
"Kuzwisa usizi ukuthi endabeni ezinengi, bakhuluma egcekeni ukuthi kabafuni usizo kwamanye amazwe, okubangela ukuthi umonakalo wakhona ube nzima," watsho njalo umama uSumbung.
Lanxa iSave the Children ilezisebenzi eziya ePalu, azila qiniso lokuthi bazavunyezwa yini ukusebenza.
Isikhulumeli senhlanganiso somonakalo wezwe leIndonesia, uSutopo, wathi iziphathamandla zaseIndonesia bezihlolisisa okwenzakala ePalu ukuthi zibone nxa usizo oluvela kwamanye amazwe ludingakala.
Lanxa eIndonesia kuhlala kusiba lomonakalo wokuzamazama komhlaba, kuzwisa ubuhlungu ukuthi bahlala bengalungiselelanga umonakalo lowu.
EAceh kulezindlu ezayakwayo zokuzivikela kuTsunami, kodwa kwezinye izindawo azikho lezo zindlu.
Izakhamuzi zasePalu zazitsheliwe ngomonakalo lowu, kodwa ukuswelakala kwesayirini ePalu yikho okungabe kwabangela ukufa kwabantu.
Lanxa umumo uvuma, ukuhambahamba ezihlengeni zaseIndonesia kunzima.
Izingozi lezi ezizenzakalela zodwa zenza ukuthi imisebenzi ibe nzima ukuyiyenza.
Isikepe sasesibhedlela kade siseLombok, sinakekela abayehlelwe yikuzamazama komhlaba, sokumele siye ePalu lapho okulomonakalo omutsha, kodwa sizathatha amalanga amathathu ukuthi siyefika khona.
UMongameli weLizwe laseIndonesia uJoko Widodo, uhlose ukufaka kuqala ukulungiswa kwezakhiwo ezilinyaziweyo eIndonesia njengomkhankaso wakhe wamavoti awezombusazwe, njalo ufake imali enengi ekulungisweni komgwaqo owezimota lowezitimela.
Kodwa ukungatholi imali ekwaneleyo kuphambanise uhlelo lukaMongameli uJoko labaphathi bakhe njengoba bekhangelane lokuvota umnyaka olandelayo.
UMongameli uJoko ulolunye uhlupho olubangelwa ngabasekeli besiMuslim, abasebelezindlela zabo ezicatshileyo zokukholwa esezibangele ukuba lamabhazu.
Abantu abedlula 1 000 babulawa, njalo abantu abedlula izigidi bakhitshwa ezindlini zabo lapho ixhuku lamaKristu lamaMuslims beze beqalise ukulwa emigwaqweni besebenzisa izinqamu ezinkulu, lemikonto lokunye okulimazayo.

USturridge wapaselwa nguXherdan Shaqiri esesekhatshana ngamayadi angu-30 ukusuka egedini leChelsea ithimu yakhe isadliwe 1-0.

Lahambela phezu kwebhokisi liqonga lisiya ekhoneni elingakwesokudla senethi.
Ibhola lacina lisehlela phezu kukaKepa Arrizabalaga layawela enethini.
"Ngangizama nje ukuthi ngibe sendaweni enjalo, ngizuze ibhola njalo abadlali abanjengo Shaq bahlala belitshayela phambili ngazo zonke izindlela, ngakho ngazama nje ukuthi ngiziphe ithuba elaneleyo," uSturridge watshela iLiverpoolFC.com.
"Ngabona uKante esiza ngasengilitshaya kanye njalo angizange ngicabange ngakho kakhulu ngahle ngayitshaya imvema."
IChelsea yayikhokhela nge 1-0 ekupheleni kwengxenye yokuqala ngomzuzu wesi-25 ngemva kokuhlohla komdlali waseBelgium oyingcitshi u-Eden Hazard.
Odlalela phambili oweBlues walipasela emuva kuMateo Kovacic ekudlaleni lokho engakalisusi maduzane laphakathi kwenkundla wavula ijubane engena engxenyeni yeLiverpool.
UKovacic waphangisa ukulipasa egijima ephakathi laphakathi kwenkundla.
Wasuka watshaya imvema yebhola, okwenza ukuthi uHazard angene ebhokisini.
UHazard wabatshiya bonke abavimba bengasemuva waseliqedisela enethini yeposti ekhatshana ngemvema ayitshaya ngonyawo lobunxele isedlula u-Alisson Becker oweLiverpool.
ILiverpool izadibana leNapoli emdlalweni yamaqembu yeLigi yeZingqwele ngo-3 emini ngoLwesithathu eStadio San Paolo eNaples e-Italy.
IChelsea izahlangana leVideoton kuLigi ye-UEFA Europa ngo-3 emini ngoLwesine eLondon.
Inani labafileyo kutsunami yase-Indonesia seliqonge laya ku-832
Inani labafileyo ekuzamazameni komhlaba kanye letsunami e-Indonesia seliqanse laya ku-832, kutsho uhlangothi lwelizwe olubona ngezezingozi zemvelo ngeSonto ekuseni.
Kubikwa ukuthi abantu abanengi bebenyathezelwe emfucufucwini yezakhiwo ekuzamazameni komhlaba okubekulamandla emaginitshuthi engu-7.5 okwahlasela ngoLwesihlanu njalo kwabangela amagagasi ayephakame okufinyelela amafidi angu-20, isikhulumeli sohlangothi uSutopo Purwo Nugroho satshela iqula lentathelizindaba.

Amapholisa abopha indoda, eleminyaka engu-32, ngemva kokucatshangelwa ukuthi igwaze owesifazane wafa
Sekusungulwe ukuchwayisisa ngodaba ngemva kokutholakala kwesidumbu sowesifazane eBirkenhead, eMerseyside lamuhla ekuseni.
Oleminyaka engu-44 utholakale eGrayson Mews ekuJohn Street ngo-7:55 ekuseni elamanxeba okugwazwa, njalo indoda eleminyaka engu-32 ibotshiwe kucatshangelwa ukuthi yiyo embuleleyo.
Amapholisa akhuthaze abantu bakuleyondawo abangabe bebone kumbe bezwa loba yini ukuthi bazobika.
Umcuphi u-Inspector Brian O'Hagan uthe: 'Ukuchwayisisa ngodaba kusaqalisa kodwa sincenga loba ngubani obeseduze loJohn Street eBirkenhead obone kumbe wezwa loba yini esolisayo ukuthi asithinte.
Ngithanda njalo ukuncenga loba ngubani, ikakhulu abatshayeli bamatekisi, abangabe beshute loba yini ngamakhamera asemoteni ukuba basithinte njengoba bengaba lolwazi oluqakathekileyo ekuchwayisiseni kwethu.'
Isikhulumeli samapholisa siqinisekise ukuthi isidumbu esitholakeleyo ngesowesifazane waseBirkenhead njalo sitholakale phakathi kweyadi.
Lamuhla emini abangane abacabanga ukuthi bayamazi owesifazane lo bafikile endaweni yakhona ukuze babuze imibuzo ngalapho atholakale khona lamuhla ekuse.
Ukuchwayisisa ngodaba kusaqhubeka njengoba amapholisa esethe asebikela izihlobo eziseduze zomufi.
Umtshayeli wetekisi ohlala eGrayson Mews usanda kuzama ukubuyela efulathini lakhe kodwa utshelwa ngamapholisa ukuthi akulamuntu ovunyelwa ukungena loba ukuphuma esakhiweni.
Utshe amathe lapho ethola ukuthi kwenzakaleni.
Abahlala efulathini sebetshelwa ukuthi kuzathatha amahola athile bengakavunyelwa ukubuyela phakathi.
Elinye ipholisa lizwakale litshela enye indoda ukuthi indawo yonke isiphathwa njengendawo lapho okudalelwe khona icala.
Owesifazana uthutshe kuleyondawo ekhala izinyembezi.
Ulokhu ephindaphinda esithi 'kubuhlungu kakhulu'.
Ngo-2 emini amavani amapholisa abephakathi kwendawo egojolozelweyo futhi enye ivani ibingaphandle.
Amapholisa ambalwa abemiswe phakathi kwendawo egojolezelweyo enanzelela okwenzakala emafulathini.
Loba ngubani ongaba lolwazi ucelwa ukuthi athumele umlayezo DM *MerPolCC, afonele ku-101 kumbe athintane le-Crimestoppers engazivezi ukuthi ungubani ku-0800 555 111 eqamba udaba 247 lomhla ka-30 Mpandula.
Isithombe sikaCromwell esisephalamende siba ngesinye sezikhumbuzo ezisanda kuhlaselwa yingxabano 'yokubhala kutsha imbali'
Ukususwa kwaso kuzaba yikukhwitshiza okufaneleyo ngenxa yokubhidlizwa kwezinto ezinengi zamasiko lezenkolo zaseNgilandi okwenziwa ngabalandeli bakhe abeqisa amalawulo abesi-Puritan ngezindlela zakhe zobuThalibani.
Kodwa iNhlanganiso kaCromwell yachaza umcabango kaMnumzane Crick "njengongelangqondo" njalo "ukuzama ukubhala kutsha imbali."
UJohn Goldsmith, umgcinisihlalo weNhlanganiso kaCromwell, wathi: "Kwakuvele kusegcekeni ukuthi kungxoxo mpikiswano ngodaba lokukhitshwa kwezithombe ukuthi isifanekiso sika Oliver Cromwell esingaphandle kweSigodlo saseWestminster sizabe siqotshiwe.
Ukulwisana lemibono eyayisamukeleka odabeni lwezimpi zomndeni zamaNgisi kasuye uCromwell owathi kwenziwe kumbe owakwenzayo.
Mhlawumbe impambaniso uCromwell angabethelelwa ngayo yizenzo zikakhokho wakhe uThomas ekhulwini leminyaka eladlulayo.
Isithombe esihle kakhulu sikaCromwell esenziwa nguMhlonitshwa William Hamo siyibufakazi bokuthi abantu babelombono onjani ngekhulu leminyaka lesi-19 njalo uyingxenye yokwethulwa kwembali okuhlolisiswe kuhle ngomuntu osalokhu elabanengi abakholelwa ukuthi kumele athakazelelwe.
UMnumzana Goldsmith watshela iThe Sunday Telegraph: "UCromwell ubhekwa ngabanengi, engxenye abanengi kakhulu ngekhulu leminyaka lesi-19 kulakhathesi, njengomvikeli wephalamende ekucindezeleni okuvela ngaphandle, odabeni lwakhe sibili kutshiwo umbuso.
Ukuthi yikho sibili akumelayo ngeqiniso kuseseyindaba okuqhubeka iyingxoxo mpikiswano yembali.
Kodwa esileqiniso lakho yikuthi ingxabano yaphakathi laphakathi kwekhulu leminyaka lesi-17 yiyo edale intuthuko eyalandelayo yesizwe sethu, njalo uCromwell ngokwakhe ngumuntu osobala omela lolo uhlangothi.
Lokho aphumelela ukukwenza njengo Lord Protector lakho kumele kuthakazelelwe njalo kukhunjulwe."
Ingulube Ibulele Umfuyi eChina
Omunye umfuyi wengulube, ubulelwe yingulube emakethe esemzansi kwasentshonalanga eChina, njengokutshiwo kwabaphumisa indaba esabelweni leso.
Indoda elesibongo esithi, "Yuan," utholakele efile, umthambo wakhe ohambisa igazi udatshuliwe njalo egcwele igazi, duzane lesibaya sengulube eLiupanshui esabelweni saseGuizhou, iSouth China Morning Post itsho njalo ngeSonto.
Umfuyi wengulube ulungiselela ukuhlaba ingulube umuthi ovikela imikhuhlane eplazini lengulube mhlaka 30 May 2005 eXining esabelweni saseQinghai, eChina.
Kuthiwa ubuye lomzawakhe bevela esabelo esingomakhalwane esithiwa yiYunnan ngoLweSithathu ukuthi bezothengisa ingulube ezingu15 emakethe.
Ilangaelalandelayo ekuseni umzawakhe wamuthola esefile, njalo wabona ukuthi umnyango wesibaya sengulube esiseceleni kwabo wawuvulekile.
Umzawakhe lo uthe phakathi kwesibaya lesi bekulengulube enduna enkulu kade ile gazi emlonyeni walo.
Kuripoti yabo, abahlolayo ukuthi kwenzakale njani, bavumile ukuthi ingulube leyi engabe iweya amaphawundi angu-550 (amakhilogramu angu 250) yiyo ebulale umfuyi lo.
"Izinyawo zikamzawami bezigcwele igazi njalo zisikasikiwe," watsho njalo umzawakhe kamufi olesibongo esithi, "Wu," njengokutshiwo ngendaba zaGuiyang Evening News.
Ikhamera eyevhidhiyo yatshengisa uYuan engena emakethe ukuthi azonika ukudla ingulube zakhe ngoLweSine ngo4:40 ekuseni.
Ngemva kwehora elilodwa yikho lapho abathola isidumbu sakhe.
Inyamazana ebulele uYuan kade ingasiyo yakhe kumbe umzawakhe.
Umphathi wasemakethe utshele abendaba zaEvening News ukuthi, ingulube yakhona ihle yavalelwa ukwenzela ukuthi ingalimazi omunye umuntu, njalo ukwenzela ukuthi amapolisa bahlolisise ukuthi kwenzakeleni.
Kufakazwe ukuthi, imuli kaYuan labaphathamandla bemakethe, baxoxisana ngombhadhalo okumele uyenzwe ngenxa yokufa kukaYuan.
Lanxa kungajwayelekanga, indaba lezi zengulube zihlasela abantu zake zayenzakala kudala.
Ngomnyaka ka2016, ingulube yake yahlasela omunye umama lendoda yakhe eplazini labo laseMassachusetts, yatshiya indoda ilimele kakhulu.
Iminyaka elitshumi edlulileyo, ingulube eyayisinda amaphawundi angu-650 (amakhilogramu angu-290) yafithizela omunye umfuyi ongumuWelsh kutirakitha yakhe, yaze yayethuselwa ngumfazi kamfuyi lo ukuthi imuyekele.
Ngomnyaka ka2012, ngemva komunye umfuyi waseOregon edliwe zingulube zakhe, omunye umfuyi waseManitoba watshela abendaba zeCBC ukuthi ingulube kazijwayelanga ukuba lolaka, kodwa zingavele zidle igazi, yikho lapho eziba khona ngolaka.
"Ziyabe zizidlalela nje.
Ziyenza njengani ngabantwana abancane, abafuna ukuba kwazi okunengi ... kazihlosanga ukukulimaza.
Kumele uziphe inhlonipho ezizifaneleyo kuphela," watsho njalo.
Insalela zeSikhukhula uRosa zizaletha izulu elinengi kuyo yonke indawo eningizimu-ntshonalanga kwe-US
Njengokucatshangelwayo, iSikhukhula uRosa sesiphela amandla njengoba sihamba phezu kwamanzi aqandelelayo ngasokhunjini olusenyakatho kweMexico.
Lanxa kunjalo, uRosa uzaletha izulu elikhukhulayo ngasezindaweni ezisenyakatho kweMexico kanye laseningizimu-ntshonalanga U.S. emalangeni azayo.
URosa ubelomoya olesiqubu samamayira angu-85 ngehola (amakhilomitha angu-137 ngehola), Isigaba 1 seSikhukhula, ngo-5 ekuseni. Ngesikhathi saseMpumalanga ngeSonto, njalo ubetholakala amamayira angu-385 (amakhilomitha angu-620) eningizimu-ntshonalanga kwePunta Eugenia, eMexico.
URosa ulindelwe ukuya ngasenyakatho ngeSonto.
Ngesikhathi esifananayo, umgelo womoya usuqalisa ukuvela ngaphezu koLwandle lwePacific usiya empumalanga ngasoKhunjini lwaseNtshonalanga lwe-U.S. Njengoba Rosa eqonde isihlengana seBaja California ngoMvulo njengezulu elilomoya uzaqalisa ukufuqa umoya omanzi olamandla usiya ngasenyakatho ungena eningizimu-ntshonalanga U.S.
URosa uzaletha izulu elifinyelela kumaintshi angu 10 (masentimitha angu-25) kwezinye izingxenye zeMexico.
Ngemva kwalokho, umoya omanzi undawonye lomgelo womoya ofikayo kuzadala izulu elinengi eNingizimu-ntshonalanga emalangeni azayo.
Kithi lapha, amaintshi aqalisela ku-1 kusiye ku-4 (amasentimitha aqalisela ku-3 kusiya ku-10) ezulu azabangela izikhukhula eziphangisayo eziyingozi, ukugeleza kwemfucumfucu njalo kungenzeka kube lokudilika komhlabathi enkangala.
Umoya omanzi olamandla uzabangela ukuthi inani lezulu liye kumaintshi angu-2 kusiya kwangu-3 (amasendimitha angu-5 kusiya kwangu-8) ngehola kwezinye izindawo, ikakhulu ezingxenyeni eziseningizimu Nevada le-Arizona.
Kulindelwe amaintshi angafika ku-2 kusiya ku-4 (amasendimitha angafika ku-5 kusiya ku-10) ezulu ezingxenyeni zaseNingizimu-ntshonalanga, ikakhulu phezu kwezindawo ezinengi ze-Arizona.
Kungenzeka kube lezikhukhula eziphangisayo lezimo eziqhubeka zisiba zimbi okubangelwa lizulu elilomoya lapha lalaphayana.
Kungaba yikungahlakaniphi ukuhamba enkangala ngenyawo khona kulokusongela kwezulu elilomoya.
Izulu elinengi lingabangela ukuthi izifudlana ezisezindaweni eziphansi zibe yimifula egcweleyo njalo izulu elilemibani lingaletha umoya olamandla amakhulukazi lesavunguzane kwelakithi.
Umgelo womoya ofikayo uzaletha izulu elinengi kwelakithi ezingxenyeni ezisokhunjini lweNingizimu California.
Kungenzeka kube lenani lezulu lonke eledlula ingxenye ye-intshi, okungabangela ukugeleza okuncane kwemfucumfucu lemigwaqo etshelelayo.
Leli kungaba yilo izulu lokuqala lesikhathi sokuna kwezulu esabelweni.
Izulu elilomoya lapha lalaphayana lizaqalisa ukufika e-Arizona ngeSonto ebusuku langoMvulo ekuseni, izulu lakhona likangafinyeleli kuyo yonke indawo ebusuku bangoMvulo langoLwesibili.
Izulu elinengi lizaba khona eMagumbini Amane ngoLwesibili litshonele ngoLwesithathu.
UMfumfu uzabona ukutshisa okutshintsha-tshintshayo kulo lonke elase-U.S. njengoba i-Artic izobe isiqandelela kodwa izindawo ezitshisayo zibe zilokhu zikhudumala.
Kwesinye isikhathi lokhu kubangela ukutshintsha okumangalisayo kokutshisa emimangweni eseduze laduze.
Kulesibonelo somehluko wokutshintsha kokutshisa okumangalisayo phakathi laphakathi kwe-U.S. ngeSonto.
Kuphose kube lomehluko wokutshisa wamadigiri angu-20 phakathi kweKansas City, eMissouri le-Omaha, eNabraska, laphakathi kweSt. Louis leDes Moines, e-Iowa.
Phakathi kwamalanga alandelayo, ukukhudumala kwehlobo okuphuza ukuphela kuzazama ukuba khona njalo kwande.
Ezindaweni ezinengi eziphakathi laphakathi lasempumalanga U.S. kulindelwe ukuthi kukhudumale ekuqaliseni kukaMfumfu kudlalela kubo-80 ezindaweni ezinengi ukusukela eMagcekeni aseNingizimu kusiya kuzingxenye zeNyakakatho-mpumalanga.
INew York City ingafika kumadigiri angu-80 ngoLwesibili, okungaba ngaphezu kwesilinganiso phose ngamadigiri angu-10.
Okucatshangelwa ukuthi umumo uzabe unjani okwesikhathi eside kubonisa ukuthi kungenzeka sibili ukuthi kube lokutshisa okwedlula isilinganiso ngasempumalanga kwe-U.S. engxenyeni yokuqala.
Abantu abedlula abangu-20 miliyoni babukela ukuthonisisiswa kukaBrett Kavanaugh
Abantu abedlula abangu-20 miliyoni babukela ubufakazi obuthinta kwamancane bangoLwesine kumanethiwekhi etelevizhini ayisithupha, obenziwa nguBrett Kavanaugh owakhethwa liDale Eliphakemeyo kanye lowesifazane uChristine Blasey Ford ommangalela ukuthi wambamba kubi kwezemacansini ngama-1980.
Ngesikhathi esifananayo, ukuncintisana kwezombusazwe kwaqhubeka, labasakazi bemisa inhlelo zasikhathi sonke bevulela ithuba ukuphonguguquka kwendaba kwangoLwesihlanu: isivumelwano esasungulwa nguSenetha wase-Arizona uJeff Flake sokuba i-FBI yenze ukuchwayisisa kweviki yonke ngalokho okumangalelwayo.
UFord watshela iKhomithi Yokwahlulela yeSenethi ukuthi uyaqiniseka ngokuyi-100 ekhulwini ukuthi uKavanaugh wambambabamba edakiwe njalo wazama ukumkhulula izigqoko zakhe besephathini yasesikolo.
UKavanaugh, efakaza ngokulamandla, wathi uyaqiniseka ngokuyi-100 ekhulwini ukuthi lokho akuzange kwenzakale.
Kukhanya kungenzeka ukuthi abantu abedlula abangamamiliyoni angu-20.4 ababikwa yiNielsen bakubukela.
Inkampani yayibala isilinganiso sababukeli kuCBS, ABC, NBC, CNN, itshaneli yeFox News kanye leMSNBC.
Amanani ayengakatholakali masinyane ngokuvela kwamanye amanethiwekhi abukisayo, okugoqela iPBS, C-SPAN kanye leFox Business Network.
Njalo iNielsen ijayele ukuba lohlupho ekubaleni abantu ababukela besemawofisini.
Ukuze lokhu kucace, lokhu linani lezibukeli elilingana lalelo elomdlalo omkhulu webhola kumbe ukuphiwa Izicoco ze-Academy.
Itshaneli yeFox News, elabethuli bezinhlelo abasekela kakhulu ukuthola isikhundla kukaKavanaugh, yiyo eyayikhokhele wonke amanethiwekhi ilesilinganiso sababukeli abangamamiliyoni angu-5.69 ngesikhathi kusenziwa ukuthonisisisa okwathatha ilanga lonke, kwatsho iNielsen.
I-ABC yayingeyesibili ilababukeli abangamamiliyoni angu-3.26.
ICBS yayilamamiliyoni angu-3.1, iNBC yayilamamiliyoni angu-2.94, iMSNBC yayilamamiliyoni angu-2.89 njalo iCNN yayilamamiliyoni angu-2.52, kwatsho iNielsen.
Kwaqhubeka kulokuthakazelela okukhulu langemuva kokuthonisiswa.
UFlake nguye owayezibambile ezanzakalweni zangoLwesihlanu.
Ngemva kokuba iwofisi yamaRepublican ephakathi laphakathi isikhiphe ilizwi lokuthi uzavotela uKavanaugh, waphuma kumakhamera eCNN lawe CBS ngoLwesihlanu ekuseni ethukwa ngabatshengiselayo ngesikhathi ezama ukugada ilifithi esiyathonisiswa yiKhomithi Yokwahlulela.
Wama ethe mbo amehlo phansi okwemizuzu ethile bemthethisa, okwakuphunyiswa kusenzakala kuCNN.
"Ngimile khonapha phambi kwakho," kwatsho omunye owesifazane.
"Licabanga ukuthi utshela ilizwe iqiniso?
Watshelwa ukuthi, "ulawo amandla lapho abafazi abanengi kangaka bengelamandla."
Ngaphambi kokuba umnyango welifithi uvalwe, uFlake wathi iwofisi yakhe yayisikhiphe ilizwi wasesithi, uzaba lokunengi kokutsho ekuthonisisweni yikhomithi.
Amanethiwekhi asakazayo lalawo athumela ngocingo wonke ayephumisa okwakusenzakala ngemva kwamahola, lapho iKhomithi Yokwahlulela yayizavota ukuthi idlulisele ukukhethwa kukaKavanaugh kuSenethi yonke ukuze ivote.
Kodwa uFlake wathi wayakwenza njalo ezwisisa ukuthi iFBI izahlolisisa ukumangalelwa kokhethiweyo ngeviki ezayo, lokho okwakukhuthazwa ngamaDemocrat amalutshwana.
UFlake wayeleqiniso lakho mhlawumbe ngenxa yezinkulumo ayebe lazo lomngane wakhe, oweDemocratic uSenetha Chris Coons.
Ngemva kwenkulumo loCoons kanye lamasenetha ambalwa ngemva kwalokho, uFlake wenza isinqumo sakhe.
Okwakhethwa nguFlake kwakulamandla, ngoba kwakusegcekeni ukuthi amaRepublican ayengasoze abe lamavoti angamukela uKavanaugh kungazange kuchwayisiswe udaba.
UMongameli uTrump usevumele ukuthi iFBI ichwayisise amacala amangalelwa uKavanaugh.
UPrime Minister waseBritain uMay, ubeka icala kulabo abamsolayo esithi 'bamqila kwezombusazwe' ngendaba yeBrexit
Kungxongxo eyaba khona lephephandaba leSunday Times, uPrime Minister uTheresa May wathi, labo abamsolayo balecala "lokumqila kwezombusazwe," bephambanisa elakusasa laseBritain njalo bengahloniphi intando yabantu, okuyikho okumenza atshiyane leEuropean Union.
UPrime Minister waseBritain, uTheresa May efika embuthwaneni weqembu leConservative, eBirmingham, eseBritain mhlaka 29 September 2018.
Eceleni kwengxongxo leyi, kuleyinye ingxongxo eyabakhona ngomunye owake waba nguForeign Minister othiwa nguBoris Johnson, laye waqhubeka emsola mayelana lohlelo lwakhe lweChequers eyeBrexit esithi, "kwakuyinto engelangqondo," ngoba wayethe iBritain leEU kumele zibuthelelane imali yazo zonke eyemithelo.
Ukudutshulwa kukaWayde Sims: Amapholisa abopha uDyteon Simpson ocatshangelwa ukuthi nguye obulele umdlali lo oweLSU
Amapholisa abophe umuntu ocatshangelwa ukuthi nguye obulele uWayde Sims oleminyaka engu20 yokuzalwa, umdlali webhora lezandla oweLSU.
UDyteon Simpson, oleminyaka engu20 yokuzalwa, ubotshwe wafakwa ejele ethonisiswa icala lokubulala, batsho njalo amaPholisa aweDipatimenti leBaton Rouge.
Abaphathi bamapholisa baphumise ividiyo itshengisa uSims loSimpson belwisana, njalo amapholisa bathe uSims uhle walahla amangilazi amehlo akhe besilwa.
Amapholisa bawatholile amangilazi amehlo lawa endaweni yona leyo, njalo bathola leDNA ikaSimpson kuwo, njengokutshiwo kwamaripoti aweCBS leWAFB.
Ngemva kokumbuza uSimpson, amapholisa bathe uvumile ukuthi udubulile wabulala uWayde.
Igqwetha lithe, imali yakhe yebheyili ibekwe ku$350 000.
IHOfisi eyeEast Baton Rouge Parish Coroner, uphumise iripoti ngoLwesihlanu, besithi ukufa kwakhe kwabangelwa ngokudutshulwa walinyazwa ikhanda kusiyafika entameni.
Idipatimenti leli lamapholisa lifuna ukubonga amapholisa asesiqinti saseLouisiana abakhangelela ukubaleka kwezigebenga, amapholisa asebenza lapho okuhlolisiswa khona amacala kusetshenziswa imitshina, amapholisa aweSouthern University lezakhamuzi zendawo leyi, ngokubancedisa ukuhlolisisa indaba leyi okwenze bacina bethola owenze icala leli.
mphathi wezemidlalo eLSU uJoe Alleva, ubonge kakhulu abezemithetho bendawo leyi, "ngokusebenza nzima njalo lokwahlulela kuhle."
USims ube leminyaka engu20 eyokuzalwa.
Ijaha leli elalilide okokufika amafidi angu6.6 (amamitha angu-2), wayedlalela phambili njalo wakhulela eBaton Rouge, lapho ubabakhe okuthiwa nguWayne, laye wake wadlalela iLSU ebhoreni leli lezandla.
Iavhareji yakhe yokuhlohla kumidlalo eyadlulayo kumudlalo munye ngamunye kwakungamapointi angu5.6 njalo waba lamapointi angu2.6 ekubiseleni ibhora eliyabe liqale lakhutha ukungena.
NgoLwesihlanu ekuseni, umqheqhetshi wabo waseLSU uWill Wade, wathi iqembu lakhe "lakhathazeka kakhulu" njalo "bahlupheka lokuvuma" ukuthi uWayde wayesefile.
"Lokhu yikho okusenza ukuthi sihlale sime ngamazwane nsuku zonke," watsho njalo uWade.
Intaba edubukayo ijike umlotha edolobheni leMexico
Umlotha ojikwe yintaba edubukayo yasePopocatepetl, isifike ezindaweni eziseningizimu kwedolobho elikhulu leMexico.
INational Center for Disaster Prevention, yaqhapela izakhamuzi zaseMexico ngoMgqibelo ukuthi bengafiki duzane lentaba leyi edubukayo njengoba yayitshengisa ukuthi isifuna ukudubuka, ngoba yayisiphumise umlotha lomoya oyingozi kwezikhathi ezingu183 phakathi kwamahora angu24.
Endaweni leyi, kade benanzelela ukuzamazama komhlaba kanye lomsindo kade usenzakala ezikhathini ezinengi.
Imifanekiso ephume kwezokuxhumana, itshengise umlotha emawindini ezimota emadolobheni eMexico njenge dolobho leXochimilco.
Amasayendisti abona ngezomhlaba, bananzelele ukuthi intaba leyi edubukayo ekhatshana lamamaila angu45 (amakhilomitha angu72) eningizimumpumalanga kwedolobho elikhulu, ingadubuka ngemva kokuzamazama kwomhlaba okwayenzakala ngoSeptember 2017, okwakulamandla afika 7.1 phakathi kwelizwe leMexico.
Intaba edubukayo eyaziwa ngokuthi "Don Goyo" kade ihlala idubuka kusukela ngo1994.
Ukulwisana phakathi kwamapholisa labasekeli beCatalan njengoba ilanga lokukhumbula inkululeko yokwenelisa ukuvota kwabo selizafika
Amapholisa abophe abantu abayisithupha eBarcelona ngoMgqibelo ngemva kwabasekeli benkululeko belwisane labo, besekelwa yizigidi zabantu ekutshengiseleni lokhu, njengoba iCatalonia ikhumbula umnyaka wabo wokuqala wokuzikhulula.
Iqembu labantu kade bevale ubuso elisekela ukwehlukana lokhu, liqalise ukukhanda amapholisa ngamaqanda lokubajikela ipenda eliphawuda, ngemva bevimbelwe ngamapholisa ukuthi bengatshengiseli, okwenze kwaba lothuli olumnyama emgwaqweni ojayele ukuba lezihambi.
Ngemva kwesikhathi esithile, kube lokunye ukulwisana okwenze ukuthi amapholisa basebenzise imboma ukuthi bamise ukulwisana lokhu.
Amaqembu asekela inkululeko baqhubeke bebizela ukuthi, "Singakhohlwa, Singathethelele," okwamahora athile njalo bencediswa lalabo abasekela ukuthi kube lokubambana, labo bebizela ukuthi, "Maiphile phakade iSpain."
Ekutshengiseleni lokhu, kulimele abantu abalitshumi lane kodwa bathole usizo ngoba bebengalimalanga kakhulu, itsho njalo iphephandaba yendawo leyi.
Ukungazwanani phakathi kwabantu abasekela ukuthi kube lenkululeko, kulokhu kuqinile lanxa sokudlule umnyaka kusukela amavoti amhlaka 1 October eseyenziwe, asekelwa ngalabo abasekela iCatalan, kodwa abaseMadrid besithi akukho emthethweni lokhu.
Abavothayo, bakhetha ngokuvamileyo ukuthi bafuna inkululeko kungela kuphikiswa kungelani lokuthi ababuyayo ukuzovotha babe balutshwana, ngoba ukwehlukana lokhu kwakungasekelwi ngabanengi.
Abaphathi beCatalan bathi, abantu abangabe befika 1 000 balinyazwa ekulwisaneni okwabakhona umnyaka odlulileyo, lapho amapholisa beze bezame ukuvimbela abantu ukuthi bengayi ukuyavota ezindaweni ezivotelwayo esabelweni lesi.
Besekela amapholisa, amaqembu asekela inkululeko babuthana ubusuku bonke ngoLwesihlanu ukwenzela ukuthi bavimbele ukutshengisela lokhu.
Ukutshengisela lokhu kwaqhubekela phambili, kodwa babanjwa ngamandla ukuthi bantshintshe indlela ababezayisebenzisa.
UNarcis Termes, oleminyaka engu68 yokuzalwa, olungisa amagetsi, kade ekhona ekutshengiseleni lokhu bebonke lomkakhe, uthe wayengaselathemba lokuthi iCatalonia izathola inkululeko.
"Umnyaka odlulileyo saba lempilo emnandi kakhulu.
Ngabona abazali bami bephuma inyembezi ngentokozo ngenxa yokuthi kade sebesenelisa ukuvota, kodwa okwamanje asisela themba," watsho njalo.
Lanxa benelisa ukuthi banqobe kumavoti esabelweni sabo ngenyanga kaDecember kumnyaka odlulileyo, amaqembu asekela inkukuleko eCatalan bayehluleka ukuqhubeka beqinile emnyakeni lo ngenxa yokuthi abakhokheli babo abanengi abalodumo bacatshile njalo abanye basejele bemelele ukuthonisiswa amacala abo ngenxa yokuhlela ukuthi kube lamavoti njalo lokubizela ukuthi sokule nkululeko.
Umakhanika okuthiwa nguJoan Puig oleminyaka engu42 yokuzalwa, warekhodha ukutshengisela lokhu efonini yakhe, esekela amapholisa esithi, ukungazwanani lokhu kuqaliswe ngabezombusazwe kumacele onke omabili.
"Kuqhubeka kusiba kubi," watsho njalo.
NgoMgqibelo, uOriol Junqueras omunye wabaphathi abayisitshiyagalolunye abasejele kusukela umnyaka ophelileyo bemelele ukuthonisiswa amacala abo wathi, ufuna ukuthi abantu bamuvotele kumavoti aweEuropean Parliament azayenzwa kumnyaka olandelayo.
“Ukuba ngomunye wabavotelwayo kumavoti aweEurope, yindlela enhle kakhulu ezanceda ukuthi siphumise egcekeni ukwehla kwamalungelo abantu njalo lokucindezelwa kwabantu ngehulumende yeSpain," watsho njalo.

Ibhola elatshaywa nguMenga lenza iLivingston inqobe iRangers nge-1-0
Ukuhlohla kokuqala kukaDolly Menga kwenza iLivingston ithole ukunqoba
ILivingston esanda kuthuthukiswa imangaze iRangers yehlisela uSteven Gerrard ekunqotshweni kwakhe kwesibili emidlaweni engu-18 engumkhokheli weqembu lase-Ibrox.
Ibhola elatshaywa nguDolly Menga yilo elenza kube lomehluko njengoba icele likaGary Holt lafika lalingana leHibernian endaweni yesibili.
Icele lika Gerrard lilokho lingakaze linqobe nxa lingadlaleli kwabo esikhathini lesi esePremiership njalo ngeSonto ezayo, lizadibana lelikhokhelayo eleHearts, elililandela ngemva kwalo ngemiklomelo eyisitshiyagalombili.
Ngaphambi kwalokho, iRangers izadlala leRapid Vienna kuLigi ye-Europa ngoLwesine.
Ngesikhathi esifananayo, iLivingston, isaqhubekisela phambili ukunganqotshwa kwayo esigabeni emidlalweni eyisithupha, umqeqetshi omkhulu uHolt esalokhe engakanqotshwa kusukela lapho athatha khona isikhundla sikaKenny Miler ngenyanga edlulileyo.
ILivingston ilahlekelwa ngamathuba ngesikhathi idlala labasemzini abangasizo ingcitshi
Iqembu likaHolt bekumele ngabe belivele liphambili lingakahlohli, lendlela abakade beqondisa ngayo ibhola labo ibangela ukuthi iRangers ithwale nzima.
UScott Robinson ubesengenile kodwa uphuzile ukulitshaya esekhangelane legedi, kwasekusithi u-Alan Lithgow wamane walitshayela egangeni ngemva kokuzama ukuhlangabeza ibhola ebelitshayelwe egedini ngekhanda nguCraig Halkett.
Abasekhaya bebesuthiseka ngokuvumela ukuthi iRangers idlalele phambi kwabo, besazi ukuthi bangathwalisa nzima abasemzini kwezinye izingxenye.
Yiyo indlela ukuhlohla okuqakathekileyo okwenzakale ngayo.
IRangers yenza ukuthi abanye bavunyelwe ukutshaya ibhola bengavinjwa njalo iLivingston yavula isikhala, uDeclan Gallagher loRobinson bahlanganyelana besipha uMenga ithuba, owalitshaya kanye wahlohla ephakathi laphakathi kwebhokisi.
Ngalelobanga, iRangers yiyo eyayihlala ilebhola kakhulu kodwa yathola ukuthi abasekhaya bavimbe kakhulu njalo obamba amabhola egedini uLiam Kelly wayevele engelahlupho,
Kwaqhubeka kunjalo kwaze kwaba sengxenyeni yesibili, lanxa uAlfredo Morelos wake wavimba ngamandla ibhola elalivela kuKelly.
UScott Pittman wavalelwa zinyawo zobamba amabhola egedini weRangers uAllan McGregor njalo uLithgow waphangisa ukulitshayela khatshana ekudlaleni kweLivingston.
Amabhola aqhubeka eqondiswa ebhokisini leLivingston njalo ayelokhu evinjwa, ngesikhathi esifananayo okwaba njengamaphenaluthi okubili - ngemva kokuba uHalkett ethe owayengene ethatha isikhundla uGlen Middleton udlale kubi, kanye lokuthi ibhola litshaywe ngesandla - akuzange kwamukelwe.

U-Alasdair Lamont weBBC yaseScotland eseNkundleni yeTony Macaroni

U-Erdogan wamukelwe ngendlela ezitshiyeneyo eCologne
Bekuthokozwa njalo umkhathi umuhle ngoMgqibelo (mhlaka 29 September) ngesikhathi umkhokheli weTurkey loweGermany besidla ekuseni eBerlin.
Lilanga lokucina uMongameli u-Erdogan evakatshele eGermany futhi kuhloswe ukuthi kulungiswe ukungazwanani okukhona lalabo abasekela i-NATO.
Kulokungazwanani ngendaba ezigoqela amalungelo oluntu, inkululeko yabezindaba lokungena kweTurkey ku-EU.
U-Erdogan usuke waqonda eCologne ukuze ayevula inkalakatha ye-mosque.
Idolobho leli lilezizalwane zeTurkey ezinengi ukwedlula wonke amanye aphandle kweTurkey.
Bebebanengi abasekela umongameli wabo futhi befuna ukumbona, amapholisa athe afuna ukuvikela abantu yikho evimbe ixuku labantu elingafika 25 000 ukuthi lingabuthani phambi kwe-mosque.
Izizalwane zeTurkey eziphikisana lo-Erdogan lazo bezizinengi futhi bezisola izinto ezenziwa ngu-Erdogan lohulumende weGermany ngokumamukela elizweni labo.
Ukuphikisana kwamaqembu lawa kutshengisa ukuthi kulokungazwanani ngoba ezinye izizalwane zeTurkey eziseGermany zithi uliqhawe njalo ziyamthanda kodwa ezinye ziyamzonda zisithi nguntandokayiphikiswa.

Ijele yeLong Lartin: Abakhangela izibotshwa abayisithupha balimele ngemva kokutshaywa yizibotshwa
Umbiko ovela ejele le enkulu futhi egcina izibotshwa ezingamadoda uthi abantu abayisithupha abakhangela izibotshwa balimele ngenxa yokuxabana okubekhona.
Ukuxabana lokhu kwenzakale ejele yeLong Lartin eWorcestershire njalo kuqalise ngabo 09:30 BST ngeSonto futhi lokhe kuqhubeka.
Sekuthunyelwe “Izingcitshi” ukuthi ziyeqeda ukuxabana lokhu okuphakathi kwezibotshwa eziyisitshiyagalombili leziphathindamandla zejele futhi umsindo lo usasehlangothini olulodwa.
Abagcina izibotshwa belatshwe amanxeba asebusweni khona lapho ejele.
Omunye umkhulumeli wejele uthe: "Izingcitshi ezafundiswa ukugcina izibotshwa sezithunyelwe ukuyaqeda ingxabano elokhu iqhubeka lakhathesi ejele yeLong Lartin.
Abagcina izibotshwa abayisithupha belatshiwe ngemva kokulinyazwa.
Asivumeli ukulwa kumbe ukuziphatha okunje emajele ethu, labo abenze lokhu bazabonana lamapholisa futhi bangacina sebehlala isikhathi eside ejele."
Ijele yeLong Lartin ilezibotshwa ezedlula 500 ezigoqela lalezo eziyingozi kakhulu elizweni leli.
Kubikwa ukuthi ngoJune, ugavena wejele wagijinyiselwa esibhedlela ngemva kokuhlaselwa yisibotshwa.
Njalo ngo-October nyakenye kwabizwa amapholisa erayothi ukuze azoqeda umsindo owawukhona ngoba izibotshwa zazihlasela ababagcinayo ngamabhora okudlala i-pool.
Isiphepho URosa Angahlasela EPhoenix, ELas Vegas Ikanti Angaba Yisikhukhula Edolobheni LeSalt Lake (Kungaba Yinto Enhle Endaweni Ezilesomiso)
Akujayelekanga ukuthi kwenzakale into enje eHarizona kodwa kukhanya angani kuzaba njalo ekuqaliseni kweviki ezayo njengoba isiphepho uRosa silokhu silamandla futhi siqonde eNkangala eseNingizimuntshonalanga futhi lokho kungabangela isikhukhula.
AbeNational Weather Service sebexwayise izakhamizi ngokuthi lokhu kungenzakala ngoMvulo langoLwesibili entshonalanga ye-Arizona laseningizimu lempumalanga yeNevada, laseningizimumpumalanga yeCalifornia lase-Utah, kugoqele lasePhoenix, eFlagstaff, eLas Vegas lasedolobheni leSalt Lake.
Kukhangelelwe ukuthi kuzaba lezulu ngoMvulo ntambama ikanti isiphepho uRosa sikhangelelwe ukuhlasela ePhoenix ngoLwesibili.
Umlayezo othunyelwe ngetwitter ngabeNational Weather Service uthe “kusukela ngo 1950 sekube leziphepho ezilitshumi ezilamandla leziletha izikhukhula kodwa bezikhatshana lePhoenix ngamamayila angaba ngu-200 (amakhilomitha angaba ngu-322)!
Isiphepho uKatrina (1967) sasikhatshana lomngcele we-Arizona ngamamayila angu-40 (amakhilomitha angu-64)."
Okukhitshwe yiNational Hurricane Centre kutshengisa ukuthi bacabangela ukuthi izulu elizaba khona lingaba phakathi kwamaintshi angu-2 kusiya ku-4 (amasentimitha angu-5 kusiya ku-10), ikanti lingaba ngamaintshi angu-6 (amasentimitha angu-15) kwezinye indawo ezigoqela iMogollon Rim e-Arizona.
Ezinye indawo ezisenkangala eseNingizimuntshonalanga ezihlanganisa iRockies leGreat Basin zingathola izulu elingamaintshi angu-1 kusiya ku-2 (amasentimitha angu-3 kusiya ku-5), ikanti kungenzeka ukuthi ezinye zithole elingamaintshi angu-4 (amasentimitha angu-10).
Ezinye indawo ezilapha zihlaselwe yisomiso yikho izulu leli lizaba luncedo kakhulu nxa zingasoze zihlaselwe yisiphepho uRosa kumbe yisikhukhula.
Liqiniso ukuthi izikhukhula zenza abantu bakhathazeke, kodwa kukhanya angani izulu leli linganceda abantu abanengi ngoba indawo eseNingizimuntshonalanga ihlaselwe yisomiso sikhuluma nje.
Umbiko okhitshwe yi-U.S. Drought Monitor uthi indawo edlula amaphesenti angu-40 e-Arizona ihlaselwe yisomiso esinzima, futhi isimo sibi kakhulu,” itshonjalo i-weather.com.
Kukhanya angani isiphepho uRosa sizaqalisa ngaphetsheya kweBaja eCalifornia emhlubulweni weMexico.
NgeSonto ekuseni isiphepho uRosa besilokhe silamandla ngoba besihamba ngesiqubu samamayila angu-85 (amakhilomitha angu-136) nge-awa, futhi khathesi siseningizimu yePunta Eugenia, eMexico njalo sikhatshana ngamamayila angaba ngu-385 (amakhilomitha angaba ngu 620), isiphepho lesi sesihamba ngesiqubu samamayila angu-12 (amakhilomitha angu-19) nge-awa.
Okwenze isiphepho lesi saphela amandla yikuthi khathesi sesihlangane lamanzi aqandayo elwandle lwePacific.
Yikho, kucatshangelwa ukuthi isiphepho lesi sizabe sesiyisikhukhula nxa sifika eMexico ngoMvulo emini kumbe ntambama.
Kungenzakala kube lezulu elizwayo endaweni ezitshiyeneyo eMexico futhi lokhu kungabangela izikhukhula.
Umbiko okhitshwe yi weather.com uthi “Sikhangelele izulu elingaba ngamaintshi angu-3 kusiya ku-6 (amasentimitha angu-8 kusiya ku-15) eBaja eCalifornia ikanti enyakathompumalanga yeSorona, lingafika kumaintshi angu-10 (amasentimitha angu-25).
Isiphepho uRosa sizadabula siqonda enyakatho yeMexico futhi sikhangelelwe ukufika emngceleni we-Arizona ngoLwesibili ekuseni sesiyisikhukhula, besesidabula e-Arizona siqonde eningizimu besesifika e-Utah ngoLwesibili ntambama.
"Kukhangelelwe ukuthi isiphepho uRosa sizabangela umonakalo omkhulu kakhulu, okugoqela izulu elizwayo eBaja eCalifornia, lasenyakathontshonalanga yeSonora lase-Nkangala eseNingizimuntshonalanga ye-U.S,” Lo yiwo umbiko okhitshwe yiNational Hurricane Centre.
Izulu leli lingafaka ukuphila kwabantu engozini ngoba lingabangela izikhukhula lokugeleza kodaka ezinkangala lokuqhekezeka komhlabathi endaweni ezigcwele izintaba.

"Ukuvotela uMtshutshisi Kavanaugh, kuphumisa egcekeni izindlela ezimbi ezisolisayo ezeqembu leDemocratic," watsho njalo uTrump embuthwaneni wabasekeli bakhe eWheeling yaseWest Virginia.
Ngemva esekhethiwe uKavanaugh, uTrump wathi uKavanaugh, ukhathazwe liqembu leDemocratic "ngenxa yokuqinisa amakhanda abo langokumuzonda kwabo."

ULee uthe izikhathi ezinengi labo abahlolisisayo e-U.S. kuyabe kumele baqale bacele izimali kuhulumende futhi kuthatha isikhathi eside ukuthi bayiphiwe.

AbaseMacedonia bavote kusivumelwano sokubona ukuthi bangantshintsha yini ibizo lelizwe labo
NgeSonto, abantu baseMacedonia bavote kusivumelwano sokubona ukuthi bangantshintsha yini ibizo lelizwe labo ukuthi lithi, "Republic of North Macedonia," untshintsho oluzalungisa ingxabano phakathi kweGreece labo, ngoba ingxabano leyi kade ivimbela ukungena kwabo ukuba lilunga leEuropean Union leNATO.
IGreece elesabelo seMacedonia, ithi ibizo lelizwe labomakhelwane babo baseningizimu, litshengisa ukuthi yibo abanikazi bendawo leyi njalo labo bavota ukuthi babelilunga leNATO leEU.
NgoJune, ohulumende laba bobabili bavumelene ngokuntshintsha ibizo leli kodwa abasekeli belungelo lamasiko abantu, bayala besithi untshintsho lolu luzaphambanisa ukwaziwa kwabantu baseMacedonia abesiSlavic.
UMongameli welizwe uGjorge Ivanov, uthe yena kasoze avote kusivumelwano lesi, njalo ukungasekelwi komnkankaso wesivumelwano lesi kwenze ukuthi abantu balahle ithemba lokuthi sizaphumelela njengoba kufunakala i50 phesenti eyabantu kusiya phambili ukuthi siqalise ukusebenza.
Umbuzo kusivumelwano lesi uthi: "Ulilunga leNATO leEU yini ngokuvumelana okukhona ngeGreece."
Abasekeli bokuntshintshwa kwebizo lelizwe okuhlanganisela uPrime Minister uZoran Zaev, uthe kuyinto elengqondo ukuthi iMacedonia ibe lilunga leEU leNATO, njengoba iMacedonia ililizwe elaphuma ekuweni kweYugoslavia.
"Ngibuye ukuzovotha namhla ngisenzela elakusasa lelizwe lalabo abasakhulayo baseMacedonia, ngoba kuzayenza ukuthi baphile impilo bekhululekile bephansi kweEuropean Union, ngoba kutsho ukuthi sizabe silempilo ezinhle sonke," watsho njalo uOlivera Georgijevska oleminyaka engu79 yokuzalwa eSkopje.
Lanxa kungekho emthethweni, amalunga awepaliyamenti bathe bazasekela okuzaphuma kumavoti lawa ukuthi kufakwe emthethweni.
Ukuthi benelise ukuntshintsha ibizo leli, kufuna inali elidlula ihafu yamalunga awepaliyamenti.
Labo abakhangelela ngezokuvota, bathe bekungakabi lamaripoti aphambanisiweyo ngesikhathi sika1 emini.
Kodwa abantu ababuyileyo ukuzovota bekuyi 16 phesenti kuphela nxa kuqathaniswa yi34 phesenti eyamavoti awepaliyamenti ka2016 lapho abantu abafika 66 phesenti babuya ukuzovota.
"Ngibuye ukuzovota ngenxa yabantwana bami, thina indawo yethu iseEurope," watsho njalo uGjose Tanevski oleminyaka engu62 yokuzalwa, ovotele edolobheni leSkopje.
UPrime Minister waseMacedonia uZoran Zaev, umkakhe uZorica lendodana yakhe uDushko, bavote besekela isivumelwano lesi sokuthi bantshintshe ibizo lelizwe, okuzayenza ukuthi bahlanganyele kanye leNATO leEuropean Union eStromica, eseMacedonia ngoSeptember 30, 2018.
Phambili kwepaliyamenti yeSkopje, uVladimir Kavardarkov oleminyaka engu54 yokuzalwa, kade elungisa isiteji esincane njalo ekhipha lezitulo eziphambili kwamatente kade efakwe lalabo abafuna ukuvimbela abantu ababuya ukuzovotela isivumelwano lesi.
"Singamalunga eNATO leEU, kodwa sifuna ukubambana sikwenze lokhu ngendlela ehlakaniphileyo," watsho njalo uKavardarkov.
"Sililizwe elidubekayo, kodwa siyahlonipheka.
Nxa bengafuni ukusiyamukela njengabeMacedonia, siyakwanisa ukuthi siye kwabanye abanjengeChina kumbe iRussia, sibe sesisiba ingxenye yeEuro-Asia."
UPrime Minister uZaev, uthe iNATO izaletha imisebenzi eminengi eMacedonia njengoba kulabantu abedlula 20 phesenti abangelayo imisebenzi.
"Ngiyakholwa ukuthi inengi labantu lizasekela amavoti lawa, ngoba i80 phesenti yezakhamuzi yavumelana lokubambana leEU langeNATO," watsho njalo uZaev esanda kuvota.
Uthe nxa "banganqoba," kutsho ukuthi, "elakusasa labo liyabe lilihle."
Inali etshengisa abazavotayo eliphumiswe ngoMvulo ngeInstitute for Policy Research eMacedonia, itshengise ukuthi abantu abaphakathi kwe30 kusiya ku43 phesenti yibo abazavota kusivumelwano lesi - inali ephansi kwaleyo ekhangelelweyo.
Kodwa kwenye inali etshengisa abazavota eyenzwe yiTelma TV eyeMacedonia, itshengise ukuthi i57 phesenti yabantu, bafuna ukuyavota ngeSonto.
Kubantu laba, i70 pecenti ithi bazavotela isivumelwano lesi.
Ukuthi isivumelwano lesi siqalise ukusebenza, kufunakala ukuthi kubuye abantu abedlula 50 phesenti ukuzovota.
Isivumelwano lesi singayekela ukuphumelela, kuzaphambanisa kakhulu uhlelo lwalabo abasekela ohulumende eziseMpumalanga, njengoba zaqalisa ukukhokhela ngoMay umnyaka odlulileyo.

AbeLabour abafuni lakuzwa abantu bekhuluma abakucabangayo
Angizange ngimangale ngesikhathi abasekeli beMomentum eqenjini lami bevotela ukuthi ngikhuzwe.
Phela ayisimi ngedwa kubameli bePhalamende abakuhlangothi lweLabour oqalisa ukutshelwa ukuthi abasifuni, saliswa khona ukukhuluma imibono yethu.
Omunye wami uJoan Ryan laye waphathwa ngendlela efananayo ngoba wayengavumelani lokubandlululwa kwabantu ngale indlela.
Ekukhuzweni kwami bangisole ngokuthi angivumelani loJeremy Corbyn.
Endabeni zokuqakatheka kokuthi kube lemithetho kwezomnotho, kwezokuvikeleka kwelizwe, lange-Europe, okuyizo futhi indaba uJeremy angavumelani lazo labanye abake baba ngabakhokheli.
Isaziso esakhitshwa yiNottingham East Labour emhlanganweni owaba khona ngoLwesihlanu sathi “sifuna ukuthi imihlangano esiba layo ihlanganise bonke abantu futhi ibe luncedo."
Okweminyaka eyisitshiyagalombili ngingumeli wePhalamende okhangele ezeLabour, ngingathi imihlangano eminengi esibe layo okugoqela lalowu esibe lawo ngoLwesihlanu ibinjalo sibili.
Kuyadanisa ukuthi khathesi akunjalo futhi lesithembiso sokuthi abantu “babelomusa, baphathane kuhle” kwezokubusa asigcwaliswa ngitsho, kungani abantu sebakhohlwa langaso.
Lokhe kusiya kucaca ukuthi iqembu leLabour kalifuni kube lomuntu olombono otshiyene lowalo lokuthi ungakhuluma okucabangayo kuyabe kumele kukhangelwe ukuthi bayakwamukela yini.
Lokhu kwaqalisa ngemva kokuthi uJeremy ebe ngumkhokheli, labanye engangisebenza labo engangicabanga ukuthi balombono ofanana lowami endabeni le basebekhangelele ukuthi ngitshintshe engikucabangayo endabeni zokuvikeleka kwelizwe kumbe ezentengiselwano ze-EU.
Ngingavele ngikhulume loba yini kuzulu, kulandela ukuchothozwa okubuhlungu kusetshenziswa ezokuxhumana, ngisolwa ngezinto ezinengi, abanye besithi kumele ngikhitshwe esikhundleni futhi akumelanga ngibe seqenjini leLabour.
Lokhu akwenzakali kimi kuphela.
Kodwa okwami kungcono ngoba ngezinye izikhathi ngichothozwa ngendaba zezombusazwe.
Ngiyabahlonipha kakhulu abanye bami ngendlela abaziphatha ngayo labaqinisela ngayo nxa bechothozwa nsuku zonke mhlawumbe ngobulili babo kumbe bebandlululwa kodwa abakhalali.
Into ezwisa ubuhlungu ngezombusazwe zakulezi insuku yikuthi abantu kabasahlonitshwa ngitsho lakancane futhi sekukhanya angani leyo yinto eqondileyo.
Ngeviki ephelileyo uJeremy Corbyn uthe iqembu leLabour kumele lamukele imibono etshiyeneyo.
Iqiniso yikuthi abantu abasakhululekanga njengakudala, umuntu “sekhitshwa lula esikhundleni ngokuvota kuphela” ikanti ukutshintsha kwemithetho yokukhetha abantu sekwenze ukuthi iqembu liqhubeke lincipha.
Kulabantu abanengi abakade belokhu bengixwayisa eminyakeni emibili edlulileyo besithi ngibofunda ukuthula nxa ngifuna izinto “zingihambele kuhle."
Kodwa lokho ayisikho engakungenela kwezombusazwe.
Sengileminyaka engu 32 ngajoyina iqembu leLabour futhi lokhu ngakwenza ngisafunda, kwakungizwisa ubuhlungu ukubona uhulumende kaThatcher esekela ukulungisa ikilasi yethu yesikolo eyayidilika, ngisebenze nzima ngizama ukuthi abantu bancediswe baphile ngcono ngesikhathi ngingukhansila langesikhathi sengingumphathintambo kahulumende.
Angikaze ngifihle lutho emsebenzini wami wezombusazwe, lokhetho lokucina engangikulo abantu bayalwazi.
Akulamuntu eNottingham East ongathi kazwisisi ukuthi ngikhethani endleleni izinto okumele zihambe ngayo lokuthi kungaphi lapho engingavumelani khona lalabo abakhokhelayo khathesi.
Kulabo abakhetha utshintsho lolu ngoLwesihlanu ngithanda ukulitshela ukuthi ukuphuma kweBritain ku-European Union kuzakwenza abantu bathwale nzima, lamabhizimusi azadonsa nzima, lenhlelo ezenzelwa uzulu zizaswela imali, angilasizathu sokusebenzisa isikhathi lamandla ami ngisekela umkhokheli weqembu leLabour.
Nanku engithanda ukukutsho hatshi kwabeNottingham Momentum, kodwa kulabo abalamandla okukhetha abakhokheli, kungaba ngabaseqenjini leLabour kumbe hatshi: Ngiyaziqhenya ngokulisebenzela, ngilithembisa ukuthi akulalutho oluzangivimba ukuthi ngenze izinto engikwaziyo ukuthi zizanceda abantu bonke, lanxa ngezinye izikhathi ngisethuselwa ngokuthi ngizaxotshwa umsebenzi kumbe kuthiwe angenzi kuhle kwezombusazwe.

Phakathi kwamaqembu wonke alitshumi, khathesi yibo bodwa abangakanqotshwa.
Ekucineni, kwakuyivimba kuhle kakhulu ababekwenza, ndawonye lokusebenzisa kwabo kuhle amathuba, okwaphakamisa iqembu lasekhaya njalo umqeqetshi uPeter Murchie wayelalo lonke ilungelo lokuthaba.
"Emidlalweni yethu kuze kube khathesi besihlolwa, njalo sisalokhu singakanqotshwa, ngakho kumele ngithokoze," watsho njalo.
URobyn Christie oweMelrose wathi: "I-Ayr kumele ibukwe, basebenzise kangcono amathuba abo ukwedlula thina."

UClimo wathuthukisa ukukhokhela kwe-Ayr ngephenaluthi, ngaphambi nje, kokuphela kwehlandla lokuqala, wahlohla wasekhomvetha kanye okwenza ukuthi imiklomelo ye-Ayr ibe yi-17-5 ngesikhathi sekhefu.
Kodwa iMelrose yaliqalisa kuhle ihlandla lesibili njalo itrayi eyenziwa nguPatrick Anderson, yakhomvethwa nguBaggot, yehlisa umehluko waba yimiklomelo emihlanu.

Ukaputeni obambele isikhundla we-Ayr uBlair Macpherson wasuka wasephiwa iyelo khadi, njalo iMelrose yasebenzisa ubunengi babo ngetrayi engakhomvethwanga eyenziwa nguBruce Colvine, ekucineni kwesikhathi lapho ababencindezelwe khona ngokwesabekayo.
Abasekhaya baphindisela, kodwa, kuthe uStruan Hutchinson ephiwa iyelo khadi ngenxa yokugwenxa uClimo engelabhola, esemzileni wephenaluthi, uMacpherson wathinta phansi elandelwa ngabe Ayr ababefuna ukumhlasela.

‘Ulwandle ngolwethu’: litsho njalo ilizwe leBolivia eligonjolozelwe ngamanye amazwe, lilethemba lokuthi umthethwandaba uzabavulela ulwandle lwePacific
Abahamba ngezikepe balokhu bebhoda endaweni le elamawofisi amakhulu ebutho elilwa lisemanzini eLa Paz.
Izakhiwo zomphakathi zilengisa amafulegi aluhlaza okolwandle.
Indawo zebutho elilwa lisemanzini kusukela eLake Titicaca kusiya e-Amazon zaziwa ngokusebenzisa umutsho othi: “Silelungelo lokuthi ulwandle lube ngolwethu.
Silomlandu wokuthi siluthathe.”
Elizweni lonke leBolivia eligonjolozelwe ngamanye amazwe, abantu balokhu besizwa ubuhlungu ngengxenye yolwandle eyacina ithethwe yiChile futhi kwafa abantu abanengi ngeminyaka yabo 1800 ngenxa yalokhu, abanengi bakulindele ngabomvu ukuphinda babeselwandle lwePacific njengakudala.
Bacabanga ukuthi ithemba lelo selizagcwaliseka khathesi njengoba iBolivia imelele isinqumo esizakhitshwa ngumthethwandaba mhlaka 1 October ngemva kweminyaka emihlanu udaba lolu lwahanjiswa emthethwandaba.
Isizalwane seBolivia esilesikhundla kuhumende uRobert Calzadilla uthe, “iBolivia ilamandla, abantu bethu babambene njalo kulokuthula futhi silindele izindaba ezinhle.”
Izizalwane zeBolivia ezinengi zizabukela kuma T.V ngesikhathi i-International Court of Justice ikhipha isinqumo endabeni le, zilethemba lokuthi abahluli abaseHague bazasekela ilizwe leBolivia elithi sekuleminyaka lizama ukukhulumisana leChile kodwa kusehlula, iBolivia ikhangelele ukuthi layo iphiwe ingxenyana yolwandle.
Umongameli weBolivia othandwa ngabanengi u-Evo Morales futhi okhankasela ukuthi aphinde akhethwe ngomnyaka ozayo ulindele ngabomvu okuzakhulunywa ngoMvulo ngoba kutsho okunengi ngomsebenzi wakhe.
Ekupheleni kuka-August wathi, “Sokusele kancane ukuthi siphinde sibuyele elwandle lwePacific.”
Kodwa ezinye izingcitshi ezihlolisisayo ziyathandabuza ukuthi umthethwandaba uzasekela isicelo seBolivia, njalo zithi akulalutho olukhulu kangako oluzatshintsha nxa ungayisekela.
Umthethwandaba lo oseNetherlands ungaphansi kwe-UN njalo awulamandla okuthathela iChile ingxenye yawo futhi uthe awukwazi ukuthi ukukhulumisana okukhona kuzaphetha ngani.
Ingcitshi yezemithetho eyisizalwane seChile uPaz Zarate uthe udaba lolu “belungekho nzima” ngoba isinqumo se ICJ sizakhitshwa kungakedluli lezinyanga eziyisithupha kusukela kwacina ukukhulunywa ngendaba le.
Iminyaka emine edlulileyo ayizange incede iBolivia ngitsho lakancane kodwa yenza isinqumo lesi saphuza ukukhitshwa.
UZarate uphinde wathi, “Iziphathamandla zeBolivia yizo ezivimbe ukuthi abantu benelise ukusebenzisa ulwandle.”
Uphinde wathi amazwi ahlabayo akhulunywe nguMorales angenza ukuthi iChile icine itshintsha ebikuhlosile endabeni le.
IBolivia izaqhubeka ikhulumisana leChile ngendaba le ngokuhamba kwesikhathi kodwa kuzaba nzima ngemva kwalokhu okwenzakeleyo.
Amazwe la womabili ama ukuba lomuntu omele ilizwe lawo kwelinye kusukela ngo 1962.
Owake waba ngumongameli weBolivia u-Eduardo Rodriguez obemele iHague uthe akusiloqiniso ukuthi umthethwandaba ubambe indaba le ngesiphangiphangi.
Uthe okuzakwenzakala ngoMvulo kuzanika iBolivia “ithuba elitsha lokuthi isebenze kuhle leChile” njalo “iqede lokungazwanani osekuthethe iminyaka engu-139 futhi amazwe womabili azancedakala ngalokhu.”
UCalzadilla uthe kungamanga ukuthi uMorales umongameli weLatin America othandwa ngabanengi usebenzisa indaba yolwandle ukuthi akhankasele ezombusazwe.
Ungezelele ngokuthi, “IBolivia kayisoze ilahle ilungelo elalo lokusebenzisa ulwandle lwePacific.”

ULuke Armitage olungisa izitayela zabantu abadumileyo, utshele iFEMAIL ukuthi: 'Ngikhangelele ukubona izingowani lezi ezinkulu lezikhwama zakhona kumgwaqo omkhulu edolobheni, ihlobo elilandelayo - njengoba sokukhanya ukuthi abantu bazabe befuna izigqoko lezi ezikhulu, yikho kumele sibe leqiniso lokuthi zikhona.'
UJohn Edward: Kuqakathekile ukuthi abantu bonke babekwazi indimi ezitshiyeneyo
Izikolo ezizimele zodwa eScotland zilabantu abanengi abahlala bepasa minyaka yonke futhi kube kuhle kakhulu lango-2018, ngempumela yemihloliso emihle okwamagama, lokhu kwenziwa yikuthi abantu ngabanye, lamaqembu enza kuhle kwezemidlalo, kwezokudweba, ekuhlabeleni lakokunye okunceda umphakathi.
Izikolo lezi ezigcwele kulo lonke eleScotland zilabafundi abangafika 30 000 futhi zimelwa yinhlanganiso okuthiwa yiScottish Council of Independent Schools (SCIS), njalo zizimisele ukwenza ezikwenelisayo ekuncediseni abafundi labazali.
Izikolo ezizimele zodwa zihlose ukunceda abafundi ukuthi balungiselele ukuthola imfundo yaphezulu, imisebenzi abayikhethayo lalokho abafuna ukukwenza ukuze bancede lelizwe lonke.
Njengohlangothi lwezemfundo olwenelisa ukuhlela okumele kufundwe lokuthi kuzafundiswa njani ezikolo, sibona kulokhu kusiba labafundi abanengi abakhetha izindimi ezikhulunywa kulezinsuku.
UNelson Mandela wathi: “Nxa ungakhuluma lomuntu ngolimi aluzwisisayo, okutshoyo kuzangena ekhanda lakhe.
Kodwa ungakhuluma laye ngolimi alumunyayo lokho kuzangena enhliziyweni yakhe."
Lokhu kusikhumbuza ukuthi akumelanga sithembe ulimi lwesiNgisi kuphela nxa sifuna ukuba labangane abazasithemba abavela kwamanye amazwe.
Impumela yemihloliso esiyithole lonyaka, itshengisa ukuthi abafundi abanengi benza kuhle kakhulu ekufundeleni izindimi njalo abanengi abapase kuhle kakhulu ngabasezikolo ezizimele zodwa.
Phakathi kwalabo abafundela izindimi, abafika amaphesenti angu-68 bapasa ngabo-A.
Umbiko esiwuthole kuhlanganiso ye SCIS elezikolo ezingu-74 utshengisa ukuthi amaphesenti angu-72 abafundi baphume lo-A kuMandarin kwazothi amaphesenti angu-72 alabo abafunda isiGerman, amaphesenti angu-69 alabo abafunda isiFrench kanye lamaphesenti angu-63 alabo abafunda isiSpanish labo baphume lo-A.
Lokhu kutshengisa ukuthi izikolo ezizimele zodwa eScotland ziyasekela sibili ukuthi abantu bafunde indimi zakwamanye amazwe ngoba abantwana labasakhulayo kumele babezazi indimi lezi ukuze zibancede kusasa.
Ukufundela indimi khathesi sokuqakathekiswa ngendlela efanana leyezifundo zeSTEM (science, technology, engineering lemathematics) ezikolo ezizimele zodwa lakwezinye indawo.
Ukuhlola okwenziwe yi-UK Commission for Employment and Skills ngo 2014, kuveze ukuthi amaphesenati angu-17 emisebenzi engelabantu ibangelwa yikuthi abaqhatshi baswela abantu abakhuluma izindimi abayabe bezikhangelele.
Lokhu kwenza kucace ukuqakatheka kokuthi abafundi bazazi izindimi ezitshiyeneyo ngoba zizabanceda nxa sebedinga umsebenzi.
Amathuba emisebenzi avulekayo atshengisa ukuthi umuntu usengasebenzela kuloba yiliphi ilizwe, yikho kuqakathekile ukuthi abantu bafunde indimi zakwamanye amazwe.
Kungelani lokuthi umuntu ukhetha ukwenza msebenzi bani, ukufundela olunye ulimi kuzamnceda endabeni ezinengi.
Uzakwenelisa ukukhuluma labantu abavela kwamanye amazwe futhi lokhu kumvulela amathuba umuntu okhuluma ulimi olulodwa angalawo.
Ukuhlola okwenziwa yi YouGov kwezizwalane esezikhulile ze-UK ezedlula 4 000 ngo-2013, kwatshengisa ukuthi amaphesenti angu-75 ehluleka ukukhuluma labantu abavela kwamanye amazwe, ikanti amaphesenti angu-15 kuphela yiwo ayesenelisa ukukhuluma isiFrench.
Lokhu kwenza kuqakatheke kakhulu ukuthi abantwana bafundiswe izindimi zakwamanye amazwe.
Ukwazi indimi ezinengi, ikakhulu ezikhulunywa emazweni asathuthuka, kuzanceda abantwana ukuthi bathole imisebenzi ezabanceda kusasa.
Akusoze kufundiswe indimi ezifananayo esikolo ngasinye lapha eScotland.
Ezinye izikolo zizafundisa indimi ezikhulunywa ngabanengi, ikanti ezinye zifundise lezo ezikhanya ziqakathekile e-UK ikakhulu nxa sesikhangele umnyaka ka-2020 sesicabanga ngesiMandarin lesiJapanese.
Kungelani lokuthi umntanakho uthandani, kulezindimi ezinengi angakhetha kuzo ezikolo ezizimele zodwa futhi uzafundiswa ngababalisi abazingcitshi.
Izikolo ezizimele zodwa eScotland zilakho konke okunceda abantwana babelolwazi abaludingayo ukuze baphumelele njalo benelise ukwenza loba yini nxa sebeqedile isikolo.
Akulamuntu ongaphika ukuthi ezokuthengiselana sezisenziwa emhlabeni wonke lokuthi ukufundela izindimi zakwamanye amazwe kuqakathekile, yikho lokho kumele kukhanye kwezemfundo.
Akulambuzo ukuthi izindimi ezikhulunywa ngabantu “abanengi ziqakathekile ekukhulumisaneni.”
Izikolo ezizimele zodwa eScotland zizaqhubeka zinika abafundi ithuba lokufunda, lelokukhetha abafuna ukukwenza, lelokubancedisa baphumelele.
Il faut bien le faire.

ULeBron uzadlalela iLakers okokuqala ngeSonto eSan Diego
Ukulinda sekuzaphela kubasekeli abakhangelele ukubona uLeBron James edlalela iLakers yaseLos Angeles okokuqala.
Umqeqetshi weLakers uLuke Walton ubike ukuthi uJames uzadlala emdlalweni wangaphambi kokuqalisa kwemidlalo yonke wokuqala bedlala leDenver Nuggets eSan Diego.
Kodwa ukuthi uzadlala okwemizuzu emingaki akukatshiwo.
"Kuzaba ngowedlula owodwa njalo kube ngaphansi kwengu-48," kwatsho uWaltson kuwebhusayithi engokomthetho yeLakers.
Obika izindaba weLakers uMike Trudell wathwitha ukuthi kukhanya uJames uzadla okwemizuzu elinganiselweyo.
Ngemva kokuphrakithiza ekuqaliseni kwaleli viki, uJames wabuzwa ukuthi uhleleni ngemidlalo eyisithupha ehlelwe yiLakers ukuba idlalwe ngaphambi kokuqalisa kwesikhathi semidlalo yonke.
"Ebangeni lokudlala kwami engikulo kangiyidingi imidlalo yangaphambi kokuqalisa kwesikhathi semidlalo ukuze ngilunge," watsho njalo.
Isikhathi samarali kaTrump aseWest Virginia, kuTshaneli yeYouTube
UMongameli uDonald Trump uqalisa amarali amanengi okukhankasa lamuhla ntambama eWheeling, eWest Virginia.
Ngeyokuqala kumarali amahlanu kaTrump ahleliweyo ngeviki ezayo, okugoqela ukudlula esima ezindaweni alobungane lazo okugoqela iTennessee leMississippi.
Njengoba ukuvunyelwa kwalowo amkhethileyo ukuthi avotelwe ukungena esikhundleni kuDale Eliphakemeyo kuke kwamiswa, uTrump uhlose ukuthola usekelo ekuvoteni kwaphakathi laphakathi kwesikhathi okuzayo njengoba amaRepublican esengozini yokulahlekelwa ngamandla okutshaya imithetho kuCongress nxa sekuvotwa ngoLwezi.
Irali kaTrump eWest Virginia ikhona sikhathi bani njalo uhlela ukuyibukela njani kwezempucuko?
Irali kaTrump yaseWheeling, eWest Virginia ihlelwe ukuqalisa ngo-7 p.m. ET kusihlwa, ngoMgqibelo, Mpandula 29, 2018.
Ungabukela irali kaTrump yaseWest Virginia kwezempucuko ubukela ngesikhathi kusenzakala khonapho kuYouTube.
Kungenzeka ukuthi uTrump akhulume ngodaba lwalowo okhethwe ukuba avotelwe ukuba kuDale Eliphakemeyo uBrett Kavanaugh, oselusuke lwabanzima ngenxa yokwethweswa kwakhe icala lokungaziphathi kwezemacansini futhi ukuvunyelwa kwakhe ukuvotelwa okumelwe kwenziwe yiSenethi kuke kwamiswa okweviki ngesikhathi iFBI isachwayisisa.
Kodwa inhloso enkulu yamarali lawa yikuncedisa amaRepublican ukuba athuthuke njengoba ekhangelane lokuvota okulukhuni ngoLwezi.
Ngakho, ukukhankasa kukaMongameli uTrump kuthe amarali lawa amahlanu ngeviki ezayo ahlose "ukupha amandla kumavolontiya labasekeli njengoba amaRepublican ezama ukuvikela lokwandisa ukuba banengi kwawo kuSenethi lakuDale Labameli," njengokutsho kweReuters.
"Ukuqondisa iCongress kuqakatheke kakhulu kulokho okumele kwenziwe okokuthi umongameli uzahamba ezabelweni ezinengi angazenelisa njengoba singena esikhathini sokukhankasa esibambekileyo," kwatsho umkhulumeli wokukhankasa kukaTrump owala ukuqanjwa ngebizo etshela iReuters.
Ihlelelwe ukwenzelwa eNkundleni yeWesbanco eWheeling, irali yakusihlwa lamuhla ingaletha abasekeli abavela "e-Ohio lePennsylvania njalo isakazwe ngabezindaba abasePittsburgh," njengokutsho kweWest Virginia Metro News.
NgoMgqibelo kuzakuba ngokwesibili ezinyangeni ezimbili lapho uTrump avakatshele khona iWest Virginia, isabelo lapho anqoba khona ngokwedlula i-40 ekhulwini ngemiklomelo ngo-2016.
UTrump uzama ukuncedisa ovotelwa esikhundlenin seSenethi oweRepublican uPatrick Morrisey, osalele ngemuva ekuvotelweni.
"Akuphi umbono omuhle ngoMorrisey ukuthi sekuze kumele ukuthi umongameli abuye azozama ukumthuthukisa ekuvotelweni," kwatsho uSimon Haeder, owezesayensi yezombusazwe e-Univesithi yaseWest Virginia, njengokutsho kweReuters.
Inkezo YeRyder Ka2018: TIqembu le-USA alikalahli ithemba lokuthi kungalihambela kuhle ngeSonto njengoba ngamunye wabo ezaba lethuba lokudlala
Ngemva kokuthi umdlali ngamunye edlale eyedwa kathathu, umdlalo wangoMgqibelo emini ozabe ulabadlali abane ungaba yiwo kanye obufuneka kuNkezo yeRyder.
Umdlalo lo wokutshaya ibhola ngensimbi awuzwisiseki kwabanengi ukuthi waqalisa njani kodwa abawudlalayo bawuthanda okwamagama, futhi umncintiswano onjengalowu ubanika amadlabuzane.
Manje bawathatha ngaphi amandla okuqhubeka bedlala?
Ngesikhathi uJordan Spieth eseqedile umdlalo wakhe uthe, “Bebephambi kwethu ngemiklomelo eyisithupha kodwa khathesi sebephambili ngemine, yikho ngicabanga ukuthi akumelanga silahle ithemba.”
Kuyihambela kuhle i-Europe ngoba ivele ilemiklomelo elitshumi lambili besekusithi khathesi iphinde ibephambili ngemiklomelo emine.
USpieth uthe abadlali be-America balezizathu ezinengi zokungakhalali futhi abasoze bakhangele emuva ngoba uSpieth loJustin Thomas benze kuhle baze badlale ndawonye okwelanga lonke njalo ngamunye wabo ulemiklomelo emithathu kwemine obekumele bayithole.
USpieth utshengise abeqembu lakhe okumele bakwenze ngoba ubetshaya ibhola okuzwayo kusukela eqalisa ukulitshaya kuze kube seduze legodi.
Ixuku ebelibukele belisehluleka ukuzibamba ngenxa yentokozo ngemva kokuthi engenise ibhola egodini okwenze umdlalo wabo wesine waba ngutshiki lobhanqa ngoba yena loThomas besebesele emuva ngemiklomelo emibili.
Ukutshaya kwakhe ibhola elenze imiklomelo yabo yafika ku-15 njalo banqoba kwenze ixuku lathokoza kakhulu, lokhu kumenza akholwe ukuthi iqembu le-America lingayithatha inkezo.
USpieth uthe, “Umuntu kumele asebenze nzima acabange ngomdlalo ophambi kwakhe.”
Yikho okumele kwenziwe ngumdlali ngamunye khathesi.
Amagodi angu-18 azatsho ukuthi ingcitshi ngobani.
Abadlali abalemiklomelo edlula ekaSpieth loThomas emalangeni amabili asanda kudlula nguFrancesco Molinari lo Tommy Fleetwood futhi lokhu kujayelekile nxa kudlalelwa iNkezo yeRyder.
Abadlali be-Europe abane abakanqotshwa futhi bayawazi okuzwayo umdlalo lo.
Iqembu lika “Moliwood” yilo lodwa elingazange lidlalise amathuba okutshayela ibhola egodini ngoMgqibelo emini, njengoba lalenzile langoMgqibelo ekuseni njalo lenza okufanayo ngoLwesihlanu ekuseni lasemini.
Indlela iqembu leli elidlala ngayo lendlela elithandwa ngayo ngababukelayo itshengisa ukuthi yibo abadlali okumele besatshwe kakhulu ngeSonto, kungenzakala ukuthi iqembu leli le-Europe linqobe emdlalweni ozaba khona e-Le Golf National hatshi uFleetwood kumbe uMolinari.
Bekungaba kuhle bengadlala ngesikhathi esifananayo betshayela amabhola emagodini atshiyeneyo.
Kusasemasinyane kodwa ukutsho ukuthi i-Europe izanqoba.

Kodwa ngeSonto yindoda zibonele, akula ozabe encedisana lomunye.

Abadlali be-Europe badlale kuhle beliqembu futhi baphambi kwabanye abadlali kodwa esesikubonile kubadlali abane kutshengisa ukuthi iqembu le-USA alikalahli ithemba lokunqoba lanxa abanye ,ikakhulu abeStateside, bengakukholwa lokhu.
I-Europe isikhangele iNkezo yeRyder futhi iphambili nge10-6
Izinto ziyihambela kuhle i-Europe ngemva komdlalo wamabhola amane labadlali abane obekhona ngoMgqibelo futhi baphambi kwe-United States nge10-6, lokho kungatsho ukuthi bangayithatha iNkezo yeRyder.
UTommy Fleetwood loFrancesco Molinari bahle bakhokhela ngokunqoba kabili betshiya uTiger Woods emuva emdlalweni obekhona eLe Golf National futhi lokho kubanike imiklomelo emine.
UThomas Bjorn we-Europe ubelwisa nzima ngemva kokwehluleka ukuthatha inkezo emdlalweni owabakhona eminyakeni emibili edlulileyo eHazeltine, ubedlala okuzwayo lamuhla ekuseni wanqoba abe-America nge 3-1.
Abe-US balwiswile beliqembu, banqoba emidlalweni emibili kodwa lokhu akubancedi kangako.
Iqembu lika Jim Furyk lizafuna imiklomelo eyisitshiyagalombili emidlalweni engu 12 ngeSonto ukuze bangathathelwa inkezo.
Kubadlali be-Europe abangelasikhathi eside, uFleetwood ngowokuqala ukuthi athole imiklomelo emine kulandelana ikanti yena loMolinari sebebizwa ngokuthi “Molliwood” futhi babe liqembu lesibili ukuthola imiklomelo emine emidlalweni yabo emine selokhu kwaqalisa ukuba leNkezo yeRyder ngemva kokudlala kuhle kakhulu ngempelaviki.
Baqalise ngokunqoba uWoods loPatrick Reed ngesikhathi somdlalo wamabhola amane, basuka lapho baphinda bamnqoba futhi uWoods lomdlali omutsha we-America uBryson Dechambeau nge 5 lange 4.
UWoods udonse nzima sibili emidlalweni emibili abelayo ngoMgqibelo lanxa ebesenza kuhle kweminye kodwa udliwe emidlalweni engu 19 phakathi kwengu 29 yamabhola amane lalapho beliqembu futhi udliwe kweyisikhombisa ilandelana.
UJustin Rose kazange adlale eyamabhola amane ekuseni kodwa ujoyine uHenrik Stenson lapho abanqobe khona nge 2 lange 1, futhi abanqotshiweyo nguDustin Johnson loBrooks Koepka -omunye ngowokuqala ikanti omunye ngowesithathu kuntshantshu zomdlalo lo emhlabeni wonke.
Lokhu akutsho ukuthi bekulula kubadlali be-Europe, lanxa umkhathi ubumuhle kuphephetha umoya eningizimuntshonalanga yeParis.
Osenqobe kathathu emidlalweni enjengalowu uJordan Spieth loJustin Thomas abe-America badlale kuhle kakhulu bathola imiklomelo emibili ngoMgqibelo.
Balwise nzima banqoba nge-2-1 ngesikhathi bencintisana labadlali beSpain uJohn Rahm lo-Ian Poulter emdlalweni wamabhola amane bazophenduka futhi banqoba uPoulter loRory Mcllroy nge 4 lange 3 bedlala betshintshana ngemva kokwehluleka ukungenisa emagodini okuqala amabili.
Ngokwesibili kumbali yeNkezo yeRyder ukuthi iqembu ebelisele emuva ngemiklomelo engu 4 licine lifika kuhlandla lokusala lomdlali oyedwa, iqembu likaFuryk yilo elilenkezo khathesi njalo izaqhubeka ingeyabo nxa kungaba ngutshiki lobhanqa.
