INyakatho Korea ithi 'akulandlela' engenza bona bebodwa batshiye izikhali kungela kuthembana
Isiphathamandla esibona ngezokwenzakala ngaphandle kwelizwe saseNyakatho Korea satshela Izizwe Ezibambeneyo ngoMgqibelo ukuthi ukuqhubeka ngezijeziso kwakujulisa ukungathembi kwabo i-United States njalo akulandlela engenza ukuthi ilizwe labo lilodwa liyekele izikhali zalo zenyukliya ngaphansi kwezimo ezinjalo.
URi Yong Ho watshela iqula lomhlaba eMhlanganweni oMkhulu waminyaka yonke ukuthi iNyakatho Korea yayisiyenze "amanyathelo acacayo okutshengisa ubuntu" emnyakeni odlulileyo, anjengokuyekela ukuhlolwa kwenyukliya lokwezikhali, ukudiliza indawo yokuhlola inyukliya, lokuthembisa ukuthi kayisoze yengezelele izikhali zenyukliya lezempucuko zenyukliya.
"Kodwa kasiboni impendulo ehambelanayo evela e-U.S.," watsho njalo.
"Kungela kuthemba i-U.S. kuzabe kungela siqiniseko ngokuvikeleka kwethu njengesizwe njalo ngaphansi kwezimo ezinjalo akulandlela thina sisodwa esingaba ngabokuqala ukutshiya izikhali."
Lanxa uRi waphinda watsho lokho okuhlala kusolwa yiNyakatho Korea ngokwala kweWashington ekuyekelisweni ukusebenzisa inyukliya okwenziwa "ngezigaba" lezo ngaphansi kwazo iNyakatho Korea ezathola khona umvuzo njengoba ithatha amanyathelo kancane kancane, akutshoyo kwakhanya kulesisindo ngenxa yokuthi kazange ale ukuyekeliswa kwabo bebodwa ukusebenzisa inyukliya njengokungeke kwenzeke njengalokho okwakwenziwe ePyongyang esikhathini esidlulileyo.
URi wabhekisela emazwini ake akhulunywa nguKim Jong Un loDonald Trump emhlanganweni wabo wokuqala ngqa phakathi komongameli osesihlalweni wase-U.S. lomkhokheli waseNyakatho Korea eSingapore ngoNhlangula 12 lapho uKim athembisa khona ukuthi uzasebenzela "ukuyekelisiswa ukusebenzisa inyukliya kusihlengana saseKorea" ngesikhathi esifananayo uTrump ethembisa ukuqiniseka kokuvikeleka kweNyakatho Korea.
INyakatho Korea ibilokhu ifuna ukuphelisa Impi yaseKorea ka-1950-53 ngokusemthethweni kodwa i-United States ithe iPyongyang kumele iqale itshiyane lezikhali zayo zenyukliya kuqala.
IWashington ihlala isala ukwamukela izicelo zokuthi izijeziso zamazwe ezinzima kuNyakatho Korea ziyekethiswe.
I-U.S. iphikelela ukuthi "kuqale kuyekeliswe ukusebenzisa inyukliya" njalo yengezelela ukuncindezela ngezijeziso ukuze ifeze inhloso yayo ngendlela yokubamba ngamandla, ngitsho lokwala ukuthi "kumenyezelwe ukuphela kwempi,"" kwatsho uRi.
"Umcabango wokuthi izijeziso zizasihlalisa phansi liphupho nje labantu abangasaziyo thina.
Kodwa uhlupho yikuthi izijeziso eziqhubekayo zilokhu zijulisa ukungathembani kwethu."
URi kazange atsho lutho ngenhlelo zomhlangano wesibili phakathi kukaKim loTrump ezazike zaqokonyiswa ngumkhokheli we-U.S. eZizweni Ezibambeneyo ekuqaliseni kweviki.
Kulokutsho lokho isiphathamandla saqokomisa imihlangano emithathu phakathi kukaKim lomkhokheli weNingizimu Korea uMoon Jae ezinyangeni ezinhlanu ezidlulileyo njalo saphinda sathi: "Aluba umhlangano wokuyekeliswa ukusebenzisa inyukliya ubuyenziwe leNingizimu Korea hatshi i-U.S., ukuyekeliswa ukusebenzisa inyukliya kwesihlengana seKorea bekungasoze kucine sekungutshiki lobhanqa."
Lanxa kunjalo, indlela uRi ethula ngayo inkulumo yakhe yayihlukile kakhulu kulanyakenye lapho atshela khona i-U.N. EMhlanganweni Omkhulu ukuthi ukuqopha ilizwe le-U.S. ngamarokhethi eNyakatho Korea vele kwakuzakwenzeka ngemva kokuba "uMnumzane Mongameli Omubi" Trump ebize uKim ngelokuthi "indoda yerokhethi" edinga ukuzibulalisa.
Lonyaka eZizweni Ezibambeneyo, uTrump, lowo nyakenye owayesongele ukutshabalalisa iNyakatho Korea, wamncoma engaqedi uKim ngesibindi sakhe sokuthatha amanyathelo okutshiya izikhali, kodwa watsho ukuthi kuseselomsebenzi omnengi okumele wenziwe njalo izijeziso kumele ziqhubeke zikhona iNyakatho Korea ize iyekele ukusebenzisa inyukliya.
NgoLwesithathu, uTrump wathi kwakungela sikhathi esibekiweyo sokwenza lokhu, esithi "nxa kungathatha iminyaka emibili, iminyaka emithathu kumbe izinyanga ezinhlanu - akulandaba."
IChina leRussia ziphikisa zisithi iDale Lokuvikela le-U.N. kumele liphe iPyongyang umvuzo ngamanyathelo asethethwe.
Kodwa, i-U.S. eloNobhala Wesizwe uMike Pompeo watshela iDale Lokuvikela le-U.N. ngoLwesine ukuthi: "Ukwenza ukuthi izijeziso zokuvikela zeDale Lokuvikela zisebenze kumele kuqhubeke ngamandla njalo kungehlulwa kuze kufike emaphethelweni, ngokugcweleyo, sekuleqiniso lokuthi sekuyekeliswe ukusebenzisa inyukliya."
IDale Lokuvikela livumelane ngazwi linye ukuthuthukisa izijeziso kuNyakatho Korea ukusukela ngo-2006 ekuzameni ukuvimba izimali zokubhadala inhlelo zenyukliya lezobuhlanya zePyongyang.
UPompeo wahlangana loRio ngaphandle koMhlangano Omkhulu we-U.N. njalo ngemva kwalokho wathi uzaphinda avakatshele iPyongyang ngenyanga ezayo ukuze alungiselele umhlangano wesibili.
Sekuze kukathathu uPompeo evakatshela iNyakatho Korea lonyaka, kodwa uhambo lwakhe lokucina aluhambanga kuhle.
Wasuka ePyongyang ngoNcwabakazi esithi sekube sekulentuthuko, kodwa kungakapheli amahola amangaki iNyakatho Korea yamchothoza ngokuthi "uzenza ingqwele etshaya imithetho."
Emhlanganweni loMoon kuyonale inyanga iNyakatho Korea yathembisa ukudiliza indawo yezikhali kanye lezakhiwo zenyukliya nxa i-United States ingathatha "amanyathelo ahambelanayo."
Wathi uKim wayemtshele ukuthi "amanyathelo ahambelanayo" ayewadinga kwakuyikuqinisekiswa ngokuvikeleka lokho okwakuthenjiswe nguTrump eSingapore kanye lamanyathelo okwenza kube lobudlelwano obuhle leWashington.
Izifundi zaseHarvard sezingena ikhosi ezabanceda ukuthi babe bephumula
Ikhosi entsha yeYunivesithi yaseHarvard yalowo mnyaka, isincede zonke izifundi zabo ukuthi zenelise ukuba lesikhathi esinengi sokulala kuyindlela yokulwisana lomkhuba kade usukhona owokusebenzisa icaffeine ukuthi bengalali 'ubusuku bonke.'
Ofundisa abantwana laba eYunivesithi leyi, uthi izifundi ezisesikolo lesi edumileyo umhlaba wonke, kazazi lutho nxa sesikhuluma ngendaba yokuzinakekela.
UCharles Czeisler, uProfesa okhangelela ngezomuthi oncedayo ukulala eHarvard Medical School, njalo eyingcitshi yokwelapha eBrigham Women's Hospital, nguye owalungisayo ikhosi leyi, njalo uthi yiyo yodwa eUS.
Wakhuthazwa ukuthi aqalise ikhosi leyi ngemva esenikeze enye inkulumo eyayitshengisa ukuthi ukungalali kulengozi.
'Sengiqedile ukukhuluma, omunye unkazana wabuya kimi wathi: 'Kanti ngenxa yani sengitshelwa lokhu khathesi, mina sengisemnyakeni wami wokucina?'
Wathi akula muntu owake wamtshela ngokuqakatheka kokulala - okwangimangalisayo kakhulu,' watshela iThe Telegraph.
Ikhosi leyi eqalise lowo mnyaka, icasisa kuzifundi ukuthi ukulala kuqakathekile, njalo kuyanceda abafundi kwezemidlalo futhi kwenza uzizwe ungumuntu sibili.
UPaul Barreira, uProfesa ohlola ngokwengqondo eHarvard Medical School, njalo engumphathi wezempilakahle eYunivesithi leyi, wathi iYunivesithi yakhetha ukuthi kube lekhosi le ngemva kokubona ukuthi kulabafundi kade bengalali phakathi kweviki.
Ikhosi leyi ethatha ihora elilodwa, ihlanganisela izifundo ezenza baxoxisane bencedisana.
Kwesinye isifundo kule isifanekiso sendlu yokulala, njalo kumele abafundi laba baklikhe okulamankomitsho awekhofi, amakhetheni, abaqeqetshi lamabhuku ukuze babone ukuthi icaffein iyalimaza njani, lokungacitshi ilayithi njalo ngokuthi kuphambanisa njani kwezemidlalo nxa umuntu engalali, langokuqakatheka kokulala lokuvuka ngesikhathi.
Kwesinye isifundo, abafundi batshelwa ukuthi nxa ungathatha isikhathi ungalali okwaneleyo kubangela imikhuhlane yenhliziyo, istroke, ukudana kakhulu lemvukuzane.
Kulemephu eyesikolo elemifanekiso encedisa abafundi ukuthi bazwisise njalo bahlolisise ukuthi bahlala besenzani langa linye ngalinye.
'Siyakwazi ukuthi ukuziphatha kwabafundi akusoze kwantshintsha ngelanga elilodwa.
Kodwa balelungelo lokuthi babekwazi okwenzakalayo - njengoba umuntu elelungelo lokubakwazi ukuthi ukubhema igwayi kuyalimaza umzimba,' wangezelela uProfesa Czeisler.
Umkhuba lo owokungalali ebusuku lokhu usasekhona, njalo ezempuncuko langokwanda kwemisebenzi yabantwana besikolo kwenza ukuthi ukungalali kuqhubeke kuluhlupho.
Ukuba leqiniso lokuthi uyalala okwaneleyo njalo lokulala kuhle, kumele kube 'ngumuthi' wabafundi bonke onceda ukuthi bangakhathazeki kakhulu njalo bangahlali bediniwe, watsho njalo - ukulala kuyanceda ukuthi umuntu angabi yisidudla, ngoba ukungalali kwenza ukuthi ingqondo ithumeze umlayezo wokuthi umuntu ahlale esidla.
URaymond So, oleminyaka engu19 eyokuzalwa oweCarlifonia ofunda ngokwamakhemikhali langokuphila kwezintu eziphilayo, wanceda uProfesa Czeisler ukuthi alungise ikhosi leyi, ngemva esengene enye yezifundo zakhe umnyaka odlulileyo eHarvard.
Wathi ikhosi leyi yamvula amehlo njalo yamkhuthaza ukuthi benze ikhosi enkulu esikholweni lesi.
Uthi okulandelayo yikucela abafundi bonke ukuthi benze ikhosi leyi bengakangeni emisebenzini eyokuziphilisa.
UProfesa Czeisler, wakhuthaza abafundi ukuthi kumele bafake ialamu yokuthi bayelala langokuvuka, njalo ngokunanzelela ukulimaza okwenzwa ngokukhanya kwefoni langokukhanya kweLED, okwenza ukuthi babe lohlupho lokulala.
ILivingston 1-iRangers 0: Ukuhlohla kukaMenga kutshiye iqembu likaGerrard lidliwe
IRangers ibingadlaleli egumeni layo njalo iphinde yadliwa futhi ngemva kokuthi uDolly Menga ethele ibhola emambuleni, abadlali beqembu likaSteven Gerrard basele bekhamise imilomo ngoba benqotshwe nge 1-0 ngesikhathi bedlalela eLivingston.
Iqembu eliqeqetshwa ngu-Ibrox belifuna sibili ukunqoba ngoba lacina ukwenza njalo ngoFebruary lize linqobe nge 4-1 eSt Johnstone, kodwa iqembu likaGary Holt lanqoba elikaGerrard futhi lokhu kwakungokwesibili ukuthi linqotshwe emidlalweni engu-18 ngesikhathi engumphathi futhi lokhu kwenza ukuthi kube lomehluko wemiklomelo eyisitshiyagalombili leqembu le-Hearts elalikhokhela kuLadbrokes Premiership.
UMenga uhlohle sokusele imizuzu eyisikhombisa ukuthi ihlandla lokuqala liphele ikanti iqembu leRangers belivele lingaqinanga futhi lingalwisi kangako.
Khathesi iRangers isingeyesithupha, ikanti iLivingston isingeyesithathu njalo ilandela iHibernian ngomehluko wokuhlohlwa ibhola elilodwa kuphela.
Kungenzeka ukuthi iRangers khona isazothwala nzima futhi ngoba kukhanya angani abasekeli bayo baphose into etshaye oncedisa umgcinimpembe uCalum Spence ekhanda kwaze kwadingeka ukuthi afakwe umuthi.
UGerrard ufake abadlali abayisitshiyagalombili ababengekho kuqembu elanqoba i-Ayr ngesikhathi kudlalelwa iNkezo yeBetfred kumasemi-final.
UHolt umqeqetshi weqembu leLivi 11 katshintshanga abadlali bakhe abanqobe iHearts ngeviki ephelileyo, futhi imthokozisile indlela abadlale ngayo ngoba kube lula sibili ukuthi banqobe.
Izikhathi ezinengi ibhola belisenyaweni zeRangers kodwa iLivingston ibisithi ingalithatha ibatshengise okumele kwenziwe ngalo.
Bekumele bahlohle nje kungakedluli imizuzu emibili zisukelene ngemva kokuthi uMenga ekhabele uScott Pittman ibhola sokumele akhabele egedini elivinjwa ngu-Allan McGregor kodwa umdlali lo odlalela phakathi laphakathi kwenkundla usuke wakhabela eceleni.
UKeaghan Jacobs uphiwe ithuba lokuthi akhabe ibhola engamakwanga ngumuntu, elifikele enyaweni zikaCraig Halkett kodwa umdlali ovimbayo u-Alan Lithgow ulithinte kancane laselisiya ngemva kwegedi.
IRangers icine ilithethe ibhola kodwa bekudlala inhliziyo ngapha enyaweni kusala khona umdlalo sekuseduze ukuthi uphele.
U-Alfredo Morelos ubesithi kumele baphiwe umbekwa ngemva kokudlala okwemizuzu elitshumi lanhlanu ngenxa yokuthi ethuzane loSteven Lawless kodwa unompembe uSteven Thomson uthe umdlalo kawuqhubeke, kazange azihluphe ngobekufunwa yisizalwane seColombia.
IRangers ike yakhabela egedini kabili kuphela ngehlandla lakuqala lomdlalo kodwa uLiam Kelly owake wabambela i-Ibrox kazange ethuke ngitsho ngesikhathi uLassana Coulibaly engqikilela ibhola egedini lalapho u-Ovie Ejaria ekhabela ibhola elingatsho lutho egedini lakhe.
Lanxa iqembu leLivi belingadlali ngendlela emangalisayo, lihlohlile ngemva kwemizuzu engu-34 futhi lokhu bekufanele kwenzakale ngenxa yokusebenza kwalo nzima.
Lakhathesi iRangers iyehlulekile ukuvimba ibhola elikhatshwe nguJacobs.
UScott Arfield kenzanga lutho lapho uDeclan Gallagher ekhabela ibhola kuScott Robinson, oligcine kuhle enyaweni zakhe waselikhabela uMenga oqedise ngokulithela emambuleni engazange athwale nzima.
Ngesikhathi sokuphumula ngemva kwehlandla lokuqala, uGerrard ukhiphe uCoulibaly wafaka uRyan Kent futhi utshintsho lolu lukhanyile ngoba umdlali lo odlalela emhlubulweni udlule uMorelos kodwa uvinjwe nguKelly ukuze ibhola lingangeni.
Kodwa iLivingston iqhubeke ilithwalisa nzima iqembu leli elivakatshileyo, kukhanya bebekukholisa sibili ukubona uLithgow loHalkett bekhaba amabhola atshisayo ahamba umango omude.
Iqembu likaHolt belingenelisa ukuphinda lihlohle futhi umdlalo ususiyaphela, kodwa uMcGregor ulivimbile ebelilivela kuJacobs njalo kulelinye ebelisuka ekhoneni uLithgow alitshayele phandle ngekhanda.
UGlenn Middleton umdlali weRangers othethe indawo yomunye laye ukhalakhalaze ngokuphiwa umbekwa umdlalo usuzaphela ngemva kokugwenxana loJacobs kodwa uThomson uphinde wazikhangelela eceleni engafuni lakuzwa.
IAlmanac: Ingcitshi eyalungisa iGeiger Counter
Okukupeji lethu le"Sunday Morning" Almanac: NgoSeptember 30, 1882, iminyaka engu 136 eyadlulayo, njalo SIQHUBEKA SIYIBALA..., ilanga lapho okwazalwa khona uJohannes Wilhelm "Hans" Geiger eGermany, owayezakuba yingcitshi yezesayensi.
UGeiger walungisa indlela eyayizayenza ukuthi kube lula ukubona langokuzwa, abakubiza ngesikhiwa besithi yiradioactivity, okwacina kusenza ukuthi kube lomtshina othiwa yiGeiger Counter.
Yaqaliswa ukusekelwa ngabezesayensi njalo yaqhubeka isisekelwa ngabasakhulayo njengoba kwaphuma kwenye ifilimu ika1950 eyayithiwa yi"Bells of Colorado," eyayilabantu ababenjengani ngabelusi benkomo kodwa bengamasayendisti uRoy Rogers loDale Evans:
Indoda: "Kuyini lokhu?"
URogers: "YiGeiger Counter esetshenziswa ukudinga izinto okwembiwa emhlabathini, ezinjenge uranium.
Nxa ungafaka amaearphones lawa, uyakwanisa ukuzwa ama-atoms aphumayo kulokhu okwembiwa emhlabathini."
UEvans: "Hawu, sokusebenzeka khathesi!"
U"Hans" Geiger wafa ngomnyaka ka1945, sokusele amalanga amalutshwana nje ukuthi akhumbule usuku lokuzalwa kwakhe, esefika imnyaka engu63.
Kodwa umtshina lo olebizo lakhe, lokhu usasekhona.
Ivakisini entsha yemvukuzane ingafundisa amandla omzimba okuzivikela emikhuhlaneni 'ukubona' amacell axhwalileyo
Ivakisini entsha yemvukuzane ingafundisa amandla omzimba okuzivikela emikhuhlaneni 'ukubona' amacell axhwalileyo ibisiwabulala
Njengengxenye yokwelapha ivakisini ifundisa amandla omzimba okuzivikela emikhuhlaneni ukwenelisa ukunanzelala amacell axhwalileyo
Indlela yakhona igoqela ukuthatha amacell amandla omzimba okuzivikela emikhuhlaneni esigulane, abesetshintshwa elebhu
Ayenelisa 'ukubona' ipurotheyini ejayele ukutholakala kumvukuzane ezinengi abesephinda ebuyiselwa futhi emzimbeni
Ivakisini yokuhlola ibonisa impumela ethembisayo ezigulaneni ezilemvukuzane ezitshiyatshiyeneyo.
Omunye owesifazane owelatshwa ngevakisini, efundisa amandla omzimba okuzivikela emikhuhlaneni ukuba yenelise ukunanzelela amacell axhwalileyo, kwatholakala imvukuzane yakhe yasesibelethweni inyamalala okwezinyanga ezedlula ezingu-18.
Indlela yakhona igoqela ukuthatha amacell amandla omzimba okuzivikela emikhuhlaneni, ukuwatshintsha elabhorethori ukuze enelise "ukubona" ipurotheyini ejayele ukutholakala kumvukuzane ezinengi ebizwa ngokuthi yiHER2, amacell akhona abesephinda ebuyiselwa futhi emzimbeni.
UProfesa Jay Berzofsky, owe-US National Cancer Institute eBethesda, eMaryland, wathi: "Impumela yethu itshengisela ukuthi silevakisini ethembisayo kakhulu."
I-HER2 "iqhuba ukukhula kwemihlobo ethile yemvukuzane," okugoqela imvukuzane yasemabeleni, eyesibelethweni, eyamaphaphu kanye leyasemathunjini, uProfesa Berzofsky wachasisa.
Ukwenza okufananayo kokuthatha amacell amandla omzimba okuzivikela emikhuhlaneni kuzigulane "lokuwafundisa" ukuqopha amacell emvukuzane kusebenzile ekwelapheni omunye umhlobo welukhemiya.

Umlingiswa we-Game of Thrones uKit Harington usola indlela amadoda akhangelwa ngayo
UKit Harington udume ngokusebenzisa inkemba yakhe lokuyidlalidlalisa engumlingiswa uJon Snow emdlalweni weHBO wezokulwa lokubulalana okwakusenzakala ngezikhathi zakudala othiwa yiGame of Thrones.
Kodwa umlingiswa lo oleminyaka engu-31, uthi kavumelani lokuthi abantu abangamadoda abaphuma kumaTV kumele bakhanye bengamaqhawe ukuze kuthiwe ngamadoda kuzwa ngoba lokho sokusenza labafana abasakhulayo babone angani kumele babe njalo ukuze bahlonitshwe.
Ekhuluma labeSunday Times Culture, uKit uthe ‘kukhona okungahambi kuhle’ wasebuza ukuthi kanti lungaqedwa njani uhlupho lwendlela amadoda akhangelwa ngayo ngesikhathi lesi okugcwele khona abantu abaphonguthatheka ngokulandela okwenziwa ngabanye #MeToo.
UKit osanda kutshada lomlingiswa asebenza laye ku-Game of Thrones uRose Leslie laye oleminyaka engu-31, uthe indaba leyi ‘kayimphathi ngitsho’ futhi kumele kukhulunywe ngayo.
Uthe, ‘Ayingiphathi indaba leyi, ngitsho lakancane, kanti silahleka ngaphi endabeni amadoda akhangelwa ngayo?’
‘Besibafundisani abafana besakhula, kambe ukuthi yikho okubangela uhlupho esesilalo khathesi?’
UKit kathandabuzi ukuthi izinto abantu abazibona kuma-TV lazo ziyayitshintsha indlela abantu ababona ngayo amadoda futhi lokhu kungabe kubangelwa ngamadoda akhanya engamaqhawe okucatshangwa ukuthi yiwo amadoda kuzwa.
Uqhubeke ngokuthi: 'Kuyini okusengqondweni zethu futhi kuyini esikufundiswayo?
Kuyini okufundiswa kuma-TV, lasemigwaqweni okwenza abafana abasakhulayo bacabange ukuthi kumele benze ezinye izinto ukuze kuthiwe bangamadoda kuzwa?
Ngicabanga ukuthi lo ngumbuzo okumele sizibuze wona sibili - kumele kwenziweni ngohlupho lolu olukhona?
Kuyazicacela ukuthi abafana abasakhulayo kumele bancediswe.'

Kusukela ngoNovember, uKit uzaba ngumlingiswa emdlalweni obusumile ukwenziwa okaSam Shepard othi True West, umdlalo lo umayelana lendoda ebona ngezokwenza amafilimu elomfowabo olisela.

Uthe, ‘Ngabona umkami ngesikhathi sisenza umdlalo lo, lokhu kutsho ukuthi sengingaba lemuli futhi impilo yami iqhubeke isiya phambili.’
URose nguYgritte emdlalweni lo futhi uyabe ethandwa ngumlingiswa uJon Snow okunguye uKit emdlalweni lo osuthethe umvuzo we-Emmy.

I-HIV/Aids: IChina ithi inani labantu asebebanjwe umkhuhlane lo seliqanse ngamaphesenti angu-14
IChina ikhiphe umbiko wokuthi inani lezizalwane zelizwe lalo ezilegcikwane le-HIV le-Aids seliqanse ngamaphesenti angu-14.
Abezempilakahle elizweni leli bathi abantu abedlula 820 000 balegcikwane leli.
Abantu abangafika 40 000 ngabasanda kubanjwa ligcikwane leli futhi lokhu kwenzakale phakathi kwenyanga yesine kusiya kweyesithupha ngo-2018.
Abanengi bathole igcikwane leli ngenxa yokuya emacansini ikanti lokho bekungasajayelekanga kangako.
Obesekwande kakhulu ezindaweni ezinengi zeChina obekusenza ukuthi abantu bacine belegcikwane le-HIV, yikufakwa igazi lomuntu oyabe elegcikwane ngesikhathi umuntu eselatshwa.
Kodwa umbiko obekhona ngesikhathi abezempilakahle bexoxa lentathelizindaba esigabeni seYunnan uveze ukuthi besebebalutshwana kakhulu abantu abathola igcikwane leHIV ngokufakwa igazi.
Kodwa inani labantu ababanjwa igcikwane le-HIV le-Aids eChina belilokhu liqansa nge 100 000 umnyaka ngamunye.
Izitabane lalabo abalala lomuntu waloba yibuphi ubulili abaseChina, abafuni kukhulunywe ngendaba yokuthi umuntu angabanjwa ligcikwane le-HIV ngokuya emacansini.
Ngo-1997 iChina yathi akusocala ukuthi umuntu abe yisitabane, kodwa abantu abanengi bayazizonda izitabane lalabo abalala lomuntu waloba yibuphi ubulili.
Ngenxa yokuthi inengi labantu abaselizweni leli kalikhulumi kangako ngokwenzakala empilweni zabo, ukuhlolisisa okwenziweyo kutshengisa ukuthi amaphesenti angu-70 kusiya ku 90 amadoda, alala lamanye amadoda futhi azacina ethatha abafazi.
Okwenza umkhuhlane lo uthelelwane kangaka yikuthi abantu abazivikeli ngokwaneleyo nxa besiya emacansini.
Kusukela ngo 2003 uhulumende weChina wathembisa ukuthi wayezakwenza ukuthi kutholakale imithi yeHIV emhlabeni wonke ukuze abantu balwisane lomkhuhlane lo.

Ukuhlolwa kwefilimu likaJohnny English - ukungakhanyiswi kwethalenta likaRowan Atkinson edlala njengenhloli
Sokuyinjwayelo ukuthi kudingwe izinto ezifananayo leBrexit kumafilimu aphunyiswayo eBritain, kodwa kufilimu leli elintsha lika Johnny English kukhanya akula okufananayo - yaqala ngo2003 loJohnny English njalo ngo2011 kwabesokusiba leJohnny English Reborn.
Ifilimu leli elihlekisayo njalo bezikhulumela santando, yiwo amafilimu esesiwaphumisa yini elizweni lethu esiya kwamanye amazwe?
Lanxa esenza angani kahlelekanga emsebenzini wakhe uJohnny English, unikezwe isthupha esintsha sokuthi ayenze umsebenzi wokuba yinhloli - ibizo leli abizwa ngalo litshengisa ukuthi ngumuntu othanda ukuhlekisa abantu abangakhulumiyo iSikhiwa kodwa abathanda ukubukela amafilimu.
Usebenza njengenhloli ekahulumende, lanxa wayezama ukuzenza umuntu obukeka kuhle, wayekhanya angani nguClouseau kufilimu leli, kwelinye icele ekhanya njengoMr Bean njalo kwelinye icele ekhanya njengomuntu owahlabela kuChariots of Fire, ingoma eyahlatshelwa bevula imidlalo eyamazwe eLondon eka2012.

Kulokukodwa kumbe okubili okucazayo kufilimu likaJE.
Ngacazwa nguJohnny English esiyagada isikhopokhopo egqoke izigqoko zamabutho bakudala njalo okubhodhayo okuphezulu kwesikhopokhopo ukuthi iphakame kwabe sokutshaya ingowani ayeyigqokile okwesikhatshana nje.
UAtkinson ulesipho sokuhlekisa abantu, kodwa kufilimu leyi wayesenza angani kalaso nxa sesiqathanisa lamafilimu anjenge007 leMission Impossible, lawo inhloso yabo ngeyokuhlekisa abantu.
Indlela ayehlekisa ngayo abantu, kukhanya yayiqonde kubantwana kulokuthi iqonde kubadala, njalo ngikhuluma nje uJohnny English kasela zinto ezintsha ezicazayo nxa siqathanisa lamafilimu akhe uAtkinson elinjenge likaBean.

Lokhu kuzatsho ukuthi izisebenzi zizaba lamalanga amathathu okuziphumulela iviki ngayinye - kodwa zithole umholo wazo oweneleyo.

ITrades Union Congress yiyo ethutshe lecebo lokuthi abantu basebenze okwamalanga amane ngeviki besithi izimo zomnotho zilokhu zitshintsha.
Oselesikhathi eside esebenza leqembu leLabour utshele abeSunday Times ukuthi: ‘Sikhangelele ukuthi abantu batshelwe ngotshintsho lolu umnyaka lo ungakapheli.

Iqembu leLabour ayisilo lakuqala elikhuluma ngokuthi abantu kumele basebenze okwamalanga amane ngeviki, leqembu leGreen lalilesifiso sonalesi futhi babekukhankasela lokhu ngomnyaka ka-2017 ngesikhathi kusenziwa ukhetho.

Kuyini iGlobal Citizen Festival Njalo Kukhona Yini Esikwenzile Ukuze Yehlise Ubuyanga?
Ngawonalo uMgqibelo edolobheni leNew York kuzaba lomcimbi owenziwa kanye ngomnyaka okuthiwa yiGlobal Citizen Festival, umcimbi lo ubalabahlabeleli abanengi abadumileyo futhi ulenhloso enhle kakhulu eyokuqeda ubuyanga obuhlasele umhlaba wonke.
Lo ngumnyaka wesikhombisa ukuthi umcimbi weGlobal Citizen Festival ubekhona futhi uzaba lezinkulungwane zabantu ezizabuthana eCentral Park Great Lawn ezizakholisa ukubukela abahlabeleli abanengi okugoqela uJanet Jackson, uCardi B loShawn Mendes, kodwa akusoze kuphelele lapho ngoba abantu abazabe bekhona bazakhunjuzwa ngenhloso yomcimbi lo, eyokuthi kube sekuqedwe ubuyanga obukhona ngo 2030.
I-Global Citizen Festival yaqalisa ngomnyaka ka-2012 futhi iyingxenye yenhlanganiso yeGlobal Poverty Project, inhlanganiso leyi ilethemba lokuthi izenelisa ukuqeda ubuyanga ngokuqhubeka isiba labantu abanengi emazweni wonke abangancedisa ekuqedeni uhlupho lolu.
Nxa umuntu efuna itikiti lokuthi aye emcimbini lowu (ngaphandle nxa ezimisele ukuthenga itikiti labantu abaqakathekileyo) kumele aqalise ngokwenza izinto ezinenginengi ezinjengokuncedisa emisebenzini okumele yenziwe, ukubhalela loba nguphi umongameli welizwe i-email, ukufonela omunye umuntu osesikhundleni kumbe ukwenza loba yini emnika ithuba lokutshela abantu ngohlelo lolu lokuqeda ubuyanga.
Kodwa okuhlelwe yi Global Citizen kuhamba njani njengoba sokusele iminyaka engu 12 yokuthi benze lokho abakuhlosileyo?
Nxa abantu betshelwa ukuthi bazaphiwa amatikiti amahala ukuze baye emcimbini lo, kambe ukuthi lokho kungabenza basekele inhlelo lezi yini, iyanceda yini indlela yokusekela inhlelo lezi ‘kusetshenziswa ezokuxhumana’ - kambe ukuthi ukubhala umlayezo ku-inthanethi kumbe ukuthumela itweet kwenza umehluko?
Kusukela ngo 2011 iGlobal Citizen isibe lezinto ezedlula 19 miliyoni “ezenziwe” ngabayisekelayo, abanye becela ukuthi kube lokunye okunenginengi okumele kwenziwe.
Bathi lokhu sekwenze ukuthi abakhokheli abasemazweni atshiyeneyo batsho ukuthi bazimisele ukuncedisa ekusekeleni inhlelo lezi futhi imali abangayithola lapha ingedlula amadola angu 37 bhiliyoni (US) njalo imali le iyabe izanceda abantu abedlula 2.25 bhiliyoni kungakedluli umnyaka ka-2030.
Ekuqaliseni kuka-2018, iqembu leli lalilenhlelo ezingu-390 okwakumele lizenze futhi imali efika amadola angu 10 bhiliyoni yayisitholakele njalo yasetshenziselwa lokho.
Kucatshangelwa ukuthi imali etholakeleyo isincede abantu abangafika amamiliyoni angu 649 emhlabeni wonke.
Olunye uhlelo abalwenzileyo oluthiwa yiPower of Nutrition, olulabantu base-U.K abafake imali labanye abasekela ukuthi uhlelo lolu lulandelwe bathi bafuna “ukunceda abantwana bakhule ngokweneleyo,” bathembise lokunceda ilizwe leRwanda ngamadola angu-35 miliyoni (US) ukuze kuqedwe uhlupho lwendlala eselizweni leli, ngemva kokuthola imilayezo eyedlula 4,700 kutweeter evela kuGlobal Citizens.
Omela iPower of Nutrition uTracey Ullman utshele ixuku ebelisemcimbini owenzelwe eLondon ngo-April 2018 wathi, “Nxa sincediswa nguhulumende we-U. K., abancedisa bezimele bodwa, ohulumende bakwamanye amazwe lani lonke abeGlobal Citizens singenelisa ukuqeda uhlupho lobuyanga lolwendlala.”
Iqembu leli libika ukuthi ngemva kwezicelo ezedlula 5 000 ezenziwa mayelana le U.K. kucelwa ukuthi abantwana labomama bathole ukudla okwakha umzimba, uhulumende wathembisa ukuthi wayezasekela uhlelo oluthiwa yiPower of Nutrition, oluzanceda omama Labantwana abafika 5 miliyoni abaswela ukudla okwakha umzimba.

IGlobal Citizen iphendule yathi: “Ngumsebenzi omkhulu futhi onzima kakhulu- ngezinye izikhathi sizaphumelela kodwa ngezinye sizakwehluleka.

I-US ingasebenzisa Amabutho Aselwandle "ukuvimba" ukuze aphambanise ukuthengisela amandla kwamanye amazwe okwenziwa yiRussia - uNobhala Wokwenzakala Ngaphakathi Kwelizwe
"Nxa kudingeka" iWashington ingacina isisebenzisa Amabutho ayo Aselwandle ukuvimbela ukuthi iRussia ingaphumeleli ukuthengisa amandla, okugoqela eMiddle East, uNobhala Wokwenzakala Ngaphakathi Kwelizwe wase-US uRyan Zinke wakuveza, njengoba kutshiwo yiWashington Examiner.
UZinke wamangalela ngokuthi ukungenela kweRussia eSyria - ikakhulu, lapho esebenza khona ivunyelwe nguhulumende osemthethweni - yizaba zokudinga izindawo ezintsha zokuthengisela amandla.
"Ngikholwa ukuthi isizatho sabo sokuba seMiddle East yikuthi bazama ukuncedisa ukuthengisa amandla njengalokho abakwenzayo empumalanga Europe, inkabazwe engaseningizimu ye-Europe," kuthiwa watsho njalo.
Njalo, njengokwatshiwo yisiphathamandla, kulezindlela zokuphatha udaba lolo.
"I-United States ingenelisa ukwenza njalo, ngamaButho ethu Aselwandle, ukuba leqiniso ukuthi izindlela zaselwandle zivuliwe, njalo, nxa kudingeka, sizivimbe, ukuze sibe leqiniso lokuthi amandla abo kawalandawo lapho athengiswa khona," watsho njalo.
UZinke wayekhuluma lababebuye emkhosini owawenziwe ngabe Consumer Energy Alliance, iqembu elingatholi-nzuzo elizitshela ukuthi lona "liyilizwi lalabo abathenga amandla" e-US.
Waqhubeka waqathanisa izindlela iWashington eyenza ngazo ekuphatheni kwayo leRussia le-Iran, waqamba ukuthi ngandlela-thile kuyafanana.
"Indlela engokomnotho engasebenza ku-Iran leRussia, ingaba yikusebenzisa amandla lokufaka okunye esikhundleni samafutha," watsho njalo, ekhuluma ngokuthi iRussia "ilikhadi elilahlisayo" ilomnotho oweyeme kumafutha avela emhlabathini.
Amazwi la akhulunywa njengoba abakhokhelwa nguTrump bebesebenzela ukuthuthukisa ukuthengisela kwabo igasi engamanzi e-Europe, bethatha isikhundla seRussia, eyiyo etshiphela kakhulu abathengi base-Europe.
Ukuze lokho kusebenze, iziphathamandla ezikhokhelwa nguTrump, okugoqela uMongameli we-US uDonald Trump ngokwakhe, zizama ukuncenga iGermany ukuba iphume kupurojekithi "engafanelanga" yephayiphi yeNord Stream 2, leyo ngokubona kukaTrump, eyenze iBerlin yaba "yisigqila" seMoscow.
IMoscow ihlala igcizelela ukuthi iphayiphi yeNord Stream 2 ebiza imali engange-$11 amabhiliyoni, ilungiselelwa ukuthi iphinde kabili okuthwalwa yiphayiphi ekhona khathesi kube ngamacubic mitha angamabhiliyoni angu-110, imane nje iyipurojekithi yezomnotho.
IKremlin ikhalaza ngokuthi ukuphikisa ngamandla okwenziwa yiWashington kupurojekithi le kumane nje kubangelwa yizizatho zezomnotho njalo kuyisibonelo sokuncintisana okungafanelanga.
"Ngithemba ukuthi sonke silombono wokuthi amandla awasilothuluzi lokusebenzisa ukuncindezela kanye lokuthi abathengi kumele benelise ukukhetha abangafuna ukuthenga kuye," kwatsho iSiphathamandla seRussian Energy u-Aleksandr Novak ngemva komhlangano loNobhala we-US Energy uRick Perry eMoscow ngoMpandula.
Okukhethwe yi-US. kusolwe kakhulukazi yiGermany, eqinisekise ukuthi izimisele ngepurojekithi.
Inhlanganiso yaseGermany ekhokhelayo ngezokulungiswa kwezinto, iFedaration of German Industries (BDI), isicele ukuthi i-US ihlalele khatshana lemithetho yamandla ye-EU kanye lokuvumelana okuphakathi kwababili iBerlin leMoscow.
"Kuyangikhathaza nxa ilizwe lesithathu selingenela ezindabeni zokuthola kwethu amandla," kwatsho uDieter Kempf, umkhokheli weFederation of German Industries (BDI) watsho njalo kulandela umhlangano osanda kuba khona phakathi kukaChancellor waseGermany uAngela Merkel loMongameli weRussia uVladmir Putin.

Utshele abephephandaba okuthiwa yi-The Hill ukuthi, “Sekuyisikhathi sokuthi abesifazana baye eWashington balungise uhlupho esilalo kuhumende futhi lokho kuhlanganisa lami owesifazana olesikhundla esiphezulu.”

UWarren uchothoze uMongameli uDonald Trump ngesikhathi esewolu le esithi “akwenzayo kuzatshiya indawo le ingokunye.”
Uthe “Kuyangethusa okuzwayo okwenziwa nguDonald Trump endleleni abantu belizwe lethu okumele babuswe ngayo.”

Ikanti abantu abangamaphesenti angu-32 bavumelana lokuthi kumele ancintise.

Ubotshwe ethonisiswa icala lokuhlukuluza owesifazana, ngoMvulo ebusuku
Okukhangelane lomntanami, okukhangelane laye ngemva kokuphenduka kwakhe, kungenza ngizwisise ezinye izimuli ezilabantwana abaphenduka sebehlukuluzeka engqondweni(PTSD), njalo lokulimala okubuya kwenze amabutho ethu," watshela abantu ababebuthene besekela uDonald Trump eTulsa eseOklahoma.
UPalin uthi ukubotshwa komntanakhe "luhlupho olusendlini," njalo wabesekhuluma ngomntanakhe labanye abalwela ilizwe njengamabutho kudala esithi, "bayaphenduka sebentshintshile, bayaphenduka sebeqinisa intamo njalo bayaphenduka sebekhathazeka ukuthi basahlonipheka yini njengamanye amabutho, labo bonke abasebenzayo esisotsheni, ngalokhu abakwenzelayo ilizwe labo."
Wabotshwa ngoMvulo eWasilla eseAlaska, ethonisiswa icala lokuhlukuluza owesifazana ngokumulimaza, lokungenela efuna ukuphambanisa umbiko wokuhlukuluzwa kwabesifazana njalo lokuthwala isikhali edakiwe, ngokutsho kukaDan Bennett, isikhulumeli sasedipathimenti lamapholisa aweWasilla.
Izabelo ezingu 18 kanye leDC zivumelana lokusolwa komthetho omutsha omayelana labantu ababalekela kwamanye amazwe
Izabelo ezingu 18 leDistrict of Columbia zivumelana lokusolwa komthetho omutsha okhitshwe yi-U.S. owenqabela abantu ababaleka kwamanye amazwe ukuthi bahlale elizweni labo ngenxa yokubalekela iqembu lezigebenga kumbe ukuhlukuluzwa ezindlini.
I-NBC News ibike ukuthi abameli bezabelo ezingu 18 labeDistrict of Columbia bathumele isikhalazo sabo emthethwandaba ngomthetho omutsha omayelana labantu ababaleka emazweni abo ngoLwesihlanu eWashington, kodwa lokho akutsho ukuthi bethesa uhulumende icala.
Endabeni kaGrace v Sessions ebhaliswe ngo-August, I-American Civil Liberties Union isola umthetho osetshenziswa kwesinye isabelo, ibizo eligcweleyo lalowo olethe icala leli emthethwandaba alikavezwa.
Uthe indoda yakhe “labantwabakhe abaseqenjini lezigebenga” bamhlukuluza kodwa iziphathamandla ze-U.S. zamncitsha imvumo yokuthi ahlale elizweni lelo mhlaka 20 July.
Umama lo wabotshwa eTexas.
Amagqwetha kahulumende asekela uGrace athe kulabantu abanengi ababaleka e-El Salvador, eHonduras laseGuatemala bezocela imvumo yokuhlala e-U.S ngenxa yokuthwaliswa nzima ngamaqembu ezigebenga lokuhlukuluzwa ezindlini.
Umthetho omutsha otshaywe yi-U.S omayelana labantu ababalekela elizweni labo, ucitsha isinqumo esenziwa yiBoard of Immigrant Appeals ngo-2014 esasivumela ukuthi abantu abangena elizweni leli bengela zincwadi ezisemthethweni bebalekela ukuhlukuluzwa emazweni abo bangacela imvumo yokuhlala elizweni leli.
Igqwetha elikhulu leDistrict of Columbia uKarl Racine ukhulume ngalokhu embikweni okhitshwe ngoLwesihlanu esithi “umthetho lo utshintsha into esileminyaka eminengi isenziwa nguhulumende, yizabelo langamanye amazwe.”
Isikhalazo esiye emthethwandaba besisithi, “Umthetho wesabelo uthi isicelo ngasinye sokuphiwa imvumo yokuhlala kwelinye ilizwe ngenxa yokubaleka elizweni lakho kumele sihlolisiswe kukhangelwa okwenzakalayo esimeni ngasinye futhi kuhlolwe lobufakazi balokho, kodwa kukhanya angani umthetho lo obekiweyo awukwenzi lokhu.”
Amagqwetha la aphinde athi umthetho wokwalisa abantu bakwamanye amazwe ukuthi bahlale elizweni leli kubisela ezomnotho ze-U. S. emuva ngoba kungenzakala ukuthi abantu laba babe lamabhizimusi kumbe “bacine bethole imisebenzi.”
Ngenyanga kaJune, igqwetha elikhulu uJeff Sessions latshela iziphathamandla ezinika labo abangena elizweni leli ukuthi zingasaniki abantu ababaleka emazweni abo ngenxa yokuhlukuluzwa ngamaqembu ezigebenga kumbe ezindlini imvumo yokuhlala elizweni leli.
Isaziso esakhitshwa nguSessions mhlaka 11 June sasisithi, “Abangaphiwa imvumo yokuhlala elizweni lethu ngenxa yokubaleka emazweni abo yilabo abesabayo kumbe abahlukuluzwayo ngenxa yomhlobo, isonto, ukuthi yisizalwane sangaphi, kumbe ngokuba lilunga leyinye inhlanganiso kumbe ukuba ngoweqembu lezombusazwe.”
Imvumo yokuthi abantu babalekele kwamanye amazwe kayenzelwanga ukuqeda inhlupho zonke zabantu-- ngitsho lenhlupho ezinkulu ezihlangana labantu nsukuzonke emhlabeni wonke.

Kuqhubeka kusiba nzima ukuthola abasindayo.
"Sokunzima kakhulu," utsho njalo umama oleminyaka engu35, uRisa Kusuma eduduza umntanakhe ongumfana otshisa umzimba ngokugula besendaweni eyokubalekela nxa kwenzakale umonakalo ePalu.
"Imota ezithwala izigulane, lokhu zibuya ngezidumbu zabantu umzuzu ngamunye.
Amanzi ahlanzekileyo katholakali."
Izakhamuzi sezibonwa zibuyela ezindlini zabo ezibhidliziweyo, besiyadobha izinto phakathi kwamanzi bezama ukubona nxa kulezinto abangazisebenzisayo.
Kulezikhulu zabantu ezilimeleyo njalo kulezibhedlela ezilemiduli elinyaziweyo ngokuzamazama komhlaba lokhu kade kulamandla afika7.5, njalo bezigcwele abantu.
Kulabo abalimeleyo, okuhlanganisela uDwi Haris, oqamuke iqolo lokulimala ihlombe, kade behlezi phandle kwesibhedlela samasotsha sePelu lapho izigulane kade ziselatshelwa phandle ngenxa yokuzamazama komhlaba kade kusaqhubeka.
Amehlo akhe agcwele inyembezi ekhuluma ngalokho okwenzakeleyo esehoteleni, esesitezini sesihlanu sesakhiwo lesi lomkakhe lendodakazi yakhe kuze kube lokuzamazama komhlaba okulamandla.
"Bekungela isikhathi sokuthi sizisindise ngokwethu.
Ngicabanga ukuthi, bengifithizelwe phakathi komduli," uHaris etshela iAssociated Press, njalo wangezelela ukuthi imuli yakhe kade ibuye emtshadweni.
"Ngizwe umkami ebizela uncedo, kodwa ngabesengisizwa esethule.
Angikwazi ukuthi kwenzakale njani kuye lomntanami.
Ngithemba bavikelekile."
Ummeli weU.S. eChina wethesa icala iChina 'ngokuzama ukubayethusela' ngamazwi abo 'amanga'
Sokudlule iviki ngemva kwelinye iphephandaba laseChina libhale amapeji amane phakathi kwephephandaba leU.S., lifakaza ukuthi bayakholisa kwezokuthengiselana phakathi kweUS leChina, kodwa ummeli weU.S. wethesa icala iBeijing ngokusebenzisa iphephandaba leAmerica leli ukusakaza amanga lawa.
U.S. UMongameli welizwe UDonald Trump wakhuluma ngokwephephandaba leli elithiwa yiChina Daily elibhadalwayo kuDes Moines Register - iphephandaba leIowa elithengwa kakhulu - ngemva kokwethesa icala iChina ukuthi yayifuna ukungenela kwezokhetho zombusazwe zelizwe leU.S. ngoNov 6, kodwa iChina iyala ukuthi yakwenza lokhu.
Ukwethesa icala lokhu okwenzwa nguTrump esithi, iBeijing ibizama ukungenela kwezokhetho lelizwe leU.S., bekungumzamo womkhankaso owenzwa yiWashington ukuthi bacindezele iChina, abaphathi beU.S. batshele iReuters khonokho.
Lanxa kujayelekile ukuthi ohulumende bamanye amazwe bafakaze ngezokuthengiselana kumaphephandaba, iBeijing leWashington kukhanya kazizwanani ngoba kulokulwisana kwezokuthengiselana okukhona phakathi kwabo okuyenza ukuthi bakhwezelane imithelo kwezokuthengiselana.
Ukuphangisa ukukhweza kweChina imithelo yabo kwezokuthengiselana ekulwisaneni lokhu, kulungiselelwe ukuthi kuphambanise labo abathengisayo izinto kwamanye amazwe, njengesabelo seIowa esisekela uTrump kuqembu lakhe leRepublican, zitsho njalo ingcitshi ezibona ngokweChina leU.S.
UTerry Branstad, ummeli weU.S. eChina njalo owake waba ngusibalukhulu oweIowa okwesikhathi eside kusabelo esithengisa izilinywa ezinengi eChina, uthe iBeijing ilimaze izisebenzi, abalimi labezamabhizimusi.
UBranstad ubhale umbono wakhe kuSunday Des Moines Register esithi iChina, "isingezelela ukusethusela ngamazwi ayo amanga kuphephandaba lethu."
"Uhulumende weChina ungezelela ukukhuluma amanga lawa esebenzisa isiko seAmerica sokukhuluma bekhululekile njalo lokufaka abakufunayo kuphephandaba leli elibhadalwayo ukuthi lisakaze kuDes Moines Register," watsho njalo uBranstad.
"Ngomehluko, kulabo abasakaza izindaba eBeijing, balutshwana abavumelana lakho njalo kawusoze wathola iqiniso kusimo esikhona eChina, ukuthi akumanga kuhle kwezenotho ngoba abasakazayo baphansi kwesandla seqembu leChinese Communist," watsho njalo.
Wangezelela ukuthi, "enye iphephandaba elihlonitshwayo eChina layala ukuphumisa indaba leyi," eyami, lanxa engakhulumanga ukuthi yiliphi iphephandaba lakhona.

AmaRepublican amanengi alezikhundla eziphezulu asekela uBrett Kavanaugh okhethwe ukuba lilunga leSupreme Court lanxa esetheswa amacala alokwenza lokuhlukuluza abanye kwezemacansini, kodwa abahluzisisayo bathi indaba le izabaphendukela ikakhulu ebantwini besifazana ngesikhathi sokhetho olwenziwa ngemva kweminyaka emibili kukhethwe umongameli.
Abanengi ayibaphathanga ngitsho lakancane indaba leyi futhi kubikwa ukuthi amaRepublican amanengi asefuna ukuthi ukhetho lwenziwe.
Endabeni ekhitshwe liphephandaba le-The Hill ngoMgqibelo, isikhwicamfundo sesayensi yezombusazwe eseMaxwell School eYunivesithi yeSyracuse uGrant Reeher uthe, “Akulalutho esingalutshintsha ngokwenzakeleyo.”

UChristine Blasey Ford, kubika abeMic.
