Umsunguli We-World Wide Web Uhlela Ukusungula I-inthanethi Ezancintisana LeGoogle Kanye LeFacebook
UTim Berners-Lee, umsunguli we-World Wide Web, useqalise uhlelo olukhanya angani luzancintisana leFacebook, i-Amazon kanye leGoogle.
UBerners-Lee yingcitshi yezempucuko futhi usebenza lekhampani okuthiwa yi- Inrupt, ohlelweni lolu olutsha futhi luzasebenza phose ngendlela iSolid esebenza ngayo futhi ingcitshi le yasebenza ohlelweni lolu.
Uhlelo lweSolid luvumela abalusebenzisayo ukuthi bakhethe lapho abafuna ukugcina khona loba yini emayelana labo kumbe umsebenzi wabo lokunquma ukuthi ngobani abangabona lokho abasebenza kukho.
Engxoxweni abelayo labe-Fast Company, uBerners-Lee uqale ngokuhleka esithi inhloso ye-Inrupt “ngeyokubusa umhlaba.”
Ekhuluma ngohlelo lolu uthe, “Kumele sikwenze khathesi.”
“Yinto engakaze yenzakale leyi.”
I-app leyi isebenzisa uhlelo lweSolid oluvumela abantu ukuthi babe le “personal online data store” ebizwa langokuthi yi-POD.
Uyazikhethela ukuthi ufakani, kungaba zinombolo zabantu oxhumana labo, ikhalenda, izingoma, lezinye nje inhlelo ozifunayo.
Kufanana lokuthi sithethe iGoogle Drive, iMicrosoft Outlook, iSlack kanye leSpotify sakufaka endaweni eyodwa ukuze kusebenze ngesikhathi esifananayo.
Okuhle ngokusebenzisa uhlelo lolu yikuthi kuya ngoyisebenzisayo ukuthi ufuna ukunika bani imvumo yokubona lokho akwenzayo kumbe akugcinileyo.
Ikhampani le ithe lokhu “yikunika abantu amandla ngezempucuko.”
Umaqhuzu omkhulu wekhampani le u-John Bruce uthe okwenze baba lekhampani okuthiwa yi-Inrupt yikuthi bafuna uhlelo lweSolid lutholakale ebantwini bonke njalo basebenze nzima bebuthelela konke abalakho lolwazi abalalo ukuze lokhu kuphumelele.
Okwakhathesi ikhampani le ibunjwa ngu Berners- Lee, uBruce, uhlelo lokuvikeleka kwezempucuko oluthengwe yi-IBM, abanye abaqhatshwe ukwenza umsebenzi wokuthuthukisa uhlelo lolu labanye abangafuni kubhadalwa ukuthi bancedise.
Kusukela kuyonale iviki abathuthukisa ezempucuko sebengaqalisa ukuzilungisela awabo ama-app besebenzisa amathuluzi okwenza lokhu atholakala kuwebhusayithi ye-Inrupt kungelani lokuthi bakuliphi ilizwe.
UBerners-Lee uthe yena leqembu lakhe abasoze bakhulume lutho leFacebook kumbe leGoogle endabeni yokuthi kuzaba lotshintsho bani nxa uhlelo lwabo selusebenza kuhle futhi amakhampani lawa angaphelelwa ngumsebenzi ngelanga elilodwa.
“Asisoze sicele imvumo kubo.”
Lo ngumlayezo obhalwe nguBerners-Lee kuMedium ngoMgqibelo esithi inhloso ye-Inrupt “ngeyokunika abantu amandla kwezebhizimusi lokuncedisa ekuvikeleni umsebenzi wohlonzi oluphezulu wohlelo lwethu lolu esilususele kuSolid."
Ngo 1994, uBerners-Lee watshintsha okunengi kakhulu nge-Inthanethi ngesikhathi esungula i-World Wide Web Consortium eMassachusetts Institute of Technology.
Ezinyangeni ezisanda kudlula, uBerners-Lee ubelokunengi kokutsho empikiswaneni zokusetshenziswa kwe-intanethi futhi uhlonitshwa ngabanengi endabeni le.
Lanxa esungula i-Inrupt, uBerners-Lee ulokhu Engumsunguli loMqondisi we-World Wide Web Consortium, iWeb Foundation le-Open Data Institute.
UBerners-Lee ungezelele ngokuthi, "Angithandabuzi lakancane ukuthi indlela le entsha yokusebenzisa i-inthanethi izaphumelela."
UBernard Vann: Kwenziwa umkhosi wokunanza umfundisi owaphiwa iVictoria Cross ngeMpi Yomhlaba Yokuqala (WW1)
Onguyena kuphela umfundisi weSonto yaseNgilandi owaphiwa iVictoria Cross ngeMpi Yomhlaba Yokuqala elisotsha wenzelwe umkhosi wokumnanza edolobheni lakwabo sekuphele iminyaka engu-100.
ULt Col. uReverend Bernard Vann waphiwa isicoco ngomhlaka-29 Mpandula 1918 ekuhlaseleni okwenziwa eBellenglise laseLehaucourt.
Kodwa, wabulawa ngumuntu odubula ecatshile ngemva kwamalanga amane njalo akazange abe kwazi ukuthi usephiwe isicoco esihloniphekayo esiphezu kwazo zonke kumabutho amaBritish.
Ilitshe lesikhumbuzo lavulwa ngabazukulu bakhe ababili emkhosini wokufola eRushden, eNorthamptonshire, ngoMgqibelo.
Omunye wabazuku bakhe, uMichael Vann, wathi "kwakulomutsho omuhlekazi" ukuthi ilitshe livulwe sekuphele iminyaka engu-100 kanye ukusukela lapho uyisemkhulu abonisa ubugabazi obamtholisa isicoco.
NgokweLondon Gazette, ngomhla ka-29 Mpandula 1918 uLt Col Vann wakhokhela ibutho lakhe liquma iCanal de Saint Quentin "phakathi kwenkungu emnyama kakhulu njalo inhlamvu ziphapha okuzwayo zivela kwabadubulayo lakuzigwagwa."
Wasuka wagijimela emzileni wamasotsha adubulayo njalo "ngesenzo sesibindi esikhulukazi" wakhokhela amasotsha phambili engakagijimeli endaweni lapho okwakudutshulwa khona eyedwa wawisa abathathu beqembu lesitha.
ULt Col Vann wabulawa ngodubula ecatshile waseJelimane ngomhla ka-4 kuMfumfu 1918 - phezudlwana nje kwenyanga impi ingakapheli.
UMichael Vann, oleminyaka engu-72, wathi izenzo zikayisemkhulu "zazingokuthile engikwaziyo ukuthi ngeke ngenelise ukukwenza empilweni yami kodwa okuthile okwenza ngizithobe."
Yena lomfowabo uDr James Vann baphinda bafaka amaluba ngemva kokufola, okwakhokhelwa yiBhendi yeBrentwood Imperial Youth.
UMichael Vann wathi "wayesizwa ehlonitshwe kakhulu ukuba lengxenye ekufoleni" wangezelela ukuthi "isibindi seqhawe loqobo siyabonakaliswa ngosekelo oluzaluphiwa ngabantu abanengi."
Abasekeli beMMA, abalalanga bemelele ukubukela iBellator 206 ubusuku bonke, kodwa bacine befakelwa iPeppa Pig
Akucabange lokhu, kawulalanga ubusuku bonke ubukela iBellator 206, kodwa ngesikhathi sekubuya isenzakalo esiqakathekileyo, ubusucitshelwa.
Umdlalo ophumiswe nguSan Jose kade ulemidlalo engu13, kuhlanganisela eminye imidlalo eyisithupha kade izaphumiswa kuChannel 5 eUK ubusuku bonke.
Ngo6 ekuseni, njengoba uGegard Mousasi loRory MacDonald sebelungiselela ukuthi balwe, ababukeli batshiyiwe bemangele njengoba kuhle kwantshintsha uhlelo kwafakwa uPeppa Pig.
Abanye kubacaphulile lokhu ngoba bebengalalanga ubusuku bonke bemelele umdlalo lo.
Omunye umsekeli womdlalo lo, ekhuluma kwezokuxhumana ngokuntshintsha lokhu kusiya kubopopayi kwabantwana uthe, "yikuhlanya lokhu."
"Ngumuthetho kahulumende wokuthi ngo6 ekuseni, uhlelo lwezodlakela luyabe lungasasakazwi, yikho behle bantshintsha uhlelo bafaka olabantwana," watsho njalo uDavid Schwartz, isiphathi esisekela umongameli weBellator esibona ngokusakazwa langokuphumiswa kohlelo lolu, beze bemubuze ukuthi ngenxa yani bentshintshile uhlelo.
""IPeppa pig," yebo."
UMongameli weBellator, uScott Coker uthe bazalungisa uhlelo lwabo ukwenzela elakusasa lezibukeli zaseUK.
"Ngokubona kwami ngicabanga ukuthi singawudlala futi uhlelo lolu, ngicabanga ukuthi kuyayenza," watsho njalo uCoker.
"Kodwa kasenelisi ukukukwenza ngenxa yokutshiyana kwezikhathi, khona ngale ngu6 ekuseni ngeSonto khathesi, kutsho ukuthi kumele lathi simelele isikhathi esifananayo ngapha ngeSonto, kodwa khona ngale kuyabe sokunguMvulo.
Kodwa siyazama ukulungisa.
Ukukhuluma iqiniso, uhlelo lolu luthe luntshintsha kuqaliswe ukuthunyezelwa imilayezo, njalo imilayezo leyi ibingalunganga.
Sike sazama ukulungisa, ngoba besesicabange ukuthi yimitshina yethu engasasebenzi kuhle.
Kodwa kade ingayisiyo, bekulandelwa umuthetho kahulumende.
Ngiyalithembisa ukuthi, akusoze kwaphinda kwayenzakala.
Sizazama ukuthi siyitshiye imidlalo emihlanu kuphela kulokuthi ibe yisithupha - njengoba sihlala sisenza - sizame ukwenza kade kungekho emandleni ethu sifuna ukuthokozisa abasekeli bomdlalo lo kodwa kusiphambanisile.
Yinto kade singayikhangelelanga."
IDesert Island Discs: UTom Daley 'wayezikhangelela phansi' ngokuthi ulezifiso zokuya emacansini labantu baphi
Ontshezayo owe-Olympic uTom Daley uthi wakhula ezikhangelela phansi emuntwini wonke ngokuthi ulezifiso zokuya emacansini labantu baphi - kodwa lokho kwamupha izizatho zokuba aphumelele.
Oleminyaka engu-24 wathi kazange akunanzelele kwaze kwaba yilapho esesesikolo sesekhondari ukuthi "kayisibo bonke abanjengami."
Ekhuluma okokuqala kuRadio 4 Desert Island Discs eyethulwa nguLauren Laverne, wathi ukhuluma sobala ngamalungelo ezitabane ukuze anike abanye "ithemba."
Waphinda watsho ukuthi ukuba ngumzali kwamenza angabi lendaba kakhulu lokuwina kuma-Olympics.
Ojayele ukwethula uhlelo lolu oselulesikhathi eside lusenziwa, uKirsty Young, usekewathatha izinyanga ezithile engekho emsebenzini ngenxa yokugula.
Esethulwa njengolahlelwe iganga ohlelweni lokuqala lukaLaverne, uDaley wathi esakhula wayezizwa "engaphansi" kwabanye abantu bonke ngenxa yokuthi "kwakungemukeleki emphakathini ukuthanda abafana lamankazana."
Wathi: Kuze kube khathesi, imizwa yokuzizwa ngingaphansi, kanye lokuzizwa ngitshiyene, yizona kanye izinto ezingiphe amandla okuba ngiphumelele."
Wayefuna ukutshengisa ukuthi laye "ungokuthile" watsho njalo, ukuze angaze adanisa wonke umuntu lapho ekucineni sebethola ukuthi ulezifiso zokuya emacansini labantu baphi.
Lo owake wathola imendulu yebronzi kabili kuma-Olympic usebe ngumkhankaseli oveleleyo weLGBT njalo usebenzise ukuba khona kwakhe eMidlalweni yamaOlympic yeCommonwealth e-Australia ukucela ukuthi amazwe amanengi akhuphe ukungabi semthethweni kobutabane.
Uthi wakhuluma obala ngenxa yokuthi wayezizwa elenhlanhla ukuthi uyenelisa ukuziphilela ngokusobala kungela mpumela emibi njalo wayefuna ukupha abanye "ithemba."
Lo osebe yintshantshu kathathu emhlabeni wonke wathi ukuba semathandweni lendoda - owenza amafilimu wase-US uDustin Lance Black, lowo ahlangana laye ngo-2013 - "kwangijuma ngilibele"
UDaley watshada lalo oseke wawina i-Oscar, omdala kulaye ngeminyaka engu-20, nyakenye kodwa wathi ukutshiyana kwabo ngeminyaka akukaze kube yindaba ehluphayo.
"Nxa ungahlangana lokunengi kangaka usesemncane" - wahamba emidlalweni yakhe yokuqala yama-Olympics eleminyaka engu-14 njalo uyise wabulawa yimvukuzane yasengqondweni ngemva kweminyaka emithathu - wathi kunzima ukuthola omunye olingana lawe osehlangane lobunzima lobuhle obufanana lobakho.
Laba ababili baba ngabazali ngoNhlangula, indodana yabo ithiwa nguRobert Jay Black-Daley, njalo uDaley wathi "umbono wakhe wonke" wawusutshintshile.
"Aluba wawungibuze nyakenye, kwakuyikuthi 'ngikufuna ukuwina imendulu yegolide kuphela'," watsho njalo.
"Uyazini, kulezinye izinto ezinkulu ukwedlula amamendulu egolide e-Olympic.
Imendulu yami yegolide ye-Olympic nguRobbie."
Indodana yakhe ilebizo elifanana lelikayise uRobert, owafa ngo-2011 eleminyaka engu-40 ngemva kokutholakala elemvukuzane yasengqondweni.
UDaley wathi uyise kazange akwamukele ukuthi wayezakufa njalo okunye kwezinto acina ukumbuza zona kwakuyikuthi basebelawo yini amatikiti abo awe-London 2012 - njengoba wayefuna ukuba ehlezi ezihlalweni eziphambili.
"Ngehluleka ukumtshela ukuthi 'awusoze ube khona ezihlalweni eziphambili ngaleso sikhathi baba'," watsho njalo.
"Ngangibambe isandla sakhe aze ame ukuphefumula njalo kwaze kwaba yilapho eseme ukuphefumula njalo esefile lapho engacina ngivuma ukuthi sekumehlule," watsho njalo.
Ngomnyaka owalandelayo uDaley wancintisa kuma-Olympic ka-2012 wawina ibronzi.
"Ngangikwazi ukuthi yikho engangikuphupha okwempilo yami yonke - ukuntsheza phambi kwezibukeli zakithi eMidlalweni yama-Olympic, kwakungelamuzwa odlula lowo," watsho njalo.
Yikho futhi okwamenza wakhetha ingoma yakhe yokuqala - ethi Proud eyahlatshelwa nguHeather Small - eyahambelana laye ngesikhathi elungiselela ama-Olympic njalo lakhathesi isamthinta kwamancane.
IDesert Island Discs iphuma kuBBC Radio 4 ngeSonto ngo-11:15 BST.
UMickelson ukhitshiwe emdlalweni weNkezo yeRyder ngoMgqibelo
Umdlali we-America uPhil Mickelson uzakwenza into enkulu kakhulu ngeSonto ngokuba semdlalweni weNkezo yeRyder okwesi-47, kodwa kuzamele abophe ziqine ukuze awuqede ethokoza umdlalo lo.
Lo ngumdlalo wesi-12 kaMickelson emidlalweni eyenziwa ngemva kweminyaka emibili, kodwa ukhephutheni wakhe uJim Furyk umkhiphile emdlalweni wamabhola amane lowokutshaya ibhola betshintshana.
Kulokuthi kube nguye obedlala okwesikhathi eside njengoba kujayele ukuba njalo nxa kuyi United States, umdlali lo oyingcitshi osenqobe kahlanu uke wama ukudlala eqakazela abanye njalo esenza okunye emaceleni elethemba lokuthi kuzamnceda kuloba kuyini okumkhathazayo.
Umdlali lo odume ngokutshaya amabhola kuzwa aqonda lapho okumele ayekhona oleminyaka engu-48, kungani kuyamhlupha ukudlala enkundleni okuthiwa yi-Le Golf National lapho okulula khona ukutshayela eceleni ngenxa yotshani obukhulu kumbe okunye okuphambanisayo.
Kumthwalise nzima uMickelson ukudlalela enkundleni le kodwa akupheleli lapho, ngoba khona ezancintisana lentshantshu yeBritish Open uFrancesco Molinari ngeSonto futhi umdlali lo uyanemba, njalo useqenjini lejaha elingelasikhathi eside emdlalweni lo uTommy Fleetwood ikanti iqembu leli linqobe emidlalweni yonke yomine ekade lilayo kuyonale iviki.
Abadlali be-America basemuva ngemiklomelo emine kusukela emidlalweni engu-12 ngamunye wabo aseyidlalile, kodwa nxa bengaqalisa kuhle umdlalo kaMickelson uyabe uqakathekile sibili.
UFuryk uthe uyamthemba omunye wakhe, uhle wazithuthela ngoba engala okunengi kokutsho.
UFuryk uthe, “Uyakwazi umsebenzi omkhulu akade elawo lamuhla, ungimbambathile emhlane wasengigona wathi uzabe esewulungele umdlalo wakusasa.”
“Kazikhangeleli phansi kodwa uyazithemba.
Ngumdlali odumileyo futhi wenze okunengi emaqenjini la evikini edlulileyo lakuyonale.
Bengingazange ngimcabange edlala imidlalo emibili.
Ngicabange okwedlula lapho, kodwa yikho okwenzakeleyo futhi sicabanga ukuthi kumele senze njalo.
Uyafuna ukuba senkundleni adlale, njengomuntu wonke.”
Imidlalo kaMickelson izadlula inani lemidlalo yeNkezo yeRyder eyadlalwa nguNick Faldo ngeSonto.
Kungaba ngokokucina ukuthi okunje kwenzakale emidlalweni yeNkezo yeRyder aseke wayidlala lanxa indlela adlala ngayo itshiyene kakhulu ladume ngakho.
UMickelson usenqobe ka-18, wanqotshwa ka-20 ikanti wabelana labanye imiklomelo kasikhombisa, kodwa uFuryk uthe ngeke atsho ukuthi ukuba khona komdlali lo eqenjini labo kuncede ngaphi sibisibili.
Wasesithi, “Uyisiphoxo, uthanda ukusoma, uloqalo, ukhaliphile njalo siyakukholisa ukuba laye eqenjini lethu.”
“Ngicabanga ukuthi abadlali abasakhulayo bakukholisile ukuthi baphinde bamqale lakuleyi iviki, sikukholisile lokho.
Kapheleli ekudlaleni kodwa wenza okudlula lapho.”
Ukhephutheni we-Europe uThomas Bjorn uyakwazi ukuthi izinto zingaphonguthi phendu lanxa khathesi bekhokhela
UThomas Bjorn, ongukhephutheni we-Europe uyakwazi ukuthi izinto zingatshintsha loba nini ngoba lokhu kwake kwenzakala, utsho lokhu ngoba basalelwe lilanga elilodwa emdlalweni weNkezo yeRyder futhi yibo abakhokhelayo.
Isizalwane lesi seDenmark saba lomdlalo waso wokuqala ngo 1997 eValderrama lapho iqembu elalokhephutheni okuthiwa nguSeve Ballesteros lalikhokhela ngemiklomelo emihlanu ngesikhathi lidlala lele-America kodwa kwathi umdlalo ususiyaphela bananzelela ukuthi basile ngesikhala senalithi ngoba phela banqoba nge14½-13½.
“Uhlala uzikhumbuza ukuthi sasiphambili sibili eValderrama, saphinda saqalisa siphambili eBrookline, kodwa sanqotshwa, lanxa sanqoba eValderrama, kwakusele kancane ukuthi sinqotshwe,” ngamazwi kaBjorn, osemfanekisweni, eqeda kubukela iKilasi ka-2018 eyanqoba 5-3 ngoLwesihlanu layizolo futhi lokhu kuyenze yakhokhela nge 10-6 eLe Golf National.
Yikho mina labo bonke abaseqenjini leli siyakwazi ukuthi kusaselomsebenzi ngoba asikanqobi.
Kumele sonke sibophe ziqine kusasa.
Asiyeni enkundleni senze esikwenelisayo ukuze sidlale kuhle.
Asikanqobi kodwa sinqoba nxa imiklomelo isibhalwe ebhodini lathi sesiyibona.
Kukhona esikuhlosileyo, sifuna ukusebenza nzima ukuze sizame ukuthatha inkezo leyi futhi kulapho esikhangelise khona amehlo ethu.
Ngihlala ngisitsho ukuthi amehlo wami ngiwathe nhlo kubadlali beqembu lethu abangu-12, kodwa siyakwazi lokuthi ngobani abakwelinye icele, sincintisana labadlali abazingcitshi emhlabeni wonke.
Ubethokoza kakhulu ngendlela iqembu lakhe elidlale ngayo enkundleni yegolf okunzima ukudlalela kuyo, uBjorn uphinde wathi: “Angisoze ngizithembe kakhulu endabeni leyi.
Umdlalo wakusasa awuthambanga.
Okuqakatheke kakhulu kusasa yikuthi umdlali ngamunye uzadlala njani futhi lokho akulula.
Kumnandi ukudlala lomunye wakho lincedisana futhi umdlalo ulihambela kuhle, kodwa nxa udlala wedwa kuzakhanya sibili ukuthi uyingcitshi yomdlalo lo loba hatshi.
Yikho umdlali ngamunye kumele azwisise ukuqakatheka kokwenza konke akwenelisayo kusasa.
Khathesi kumele ukhohlwe ngomuntu obekuncedisa ngoba sekungundoda zibonele, wonke umuntu kumele asebenze nzima.”
UJim Furyk oleqembu elizancintisana lelikaBjorn, ufuna ukuthi umdlali ngamunye weqembu lakhe enze okungcono kakhulu ukwedlula ababekwenza ngesikhathi bedlala bencedisana, ngaphandle kukaJordan Spieth lomunye wakhe uJustin Thomas, abathola imiklomelo emithathu kwemine.
UFuryk yena uyakwazi ukuthi kunjani ukunqoba lokunqotshwa ngamalanga okucina omdlalo, uke waba seqenjini elinqobileyo eBrookline kodwa wanqotshwa ngesikhathi iqembu le-Europe lisenza “Isimanga eMedinah.”
Ephendula umbuzo abewubuziwe wokuthi owayengukhephutheni wabo ngo 1999 uBen Crenshaw wabatshelani abeqembu lakhe bengakabi lomdlalo omkhulu, uthe, “Ngikukhumbula konke akukhulumayo.”
“Silemidlalo engu 12 eqakathekileyo kusasa, kodwa kumele siqalise kuhle njengalokho esakwenza eBrookline lalokho esakwenza eMedinah.
Kodwa lokhu kuba nzima nxa abanye bengenzi kuhle, abadlali abalandelayo bacina besiba lomthwalo omkhulu.
Sihlele kuhle ukuthi sizadlala njani, kukhona esikutshintshileyo ngendlela esidlala ngayo, kusasa sifuna ukwenza into ezakwenza abantu bacabange ukuthi silamasalamusi.”
UThomas ukhangelelwe ukuthi akhokhele njengoba ezancintisana loRory Mcllroy emdlalweni omkhulu besekusithi abanye abe-Europe okugoqela uPaul Casey, uJustin Rose, uJon Rahm, uTommy Fleetwood lo-Ian Poulter labo badlale ngokulandelana kwabo.
UBjorn ukhulume ngabadlali beqembu lakhe abazabe bezimele bodwa wathi, “Ngicabanga ukuthi indlela engikhethe ngayo abadlali laba lendlela abazadlala ngayo izakwenza siphumelele.”
Sebefuqhele pambili ukubuya kwomkhumbi omutsha oweGermany
Umkhumbi omutsha owamabutho olwandle aweGermany, bekumele ubuye ngo2014 ukwenzela ukuthi bantshintshe imikhumbi empi yakudala, kodwa kayisabuyi kuze kufike umnyaka ozayo ngenxa yokungahlelekanga kwabo njalo lokudula kwawo, batsho njalo abaphumisa indaba.
Ukuthenga i"Rheinland-Pfalz," umkhumbi omutsha ozabe ukhokhela eminye imikhumbi yempi eyeBaden-Wuerttemberg, sekufuqelwe phambili kuze kuyefika umnyaka ka2019, ngokutsho kwephephandaba leDie Zeit, ikhuluma okwakhulunywa yisikhulumeli samasotsha.
Umkhumbi lo kwakumele ube usufikile ngo2014, kodwa uhlupho olwaba khona ngelokuwuletha ngapha, okwaphambanisa umsebenzi wethu.
Imikhumbi emine eyeBaden-Wuerttemberg eyathengwa ngamabutho olwandle ngo2007, azabuya ukuzontshintsha imikhumbi yamasotsha esindala eyeBremen.
Bathi izabe ilombhobho olamandla amakhulu, imibhobho eyokudubula indizamtshina njalo lamabhomba awokudubula eminye imikhumbi, njalo kuzabe kulokunye okutsha kwezempucuko okunjengeradar eyehlisiweyo, leinfrared kanye ngalokho okukwanisa ukuzwa nxa kuleminye imikhumbi ebuyayo.
Okunye okumangalisayo ngomkhumbi lo yikuthi uthatha isikhathi eside ukuthi ulungiswe - okutsho ukuthi umkhumbi lo uyabe usuhamba kweminyaka emibili ungalungiswanga.
Kodwa ngokuphuza kwabo ukuwuletha kuzabangela ukuthi umkhumbi lo - okumele utshengise ukuthi iGerman isilamandla - uyabe usundala ngesikhathi lapho ozabuya khona, yatsho njalo iDie Zeit.
Eminye imikhumbi yempi okuthiwa yiF125, ezakhulunywa ngazo kakhulu umnyaka owadlulayo, lapho amabutho olwandle aweGerman aze ayala ukumathenga njalo bawabisela eBlohm & Voss, endaweni abagcinela imikhumbi yabo eHamburg.
Kwaba ngokokuqala lokhu ukuthi amasotsha abisele umkhumbi kulabo abawulungisayo wona usufikile endaweni.
Babengakwazi okunengi ngezizatho zokubisela imikhumbi leyi, kodwa abaphumisi bendaba eGerman babona ukuthi kwakulezinto ezazingamanga kuhle, "kuhlelo lwamakhompiyutha emkhumbini leyi njalo imkhumbi yakhona yayingela imibhobho eminengi," okwayenza ukuthi imikhumbi leyi ingabi luncedo empini.
Ukuswelekala kwohlelo lwekhompiyutha emikhumbini leyi kwakuyinto eqakatheke kakhulu njengoba umkhumbi weBaden-Wuerttemberg uzabe ususetshenziswa ngabantu abafika 120, ihafu yabantu ababesebenza kumkhumbi eyeBremen.
Njalo kwabonakala ukuthi umkhumbi lo uyasinda kakhulu okwenza ukuthi ungasebenzi kuhle, njalo kuyavimbela ukuthi amabutho lawa olwandle angezelele okunye okutsha kumkhumbi lo.
Umkhumbi lo i"Rheinland-Pfalz," osinda amathani afika 7 000, wabonwa ukuthi wawusinda okuphindwe kabili ukwedlula imikhumbi eyayisetshenziswa yiGerman Empini Yezwe Yesibili.
Kungelani lokuthi imkhumbi leyi kayila imibhobho eminengi, imali efunakalayo emsebenzi womkhumbi omutsha - ukuhlanganisela ukuqeqetsha amasotsha - sokungeyinye indaba.
Kuthiwa imali esifunakala khathesi isinengi okokufika i€3.1 bhiliyoni($3.6 bhiliyoni) isuka ku€2.2 bhiliyoni.
Izinhlupho esezikhona ekuletheni imikhumbi leyi eyempi sokuyinto eseqakatheke kakhulu njengoba kuke kwaxwayiswa ukuthi amandla ebutho lolwandle lweGerman asephela.
Ekuqaleni komnyaka lo, uHans-Peter Bartels, umkhokheli wekhomithi ebona kwezokuvikeleka kwelizwe ephaliyamenti yaseGerman, uvumile ukuthi amabutho olwandle, "kasela imikhumbi eyokuhambisa empini."
Isiphathamandla lesi sithe indaba leyi kade ilokhu ihlupha ngoba imikhumbi eyakudala kayisasebenzi njalo akukaze kuthengwe eminye.
Wakhuluma etshengisa ukuhlupheka esithi, imikhumbi leyi yempi eyeBaden-Wuerttemberg, yayingasoze yaba ngeyamabutho olwandle.
AbeNational Trust bahlolisisa indlela umalulwane aphila ngayo
Ukuhlolisisa okutsha okwenzakala eScottish Highlands, kulungiselelwe ukuthi kuphumise egcekeni ukuthi umalulwane usebenzisa njani izinto ezimugombozeleyo ukuthi adinge ukudla.
Balethemba lokuthi okuzatholakala khonapho, kuzayenza ukuthi bazwisise ukuziphatha kwazo, njalo kuzanceda ukuthi bakwanise ukuzigcina kuhle.
Ukufunda lokhu okuzayenzwa ngamasayendisti aweNational Trust yeScotland, kuzalandela ukufundwa kwabomalulwane ojwayelekileyo, lezinye ezilezindlebe ezinde, lezinye okuthiwa ngamaDaubenton, eInverewe Gardens eseWester Ross.
Kuzafakwa izinto ezirekhodayo ezindaweni eziqakathekileyo, ukwenzela ukuthi zihlolisise indlela umalulwane lo oyenza ngayo izinto, kuhlobo lonke.
Amalunga eNHS labazinikeleyo, bazahlola indlela umalulwane lo ayenza ngayo izinto kodwa besebenzisa imitshina ebanjwa ngezandla.
Izingcitshi ezihlolisisa ngomdumo wezinto, zizarekhoda zihlolisisa indlela umalulwane lo abizana ngayo njalo ngokubona ukuthi umuhlobo ngamunye wenzani.
Kuzalungiswa imephu eyalapho ezihlala khona kanye lombiko ozancedisa ukuthi babone ukuthi ziphila njani endaweni ethile.
URob Dewar obona ngokugcinwa kuhle kwezomphakathi oweNTS, ulethemba lokuthi okuzaphuma ekuhloleni lokhu kuzancedisa ukuthi babone ukuthi yiphi indawo eqakathekileyo ephilwayo ngabomalulwane laba, njalo ngokuthi isetshenziswa njani labomalulwane bomunye umhlobo.
Ulwazi lolu luzanceda kuzwisiswe ukuthi kunceda ngani ukuthi endaweni yazo kube lotshani njalo lokugcina kuhle izihlahla besenzela omalulwane laba leminye imihlobo efananayo.
Ixhuku labomalulwane eScotland laseUK, seliyehlile kakhulu eminyakeni elikhulu edlulileyo.
Ziphanjaniswa ngokuyakha izakhiwo okwenzwayo, langokuphumeleliswa kwezindawo okwenze ukuthi izindawo lapho ezihlala khona kuphambaniswe, osokwenze ukuthi ziswele indawo yokuhlala.
Izinsimbi ezibhodhiswa ngumoya, kanye lamaphepha afakwe umuthi leminye imithi esetshenziswa ekwakheni kanye lokuhlaselwa labomangoye, ngokunye okuphambanisa omalulwane laba.
Umalulwane luyabona kodwa mbijana.
Ngenxa yokuthi zithanda ukuzingela ebusuku, zisebenzisa indlebe zazo kakhulu ukwedlula amehlo nxa sezifuna ukubamba ukudla.
Inyoni lezi ziyakwazi ukuthola lapho okulezibungwana khona ngokuvuma ukuqondiswa lapho njalo lokuthi zingatshayeleli nxa ziphapha.
AbeNTS abakhangelela izakhiwo ezifika 270, lezivande ezifika 38 njalo balendawo elamahekhitha afika 76 000, bayaqakathekisa omalulwane kakhulu.
Isiqeqetshe ingcitshi ezilitshumi ezihlala zihlolisisa indawo leyi, lokukhangelela lapho ezihlala khona njalo lokuzikhulula.
Inhlanganiso leyi eseScotland, isibeke indawo yokuqala njalo enikelwe ukuthi kuhlale omalulwane laba okuthiwa yiThreave eseDumfries leGalloway, indawo elemihlobo elitshumi yabomalulwane.
Umphathi wendawo leyi uDavid Thompson, wathi indawo leyi inhle kakhulu ukuthi umalulwane ahlale.
"Lapha eThreave, silendawo enkulu yabomalulwane," watsho njalo.
"Silezakhiwo ezindala, izihlahla zakudala lendawo ezinhle zokuthi zihlale.
Kodwa kulokunengi esingakabikwazi ngabomalulwane, yikho umsebenzi esiwenza lapha lezinye izindawo uzasincedisa ukuthi sizwisise ukuthi zifunani ukuthi ziphumelele."
Wakhuluma ukuthi kuhle kakhulu ukukhangela omalulwane ukuthi bangaphi endaweni leyi bengakaqalisi eminye imisebenzi ezakhiweni lezi, njengoba kungenzeka ukuthi singabhidliza singahlosanga indawo lapho ezizalela khona okungayenza ukuthi sibulale insikazi ezingu400 labantwana bazo, okungayenza ukuthi sibulale ixhuku lazo zonke.
Omalulwane bavikelwe, njalo kulicala ukubabulala, ukubaphambanisa lokubahlukuluza lokubhidliza indawo yazo yokuhlala.
UElisabeth Ferell, umphathi weBat Conservation Trust eyeScottish, ukhuthaze uzulu wonke ukuthi babambisane labo.
Wathi: "Sisaselokunengi esikufundayo ngabomalulwane laba, njalo kweminye imihlobo eminengi kasikwazi ukuthi amaxhuku azo aphila njani."
URonaldo uyala ukuthi ubambe iganyavu, njalo amagqwetha akhe aseyethesa icala imagazini eyeGerman
UChristiano Ronaldo uthe okwakhulunywayo ukuthi wabamba iganyavu, "yindaba zamanga," esithi abantu, "bafuna ukuziphumelelisa," ngokusebenzisa ibizo lakhe.
Amagqwetha akhe alungiselele ukuthi athonisise icala imagazini eyeGerman okuthiwa yiDer Spiegel eyaphumisa ukuqambelwa lokhu.
Umdlali lo owePortugal leJuventus, uthonisiswa icala lokubamba iganyavu owesifazane oweAmerica okuthiwa nguKathryn Mayorga endlini eyehotela eLas Vegas ngo2009.
Kuthiwa wabadala owesifazana lo imali efika $375 000, ukuthi engatsheli muntu ngendaba leyi, yatsho njalo iDer Spiegel, ngoLwesihlanu.
Sokudlule amahora athile imagazini leyi iphumise ngokwecala leli, ekhuluma kuvidiyo yezokuxhumana kulabo abamulandelayo abangu 142 miliyoni, uRonaldo oleminyaka engu33 ubatshele ukuthi, "yindaba zamanga."
"Hayi, hayi, hayi, hayi, hayi.
Abakukhulumileyo namuhla, yindaba zamanga," watsho njalo ekhangele ikhamera, umdlali lo osenqobe kahlanu kuBallon d'Or.
"Bafuna ukuziphumelelisa besebenzisa ibizo lami.
Yinto ejwayelekileyo leyi.
Bafuna ukuba lodumo ngokukhuluma ibizo lami, ngoba ngumsebenzi wabo.
Ngiyindoda ehlala ithokoza njalo konke kulungile," wangezelela lokhu umdlali lo ebobotheka.
Amagqwetha kaRonaldo bayalungiselela ukuthi bathonisise icala iDer Spiegel ngokukhuluma ngokwecala leli besithi yi"ndaba kade ingamelanga ikhulunywe ngoba bebengela qiniso, njalo kuyindaba eyimfihlo yomuntu," ngokutsho kweReuters.
Igqwetha lakhe uChristian Schertz, uthe umdlali lo kumele abhadalwe ngenxa yokuthi, "baphambanise ubuntu bakhe, ngoba icala leli yinto enkulu kakhulu, njengoba kuyinto kade iphambanisa amalungelo abantu iminyaka edlulileyo."
Indaba leyi kuthiwa yenzakala ngoJune 2009, endlini esehoteleni okuthiwa yiPalms Hotel and Casino eseLas Vegas.
Ngemva kokubonana kwelinye ibhawa, uRonaldo loMayorga kuthiwa babuyela bonke endlini eyomdlali lo esehoteleni lapho okuthiwa khona wabamba iganyavu owesifazana lo ngangapho okuphuma khona ngedoti, ngokutsho kwamaphepha aseClark County District Court eseNevada.
UMayorga uthi, uRonaldo wathethelela kakhulu eguqe ngamadolo ngemva kwesenzakalo lesi, wabesemtshela ukuthi wayeyi, "99 phesenti," "umuntu olungileyo," ophambaniswe yi"pecenti eyodwa."
Amaphepha lawa athi, uRonaldo wavuma ukuthi babehlangane kwezemancansini bevumelene.
UMayorga wathi, wahamba emapholiseni njalo babemthatha imifanekiso yokulimala kwakhe esibhedlela, kodwa bavumelana ukuthi abadalwe imali bengahambanga emthethwandaba ngenxa yokuthi, "wayesesaba ukuthi angaphindezelwa," njalo wayesesaba "ukuyangiswa phambili kwabantu."
Owesifazana lo oleminyaka engu34, uthe usefuna ukuntshintsha isivumelwano abasenzayo ngoba okwayenzakalayo kulokhu kumhlukuluza kakhulu.
Ngesikhathi uRonaldo eqambelwa icala leli, wayephakathi kokuntshintsha iqembu leManchester United esesiyadlalela iqembu leReal Madrid njalo kuhlobo leli wabesesiya dlalela eItaly iqembu elithiwa yiJuve bemthembise ukuthi bazambhadala i€100 miliyoni.
IBrexit: I-UK 'ingahlala izisola kokuphela' ngokulahlekelwa ngabalungisa izimota
I-UK 'ingahlala kokuphela izisola' nxa ingalahlekelwa yisikhundla sayo njengenkokheli ekulungiseni izimota emhlabeni wonke kulandela iBrexit, kwatsho uNobhala weBhizimisi uGreg Clark.
Wengezelela ukuthi "kwakukhathaza" ukuthi iToyota UK yayitshele iBBC ukuthi nxa iBritain ingaphuma ku-EU ingathengisanga lutho kwakuzake kwehlise inani lokulungiswayo efekithali yayo eBurnaston, duzane leDerby.
"Sifuna ukuthengiselana," kwatsho uMnumzane Clarke.
AbeJapan abalungisa izimota bathi okubangelwa yikuphuziswa kwezinto emingceleni yelizwe nxa kungenzeka kungabi lezinto ezithengiselwanayo eBrexit kungatsho ukulahlekelwa yimisebenzi.
Ifekithali yaseBurnaston - elungisa iToyota Auris le-Avensis - yalungisa izimota eziphose zibe ngu-150 000 nyakenye futhi phakathi kwazo i-90% zathengiselwa kwamanye amazwe e-European Union.
"Umbono wami ngowokuthi nxa iBritain ingaphuma ku-EU ekupheleni kukaMbimbitho sizabona ukulungiswa kusima efekithali yethu," kwatsho uMarvin Cooke, umphathi okhekhelayo weToyota eBurnaston.
Abanye abalungisa izimota e-UK labo bakhulume ngokwesabela ukuphuma ku-EU kungela sivumelwano ngokuthi ukuthengiselana kuchatshwa imingcele yelizwe kuzahamba njani, okugoqela iHonda, iBMW leJaguar Land Rover.
IBMW, ngokwesibonelo ithi izavala ifekithali yayo yeMini ese-Oxford okwenyanga eyodwa kulandela iBrexit.
Okukhathazekwe ngakho kakhulu kuphathelane lalokho abalungisa izimota abakuthi yibunzima obungavela emzileni wokulungiswa kwezinto nxa kungenzeka ukuthi akulaselalutho oluthengiswayo eBrexit.
IToyota ilungisa izinto ngendlela yokuthi "zifika nje ngesikhathi," lezingxenye zezimota eziyabe zilungiswa zifika ngemva kwemizuzu engu-37 ngaminye zivela kwabalungisayo abase-UK laku-EU.
Nxa i-UK ingaphuma ku-EU ngo-29 Mbimbitho ingathengisanga lutho, kungaba lokuphambaniseka emngceleni welizwe njalo i-indastiri ithi kungabangela ukuphuza lokuswelakala kwezingxenye.
Kungaba nzima ukuba iToyota ibe lezingxenye ezinganela okosuku olulodwa efekithali yayo eseDerbyshire, yatsho njalo inkampani, ngakho ukulungisa kuyabe kuzamiswa.
UMnumzane Clark wathi icebo leChequers likaTheresa May ngobuhlobo besikhathi esizayo le-EU "lilungiselelwe lalingana nje ukubalekela ukuphuziswa lokho emingceleni yelizwe."
"Kumele sithengiselane. Sifuna ukuthengiselana okuhle kakhulu okuzasivumela njengoba ngisitsho hatshi kuphela ukuphumelela kwakhathesi esingakukholisa kodzwa ukuze lathi silisebenzise ithuba leli," watshela uhlelo lweToday kuBBC Radio 4.
"Ubufakazi obungaveli nje kuToyota kodwa kwabanye abalungisayo ngobokuthi kumele senelise ngokupheleleyo ukuqhubeka ngalokho obekuyikulungisa okuqhubekayo okuphemelelayo."
IToyota kayenelisanga ukutsho ukuthi ukulungisa kwakuzathatha isikhathi eside kangakanani kumisiwe, kodwa nxa kungathatha isikhathi, waxwayisa ukuthi ezinye izindleko zokwengezelela zazizakwenza ukuthi ifekithali ingenelisi ukuncintisana kuhle lamanye njalo kucine ngokulahlekelwa yimisebenzi.
UPeter Tsouvallaris, osesebenzele eBurnastone okweminyaka engu-24 njalo enguye ohlanganisa okwe-Unite efekithali, wathi amalunga akhe aqhubeka ekhathazeka kakhulu: "Ngokolwazi lwami ngalokho engikubonileyo nxa imisebenzi le ingaphela nje kayiphindi itholakale futhi.
Isikhulumeli sikahulumende sathi: "Sesilecebo eliqondileyo njalo elisebenzayo ngodaba lobuhlobo bethu besikhathi esizayo le-EU."
White House ithi umhlangano kaTrump loRosenstein ungaphinda uphuze futhi ukwenziwa
NgeSonto, iWhite House ithe umhlangano kaDonald Trump lomsekeli wegqwetha elikhulu ozaphatha indaba eqakathekileyo kakhulu “ungafuqelwa emuva ngeviki eyodwa” njengoba ukungazwanani ekukhethweni kukaBrett Kavanaugh ukuthi abe ngoweSupreme Court kulokhu kuqhubekela phambili.
URosenstein ngumaqhuzu okhangela umsebenzi owenziwa nguRobert Mueller, ohlolisisa indaba yokungenela kweRussia kwezokhetho, ukusebenzelana kukaTrump leRussia kanye lokuhlola ukuthi kambe umongameli engabe ewasebenzisa kubi yini amandla akhe.
Sokulezinyanga ezinengi kulensindabaphenduli eWashington yokuthi kungenzakala yini ukuthi uTrump axotshe umsekeli wegqwetha elikhulu umsebenzi lokho besekuthathela uMueller inkululeko kodwa akula olempendulo.
Ekuqaliseni kwalinyanga, iNew York Times ibike ukuthi uRosenstein wake wakhuluma ngokusebenzisa umtshina wokurekhoda ukuze arekhode ingxoxo ayezakuba lazo loTrump lokuthi wayefuna ukuthi umongameli akhitshwe esikhundleni ngesikhathi sokulungisiswa umthetho okwesi-25.
URosenstein uthe akulanto enjalo ayaziyo.
Kodwa ngoMvulo odlulileyo ubeseWhite House, lanxa imibiko isithi uthe usefuna ukutshiya umsebenzi.
Kodwa kuthiwa umhlangano lo uzakuba ngoLwesine ngoba ngalesosikhathi uTrump ubesemhlanganweni we-United Nations eNew York.
UTrump uthe “engakhetha ukungaxotshi” uRosenstein umsebenzi kodwa umhlangano umisiwe ukuze kungaphambanisi umsebenzi wokwahlulela okumele wenziwe yiSenate ekumangangalelweni kuka-Kavanaugh ngomunye owesifazana othe wamhlukuluza kwezemacansini, uDokotela uChristine Blasey Ford lomangalelwayo bakhulume abakwaziyo ngendaba le.
NgoLwesihlanu, uTrump wanika abe FBI iviki eyodwa ukuthi bahlolisise ukumangalelwa kuka-Kavanaugh, ikanti lokho kwabuyisela emuva ukhetho okwakumele lwenziwe yiSenate yonke.
Umabhalani kaTrump obona ngezokukhitshwa kwemibiko uSarah Sanders uxoxe labe-Fox News ngeSonto.
Ekhuluma ngomhlangano kaRosenstein, uthe: “Akukamiswa ilanga lokuthi umhlangano lowo uzakuba nini, kungenzakala ube kuyonale iviki, kodwa kungenzeka ukuthi ufuqelwe emuva ngeviki eyodwa njengoba sibona ukuthi kulezinto ezenzakalayo esupreme court.
Kodwa sizabona ukuthi kuzahamba njani futhi ngihlala ngitshela abezindaba okuyabe kusenzakala.”
Kodwa ezinye intathelizindaba azivumelani lamazwi akhe: USanders wacina ukukhipha imibiko evela eWhite House mhlaka-10 September.
Owenzisa uhlelo lolu uChris Wallace ubuze ukuthi kungani kunjalo.
USanders uthe okwenza kube njalo ayisikho ukuthi kabathandi onozindaba beTV “abathanda ukubukwa,” lanxa ethe: “Angeke ngiphike ukuthi bayakuthanda sibili ukubukwa.”
Wasesithi kungenzakala ukuthi esikhathini esizayo kube lamathuba amanengana okuthi uTrump azikhulumele labezindaba.
Uphinde wathi, “Umongameli uhlala esiba lesikhathi Semibuzo leZimpendulo ukwedlula loba nguphi owayesesikhundleni yena engakangeni,” kodwa kazange anike ubufakazi balokho: “Sikukhangelile konke lokho.”
Imibiko izaqhubeka iphuma, uSanders uthe kodwa “nxa abezindaba bengathola ithuba lokubuza umongameli we-United States ngokwakhe imibuzo abalayo, lokho kuyabe kungcono kakhulu ukwedlula ukukhuluma lami.
Siyazama ukwenza njalo izikhathi ezinengi futhi likubonile kusenzakala emavikini asanda kudlula njalo lokho kuzangena endaweni yokuthi abezindaba bakhulume lomongameli we-United States.”
UTrump wandise ukuphendula imibuzo nxa esesuka eWhite House kumbe nxa elemihlangano engenwa ngabanengi lalapho elabezindaba ngesikhathi elabahlonitshwa bakwamanye amazwe.
Kodwa kukalutshwane ukuthi axoxe labezindaba eyedwa.
Njalo isizathu salokhu kungenzakala sicace kakhulu ngesikhathi eseNew York kuyonale iviki, ubesenza izinto ezingazwisisekiyo futhi ezitshengisa ukuthi kabahloniphi abezindaba akade begcwele lapho.
Umabhalani wezempilakahle ubhalele izizalwane ze-EU ezisebenzela i-NHS eScotland ngokuthi izinto zingahamba njani nxa iBritain ingaphuma ku-European Union
Umabhalani wezempilakahle usebhalele izizalwane ze-EU ezisebenzela i-NHS eScotland esithi ilizwe labo liyabonga kakhulu ngomsebenzi abawenzayo lokuthi bafisa baqhubeke ngomsebenzi wabo langemva kokuphuma kweBritain ku-EU.
UJean Freeman MSP uthumele incwadi le njengoba sekusele izinyanga ezingaphansi kweziyisithupha ukuthi i-UK iphume ku-European Union.
Uhulumende weScotland uvumile ukuthi uzabhadalela izincwadi zezizalwane ze-EU ezisebenzela uhulumende esezikwazi ukuthi kuzahamba njani ngazo ngenxa yotshintsho oselukhona.
Encwadini ayibhalileyo, uNkosikazi Freeman uthe: "Ngesikhathi sehlobo, ukukhulumisana phakathi kwe-UK le-EU ngendaba le akuzange kume futhi isinqumo sonke esisilindeleyo sizakwenziwa ngekwindla.
Kodwa lohulumende we-UK ulokhu esebenza nzima ukuze azilungiselele nxa kungenzakala ukuthi izinto zingakambi ngendlela ayifisayo.
Ngiyakwazi ukuthi yisikhathi esinzima kakhulu kini lonke.
Yikho bengifisa ukuthi ngiphinde engake ngalitshela khona, ngiyawuqakathekisa kakhulu umsebenzi owenziwa yini lonke, kungelani lokuthi uvela kuliphi ilizwe.
Abantu abanengi abavela emazweni aku-EU lakwamanye amazwe, bazingcitshi emsebenzini wabo futhi ulwazi abalalo luwuthuthukise kakhulu umsebenzi wethu kwezempilakahle, kwanceda lezigulane lomphakathi esiwusebenzelayo.
Lingakhohlwa ukuthi eScotland kukini futhi siyafisa kakhulu ukuthi lihlale lapha."
UChristion Abercrombie Ugijinyiswe Ukuyelatshwa Ngemva Kokulimala Ikhanda
UChristion Abercrombie odlalela iTennessee State Tigers, ugijinyiswe ukuyelatshwa ngemva kokulimala ikhanda, emdlaleni abawunqotshwayo 31-27 ngoMgqibelo, leVanderbilt Commodores, njengokutshiwo nguMike Organ oweTennessee.
Umqeqetshi wabo omkhulu oweTennessee State uRod Reed, watshela abaphumisi bendaba ukuthi ulimele sebefuna ukuthi baphumule kuhlandla lokuqala.
"Ubuye duzane lathi, wabesesiwa," watsho njalo uReed.
Abaqeqetshi labezempilakahle baqalise ukwelapha uAbercrombie ngokumnika umoya omncedayo ukuthi aphefumule kuhle bengakamuthwali besiya laye ngemva kwabantu, ukuthi babone ngenxa yani ewile.
Isiphathi esevele eTennessee State, sitshele uChris Harris oweWSMV eNashville eseTennessee ukuthi, uAbercrombie wayesephumile esejari eseVanderbilt Medical Center.
UHarris uqhubeke esithi, "asikabikwazi ukuthi kuyini/lokuthi ulimele okunganani," njalo abeTennessee bazama ukuthi bazwisise ukuthi walimala nini.
UAbercrombie ogqoka okubomvu njalo osemnyakeni wakhe wesibili wezifundo, usemdlalweni yakhe yokuqala eTennessee ngemva kokusuka eIllinois.
Wayevimbele abantu ababethwele ibhora ukuthi bamudlule ngokubajikela phansi kahlanu kumudlalo lo ngoMgqibelo engakaphumi emdlalweni wakhona, okumufikise ku18 ekuvimbeni okunjalo kumidlalo yakhe.
Abazathenga izakhiwo kumbe umhlabathi e-UK bona bekwamanye amazwe bazabhadaliswa umthelo ophezulu ukwedlula abanye
UTroy uthe abantu abazathenga izakhiwo e-UK bona bekwamanye amazwe bazabhadaliswa umthelo ophezulu ukwedlula abanye ukuze bathole amaphepha asemthethweni atshengisa ukuthi isakhiwo leso sokungesabo, besekusithi imali leyo incedise labo abangelazindawo zokuhlala
Lokhu kwenziwa ukuze icebo likaCorbyn lokuzama ukuthi avotelwe ngabasakhulayo lingasebenzi
Umthelo lo uzababhadalwa yilabo abangabhadaliyo umthelo e-UK
AbeTreasury bakhangelele ukuthola imali engafika £120 miliyoni ngomnyaka futhi imali le izancedisa abantu abangelazindlu zokuhlala
Lamuhla uTheresa May uzakwenza isaziso sokuthi abantu abahlala kwelinye ilizwe kodwa abafuna ukuthenga izakhiwo e-UK bazabhadaliswa umthelo ophezulu ukuze bathole amaphepha asemthethweni atshengisa ukuthi isakhiwo leso sokungesabo, besekusithi imali leyo isetshenziswe ekuncedeni abantu abangelazindawo zokuhlala.
Abanengi bathi lokhu kwenzelwe ukuthi icebo likaJeremy Corbyn lokuzama ukuvotelwa ngabasakhulayo lingasebenzi, ngoba uthembise abantu ukuthi bazakwenelisa ukuthenga izindlu ezingaduliyo futhi ilihlo lakhe ulithe nhlo kwabathola imali enengi.
Umthelo lo uzabhadalwa yilabo abangabhadaliyo umthelo kanye lamakhampani angabhadaliyo umthelo e-UK, besekusithi imali leyo isekele uhlelo lukahulumende lokuzama ukuqeda uhlupho lwezindawo zokuhlala.
Kukhangelelwe ukuthi imali ezabhadalwa phezu kweyomthelo, laleyo eyaqalisa ukubhadalwa eminyakeni emibili esanda kudlula ebhadalwa nxa umuntu ethenge indlu eyake yahlala abanye kumbe izindlu ezithengwa ukuze umuntu afake amaloja ingaba ngamaphesenti amathathu.
AbeTreasury bacabangela ukuthi lokhu kungenza kutholakale imali engange-£120 miliyoni ngomnyaka.
Kucatshangelwa ukuthi amaphesenti angu-13 ezakhiwo ezintsha eziseLondon athengwa ngabantu abangahlali e-UK, lokhu kwenza ukuthi izakhiwo lezi zidule kakhulu njalo labantu abathenga izakhiwo okokuqala kubathwalisa nzima ukwenza njalo.
Indawo ezinengi ezinothileyo elizweni leli, ikakhulu esigodlweni, “seziyizindlu ngebizo” ngoba zathengwa ngabantu bakwamanye amazwe futhi bahlala isikhathi eside bephandle kwelizwe leli.
Umthetho lo omutsha ufakwe kungelamaviki amangaki uBoris Johnson ethe kwehliswe umthelo obhadalwayo ukuze abanengi abasakhulayo labo benelise ukuthenga izindlu okwakuqala ngqa.
Usole amakhampani amakhulu okwakha ngokugcina intengo yezakhiwo iphezulu langokuba lomhlabathi omnengi kodwa ongasetshenziswayo, wasecela uNkosikazi May ukuthi akhohlwe ngenani lezindlu abantu abenelisa ukuzithenga ukuze iBritain iqede “uhlupho oluyangisayo lokuswelakala kwendawo zokuhlala.”
Umnumzana Corbyn ukhulume ngezindlu ezibukekayo ezitshiyeneyo afuna ukuzibona zisakhiwa, langokubhadalwa kwemali ngabantu abasebenzisa izindlu lokuqeda ukuxotshwa kwabantu ezindlini “kungelacala”abalenzileyo.
Ufuna ukunika lamakhansili imvumo yokwakha izindlu.
UNkosikazi May uthe: “Ngomnyaka ophelileyo ngathembisa ukuthi ngizasebenzisa isikhathi lesi ukuze ngigcwalise inhloso yeBritain, eyokuthi impilo yesizukulwane ngasinye iqhubeke isiba ngcono.
Njalo lokho kugoqela ukulungisa uhlupho olukhulu esilalo endabeni yezindlu zokuhlala.
IBritain izahlala ibamukela ngezandla zombili abantu abafuna ukuhlala lapha, basebenze lapha njalo bakholise impilo beselizweni lethu.
Kodwa kuzaba nzima ebantwini abangahlali e-UK kumbe abalamakhampani lapha kodwa bona bengekho lapha ukuthi bathenge izindlu, kumele kube lomehluko phakathi kwabantu beBritain abasebenza nzima labakwamanye amazwe.
Abantu abanengi sebalahla ithemba lokuthi ngelinye ilanga labo bazake babe lezindlu ezibiza bona sibili, kuyadanisa ukuthi uhlupho lokuswela indawo yokuhlala lusasekhatshana ukuthi luphele.”
UJack Ross: 'Isifiso sami esikhulu ngesokuba ngumqeqetshi weScotland’'
Umqeqetshi weSunderland uJack Ross uthe “isifiso esikhulu”alaso ngesokuba ngumqeqetshi weScotland ngelinye ilanga.
Isizalwane lesi seScotland esileminyaka engu-42 siyathokoza ngoba sincede iqembu eliseNyakatho-Mpumalanga emidlalweni yalo, khathesi lisendaweni yesithathu ku-League One futhi lifuna imklomelo emithathu kuphela ukuthi libe ngelokuqala.
Uqalise ukuqeqetsha iqembu elisebenzisa iStadium of Light khathesi nje, ngemva kokuncedisa iqembu le St Mirren ukuthi liphinde lidlale kuScottish Premiership emidlalweni esanda kuphela.
"Ngangikufisa kakhulu ukudlalela ilizwe lami.
Kodwa ngalidlalela kanye kuphela ngikuqembu-B kwaphelela lapho!,” lokhu yikho uRoss akutshele i-BBC Scotland’s Sportsound.
"Ngakhula ngibukela imidlalo yeScotland eHampden eminengi kakhulu ngilobaba futhi lokhu yikho okungenza ngiqhubeke ngilesifiso lesi.
Kodwa lokho kuzakwenzakala kuphela, nxa ngingaphumelela ukuqeqetsha kuhle iqembu lami.”
Abake baqeqetsha iqembu leSunderland uRoss engakaphiwa umsebenzi lo bagoqela uDick Advocaat, uDavid Moyes, uSam Allardyce, uMartin O’Neill, uRoy Keane, uGus Poyet loPaulo Di Canio.
Wake waba ngumqeqetshi weqembu le-Alloa Athletic, futhi uthe lanxa khathesi eqeqetsha iqembu elidume kangaka lelake laqeqetshwa zingcitshi ezedlula yena kesabi lutho, kazange avume ngesikhathi iqembu leBarnsley lele-Ipswich Town lifuna ukumqhatsha.
"Khathesi okuzangenza ngitsho sibili ukuthi ngiphumelele, yikuphendula umbuzo othi ‘ngizalibuyisela yini iqembu leli kuPremier League?'
Abadlali esilabo, lezinto esilazo enkundleni yethu kutshengisa ukuthi iqembu leli kumele libe kuPremier League,” ungezelele amazwi lawo.
“Ngumqanso ozwayo ukuthi lokho kwenzakale, kodwa nxa ngingenelisa ukubuyisela iqembu lami lapho elalikhona, ngingatsho sibili ukuthi ngiyabe ngisebenzile.”
URoss uleminyaka emithathu kuphela engumqeqetshi, wake wancedisa umqeqetshi weDumbarton waphinda wasebenza labaqeqetshi be-Hearts okwezinyanga ezingu-15.
Esuka lapho wancedisa i-Alloa ukuthi ingakhitshwa kupremiership wayenza yaqansa yayakuba ngeyesithathu, langesikhathi sekusele kancane ukuthi iSt Mirren iphume kupremiership wayincedisa yaze yanqoba kuChampionship emidlalweni eyalandelayo.
URoss uthe uzizwa ehlalisekile khathesi ukwedlula ngesikhathi edlalela iqembu leClyde, leHartlepool, leFalkirk leSt Mirren leleHamilton Academical.
Ekhumbula ngesikhathi sokumele aqalise ukuqeqetsha i-Alloa uthe, “Ngicabanga ukuthi lesi kwakuyisinqumo esinzima kakhulu okwakumele ngisenze.”
“Ngangikholwa sibili ukuthi ngingenza ngcono ekubeni ngumqeqetshi ukwedlula ukuba ngumdlali.
Ngiyakwazi ukuthi engikutshoyo akuzwisiseki kwabanye ngoba ngangidlala kuhle, ngiziphilela kuhle ngemali engangiyithola njalo zinengi izinto engangizikholisa.
Kodwa ukuba ngumdlali kunzima.
Kulezinto ezinengi okumele uzenze iviki ngayinye.
Liqiniso ukuthi lokhe kulezinto ezinengi ezingikhathazayo emsebenzini lo lokumele ngizenze iviki ngayinye kodwa ngiyakukholisa ukuba ngumqeqetshi.
Ngangilesifiso sokuba ngumqeqetshi kusukela kudala futhi sengingumqeqetshi khathesi, ngizizwa ngihlalisekile njalo ngichelesile selokhu ngaba ngumuntu omdala.”

Umbiko lo wethuse abanengi ngoba kucatshangelwa ukuthi bathumelana imifanekiso lokunye okutshengisa abantu besiya emacansini
Inani labantwana abangamaphesenti angu-20 lithe bale-akhawunti “eyaziwayo” abayitshengisa abazali babo
Umtwana oyedwa kwabahlanu - abanye bakhona abaleminyaka engu-11 bavula ama-akhawunti abawasebenzisa kwezokuxhumana njalo lokhu bakufihlela abantu abadala.
Ukuhlola okwenziwe ebantwaneni abangu-20 000 abasesekhondari kuveze ukuthi inani lama-akhawunti amanga (“fake Insta”) liqansa ngendlela emangalisayo-kukhulunywa nge-Instagram esetshenziswa kwezokuxhumana lokuthumelana imifanekiso.
Umbiko lo wethuse abanengi ngoba kucatshangelwa ukuthi bathumelana imifanekiso lokunye okutshengisa abantu besiya emacansini.
Inani labantwana abangamaphesenti angu-20 lithe bale-akhawunti ecacayo “eyaziwayo” futhi yiyo abayitshengisa abazali babo, kodwa baphinda babe lamanye agcinwa eyimfihlo.
Omunye umama otshayisane le-akhawunti eyimfihlo yendodakazi yakhe eleminyaka engu-13 ubone umlayezo obhalwe ngomunye osakhulayo obetshela abanye ukuthi “ngibambani iganyavu.”
Ukuhlolisisa okwenziwe yi-Digital Awareness UK kanye le Headmasters” and Headmistresses Conference (HMC) yezikolo ezizimele zodwa, kutshengise ukuthi amaphesenti angu-40 abantwana abaleminyaka engu-11 kusiya ku-18 balama-akhawunti amabili, ikanti oyedwa kwababili uthe ulama-akhawunti abawagcina eyimfihlo.
Isikhulu se-HMC uMike Buchanan uthe: “Kuyethusa ukuthi abasakhulayo abanengi bayathatheka ngokuvula ama-akhawunti ezokuxhumana abawagcina eyimfihlo kubazali babo lakubabalisi.”

Ekhuluma esemhlanganweni we-UN General Assembly, uMphathintambo obona ngokwenzakala phandle kwelizwe uWalid al-Moualem uphinde watshela iziphepheli ezabaleka kweleSyria ukuthi ziphenduke ekhaya, lanxa impi eselizweni leli isileminyaka engu-8.
UMoualem ophinda abe ngumsekeli ka-prime minister, uthe amabutho lawa avela phandle kwelizwe aseSyria ngokungekho emthethweni, esithi azoqeda omalwabecatsha njalo “azajeziswa ngenxa yalokho akwenzileyo."
"Kumele baphume baphele ngokuphangisa kungela kubalabalisa,” ukhulume lokhu esemhlanganweni lo.
UMoualem uthe “impi yokuqeda omalwabecatsha isizaphela” eSyria, lapho osekufe khona abantu abedlula 360 000 kusukela ngo-2011 ikanti amamiliyoni amanengi asala engasela zindlu zawo.
Uthe iDamascus izaqhubeka “isilwa empini le engcwele iSyria yonke” ize isale ingela abalwabecatsha kanye “laloba ngobani abaselizweni leli ngokungekho emthethweni."
I-United States ilamasotsha angafika 2 000 eSyria futhi inhloso yawo enkulu ngeyokuqeqetsha lokucebisa amabutho angamaKurdish lamaArabhu angamaSyria aphikisana loMongameli uBashar al-Assad.
IFrance yona ilamabutho edlula 1 000 elizweni leli eselitshabalaliswe yimpi.
Endabeni yeziphepheli, uMoualem uthe izimo zilungile ukuthi baphenduke ekhaya wasesola “amanye amazwe asentshonalanga” alokhu “efafaza amanga enza abantu besabe” ukucabanga ngokubuyela elizweni leli.
Uthe, “Sesicele amazwe amanengi lenhlanganiso ezincedisa abantu ukuthi basincedise ukuthi abantu laba basuke elizweni lethu.”
“Bathatha indaba elokwenza lenhlalakahle yabantu bayenze indaba yezombusazwe.”
I-United States le-European Union ithe akulamali ezaphuma kuthiwa ngeyokuncedisa ukwakha eSyria nxa kungela sivumelwano phakathi kuka-Assad leqembu eliphikisayo esokuthi impi yabo isiphelile.
Abalezikhundla ku-UN bathe isivumelwano esisanda kuba khona phakathi kweRussia leTurkey esokuthi bangezelele amabutho e-Idlib okuyindawo elabanengi abalwisana lohulumende sesibavulele elinye ithuba lokuthi bakhulumisane ngezombusazwe.
Isivumelwano seRussia le-Turkey sincede ukuthi kungahlaselwa izizalwane zeSyria ezihlala esigabeni esisekelwa yiRussia, isigaba lesi silabantu abangamamiliyoni amathathu.
UMoualem uthe isivumelwano leso “silamalanga abekiweyo” futhi ulethemba lokuthi ibutho lizahlasela amaqembu abahlamuki okugoqela labeNusra Front okukhanya basebenza le-Al-Qaeda, okumele “baqedwe."
Othunywe yi-UN uStaffan de Mistura ulethemba lokuthi bazakuba lomhlangano wabo wakuqala olekhomithi entsha elabantu abamele uhulumende labeqembu eliphikisayo ukuze kubhalwe umthetho welizwe ozasebenza eSyria nxa impi isiphelile futhi kuvulwe lethuba lokwenza ukhetho.
UMoualem wenze kwacaca ukuthi ukungena kwalabo abamele uhulumende weSyria kukhomithi le kuzasebenza njani, uthe umsebenzi wekhomithi le uphelela “ekuhlolisiseni izinto ezibhalwe emthethweni welizwe okhona khathesi,” wasesithi akumelanga bangenele kwezinye izindaba.

U.S. Ijeziswe Kabuhlungu I-El Salvador Ngokusekela IChina, Khathesi Ayisafuni Lakuzwa
Abasezikhundleni bathi iDominican Republic lePanama ibesikwamukele okukhulunywe yiBeijing kodwa yasitshintsha ingqondo ngenxa yeWashington.
Umnumzana Trump waba lomhlangano omuhle loMongameli wePanama uJuan Carlos Varela ngoJune 2017 njalo wayelewotela ePanama kodwa abantu ayelabo kubhizimusi le baxotsha abaphathi behlanganiso kaTrump.
Abaphathintambo bakahulumende bacele ukuthi izizalwane ze-America ezisebenzela uhulumende ebezithunywe e-El Salvador, eDominican Republic lasePanama ziphenduke ukuze kuxoxwe “ngezinqumo ezisanda kwenziwa zokuthi bangavumelani leTaiwan,” la ngamazwi omkhulumeli wequla leli uHeather Nauert embikweni okhitshwe ekuqaliseni kwalinyanga.
Kodwa ilizwe okwathiwa lizajeziswa ngele-El Salvador kuphela, elathola uncedo oluvela e-America ngo-2017 lwezinto ezingabiza $140 miliyoni, ezazigoqela ezingasetshenziswa ukuhlola ukungena kwezidakamizwa, ukuthuthukisa ilizwe lokuncedisa kwezomnotho.
Isijeziso esasicatshangelwa sasigoqela ukuncitshwa uncedo lwemali lokuthi abanye abantu bancitshwe amaviza, futhi lokhu kwakuzaba buhlungu kakhulu elizweni leli eliseCentral America elilenani eliphezulu kakhulu labantu abangasebenziyo lababulalanayo.
Ngesikhathi umhlangano lo uqhubeka, abeNorth America labeCentral America bona batshovele umhlangano oqakathekileyo obekumele babe lawo emuva, bekumele kuxoxwe ngezokuvikeleka lezomnotho kusakhelwa emhlanganweni wanyakenye futhi kucatshangelwa ukuthi lokhu kuzanceda ukuthi abanengi bangabalekeli e-United States.
Kodwa phakathi kukaSeptember, abasezikhundleni eziphezulu bakwenza kwacaca ukuthi babefuna umhlangano lo wenziwe njalo lokho kwakuzatsho ukuthi i-El Salvador yayingasoze ijeziswe.
Iziphathimandla zithe umsekeli kaMongameli uMike Pence uzakhuluma emhlanganweni lo osuzakwenziwa phakathi kuka-October, lokhu kutshengisa ukuthi lo ngumhlangano oqakathekileyo sibili okumele wenziwe.
Kusenjalo, izithunywa ze-America ezintathu zithe nyelele zabuyela e-El Salvador, ePanama, laseDominican Republic njalo akula mlayezo omutsha kumbe isijeziso esivela eWashington.
Umkhulumeli kamnumzana Bolton oseWhite House walile ukukhuluma ngendaba le, lanxa izizalwane ezintathu ze-America ezisesikhundleni, ezigoqela ezimbili ezisebenzela uhulumende zivumile ukuxoxa ngezinqumo ezenziweyo kodwa zacela ukuthi amabizo azo angaqanjwa.
Abakukhulumileyo bekuvumelana lokukhulunywe ngomunye ozimele yedwa kodwa osebenza labahleli bomhlangano lo njalo laye ucele ukuthi ibizo lakhe lingaqanjwa.

Ngilethemba lokuthi, khathesi sesingaya phambili sifake emuva imidlalo edlulileyo ukwenzela ukuthi siphumelele."
Abesifazana bakhathazekile ngokonga imali ezabagcina sebegugile
Ukuhlola okwenziweyo kutshengise ukuthi lanxa abanengi bekwazi ukuthi bafuna ukunakekelwa njani, balutshwana kakhulu abaxoxa lemuli zabo ngalokho.
Phose ingxenye eyodwa ebantwini abaxoxe le-Nationwide ithe bebexoxa lomuntu abatshade laye ngendaba yemali ezabagcina okwesikhathi eside.
Kodwa abantu abangamaphesenti angu-10 kuphela bathe bayake baxoxe ngakho labantwababo.
"Abantu bafuna ukugcinwa lilunga lemuli, kodwa akula abakwenzayo ukuze baxoxe labo ngalokhu,” la ngamazwi kaHolly Snyder, umsekeli kamongameli weNationwide ibhizimusi ye-insurance.
Ungaqalisela lapha.
Xoxa lomkakho kanye labantwabakho: Kuba nzima ukuthi imuli yakho ikunakekele kuhle nxa ungazange uhlele kuseselisikhathi ukuthi ufuna izinto zihambe njani.
Xoxa lokucebisayo lilemuli yakho ngokuthi uzabe ungaphi lokuthi uzanakekelwa njani, ngoba izinqumo lezi zingakwenza ubone ukuthi kuzadingeka imali engakanani.
Xoxa lomunye futhi okucebisa kwezezimali: Yena uzakunceda ubone ukuthi ungayibhadala njani imali efunakalayo.
Zinengi indlela ongabhadala ngazo futhi zigoqela i-insurance yokunakekelwa okwesikhathi eside, eyokukhipha imali ezasetshenziswa kungaba lokunye okumele kubhadalelwe, kumbe ukubhadala ngenotho olayo - kumele ube lemali kuphela.

Ukuzamazama komhlaba lezikhukhula e-Indonesia
Iziphathamandla zithi abantu abangafika 384 bafile ngemva kokuzamazama komhlaba lezikhukhula ezibe khona edolobheni lePalu, e-Indonesia ngoLwesihlanu, ikanti kukhangelelwe ukuthi inani lelo lizaqhubeka liqansa.
Ezokukhulumisana azisebenzi okwakhathesi, yikho leziphathamandla ezincedisayo azikezwa lutho oluvela esiqintini seDonggala, esenyakatho kwePalu duze lalapho okube lokuzamazama komhlaba okuyi-7.5.
Ngemva komonakalo lo abantu abangu-16 000 basusiwe ePalu.
Nanku esikwaziyo ngePalu langeDonggala esesihlengeni seSulawesi:

IDonggala iyisiqinti esingaphansi kwesabelo, njalo yayilabantu abangafika 299 200 ngo-2017.

Nanku umbiko otshengisa ukuzamazazama komhlaba okukhulu lezikhukhula okube khona eminyakeni esanda kudlula:
Ngo-2004: Ukuzamazama okwenzakala entshonalanga kwesabelo se-Indonesia okuthiwa yi-Aceh enyakatho kweSumatra mhlaka 26 Dec kwabangela isikhukhula esahlasela amazwe angu-14, kwafa abantu abangu-226,000 emhlubulweni we-Indian Ocean, abedlula ingxenye yenani leli ngabe-Aceh.
Ngo-2005: Ukuzamazama okulamandla kwenzakala izikhathi ezinengi entshonalanga kweSumatra ekupheleni kukaMarch lasekuqaliseni kuka-April.
Kwafa amakhulu abantu eSihlengeni seNias, duze letheku leSumatra.
Ngo-2006: Ukuzamazama kwe-6.8 kwahlasela eningizimu yeJava, eyisihlenge se-Indonesia esilabantu abanengi ukwedlula ezinye, lokho kwabangela isikhukhula esaqonda ethekwini eliseningizimu, esabulala abantu abangafika 700.
Ngo-2009: Ukuzamazama kwe-7.6 kwahlasela duze kwedolobho le-Padang, okulidobho elikhulu lesabelo seWest Sumatra.
Kwafa abantu abedlula 1 100.
Ngo-2010: Ukuzamazama kwe 7.5 kwahlasela izihlenge zeMentawai, duze leSumatra lokho kwabangela isikhukhula esasiphakeme okwamamitha angu-10 esatshabalalisa imizi eminengi sabulala labantu abangaba ngu-300.
Ngo-2016: Ukuzamazama kwahlasela ePidie Jaya isiqinti esise-Aceh, futhi lokho kwabangela umonakalo lokwesaba ebantwini sebekhumbula ukuzamazazama okwenzakala ngo-2004 okwabuya kubhabhule isikhukhula njalo kwabulala abanengi.

Ngo-2018: Ukuzamazama okukhulu kwahlasela isihlenge esithandwa yizethekeleli zakwamanye amazwe eseLombok, e-Indonesia, kwafa abantu abedlula 500, njalo abanengi bakhona babesenyakatho yesihlenge lesi.

Abatshutshisi beNew York bafuna uSayfullo Saipov abulawe, kucatshangengelwa ukuthi ngoweqembu elilwalicatsha obulele abantu abangu-8 eNew York City—isijeziso esinje sacina ukuba khona ngo1953 nxa umuntu enze icala esabelweni esizimele sodwa.
Kuthiwa ngo-Oct, uSaipov oleminyaka engu-30, wasebenzisa imota eqhatshiweyo ye-Home Depot ukuze ahlasele abantu abasebenzisa indlela yamabhayisikili eWest Side Highway eLower Manhattan, wabulala ababehamba ngenyawo lowayetshova ibhayisikili endleleni le.
Incwadi yomthetho omayelana lokugwetshelwa kwabantu ugodo, esemawofisini eSouthern District of New York ithi ukuze umuntu aphiwe isigwebo lesi abatshutshisi kuzamele balethe ubufakazi bokuthi uSaipov wakwenza “ngabomo” ukubulala abantu abangu-8 lokuthi walimaza abantu okuzwayo emzimbeni “ngabomo.”
Ngokwencwadi yemthethwandaba kubikwa ukuthi amacala womabili angenza ukuthi umuntu agwetshelwe ukubulawa.
Sokwedlule amaviki ukuhlasela lokhu kwenzakele, iqula labahluli besabelo laveza ukuthi uSaipov ulamacala angu-22, okugoqela angu-8 okubulala elenhloso yokuncedisa ekutholeni izinto ngokungekho emthethweni, icala lokuba lodlakela lelokubulala izimota, amacala anjengalawa andise ukuphathwa liqula labahluli.
Abatshutshisi bathe ukuhlasela lokhu “kwakufuna ukuhlelwa lokucabangisisa ngakho,” bathe indlela uSaipov abulala ngayo abantu laba itshengisa ukuthi “mubi, ulolunya futhi uxhwalile."
Umbiko okhuluma ngenhloso yokwenza lokhu uthe, “USayfullo Habibullaevic Saipov wabangela ukulimala, ubuhlungu lokulahlekelwa kwezihlobo labangane baka-Diego Enrique Angelini, Nicholas Cleves, Ann-Laure Decadt, Darren Drake, Ariel Erlij, Hernan Ferruchi, Hernan Diego Mendoza lo-Alejandro Damian Pagnucco.”

U.S. OweDiphathimenti lemthethwandaba leUS eyingcitshi yokuhlola okwenzakeleyo uPaul Rowlett, ufakaze okwamahora athile njengomfakazi wendaba zokuhlolisisa.

IThe High Breed: Kuyini okuthiwa yiconscious hip hop?
Abahlabeli abathathu abehip hop laba bafuna ukuntshintsha indlela engayisiyo ebonwa ngayo umculo lo, ngokuhlabela amazwi akhuthazayo.
IThe High Breed esuka eBristol ithi, umculo wehip hop watshiya izindlela zawo zakuqala ezokuhlabela ngezombusazwe njalo lendaba ezibamba impilo zabantu.

Omunye futhi umuntu omnyama?!
Uneni waseNY ubophisa indoda lomfazi ngemva kokuxotshwa umsebenzi ngemva kokuthunyelwa komlayezo "wokubandlula" efonini
Uneni waseNew York ubophisa indoda lomfazi ngenxa yokuxotshwa umsebenzi ngobandlululo ngemva kokwamukela umlayezo owasuka walahleka efonini uvela kumama ekhalaza ngokuthi yena wayengo "munye futhi umuntu omnyama."
Indoda lomfazi bayaphika ukuthi balobandlululo, befanisa ukubotshiswa kwabo "lokudinga imali ngezindlela eziphansi."
ULynsey Plasco-Flaxman, olabantwana ababili, wasala engasela nkani lapho ethola ukuthi omutsha owayezasebenza ukunakekela abantwana, uGiselle Maurice, wayengumuntu omnyama mhla efika ngelanga lakhe lokuqala umsebenzi ngo-2016.
"HAYI BOOOOOOOOOOOO OMUNYE FUTHI UMUNTU OMNYAMA," kwabhala uNksz Plasco-Flaxman kumyeni wakhe kumlayezo efonini.
Kodwa, kulokuthi awuthumele kumyeni wakhe, wawuthumela kuNks. Maurice, kabili.
Ngemva kokunanzela ukulahla kwakhe umlomo, uPlasco-Flaxman "owayengasahlalisekanga" waxotsha uNks. Maurice emsebenzini, esithi uneni abakade belaye, obengumhlobo wamaMelika ase-Africa, wasebenza kubi njalo yena ubilindele umuntu ongomFilipino, njengokutsho kweNew York Post.
UMaurice waphiwa umholo wakhe welanga elilodwa wasebizelwa i-Uber ukuba abuyele ngekhaya.
Manje, uMaurice usebophisa indoda lomfazi efuna ukuhlawulwa ngenxa yokuxotshwa umsebenzi, njalo ufuna ukuhlawulwa ngemali engange-$350 ngelanga okwezinyanga eziyisithupha, okukade kuthiwe uzazisebenza ehlala khona, lanxa bekungela sivumelwano esibhaliweyo.
"Ngifuna ukubatshengisa ukuthi, khangelani, into enje kayenziwa," watshela iPost ngoLwesihlanu, wangezelela "ngiyakwazi ukuthi yikubandlulula."
Indoda lomfazi labo baphika ukumangalelwa kokuthi balobandlululo, besithi ukumisa uMaurice umsebenzi kwakuyinto elengqondo ababengayenza, besesabela ukuthi babengasamthembi ngemva kokuba sebemkhubile.
"Unkosikazi wami wamthumela okuthile okungayisikho ayekutsho.
Kasuye muntu obandlululayo.
Kasisibo bantu ababandlululayo," indoda yakhona uJoel Plasco yatshela iPost.
"Kodwa ungafaka yini abantwana bakho ezandleni zomuntu oke wameyisa, lanxa ukwenze ngokuphambanisa?
Usane lwakho olusanda kuzalwa?
Loba sekuthiwani."
Efanisa ukubotshiswa kwabo "lokudinga imali ngezindlela eziphansi," uPlasco wathi kwasekusele izinyanga ezimbili nje ukuba unkosikazi wakhe abelethe njalo "wayesesimweni esinzima kakhulu."
"Ubungakhetha umuntu onjalo?
Kasiyonto enhle yokwenza," osebenza izimali ebhanga wangezelela.
Lanxa udaba lwasemthethweni lusaqhubekela phambili, umthethwandaba wemibono yabantu uphangise ukusola indoda lomfazi kwezokuxhumana, ubasola ngobuntu babo kanye lendlela yabo yokucabanga.

Sokumangalisa khathesi ukuba kwazi ukuthi uPaddington wacina esephumelele kakhulu."

Lanxa kunguye owamulungisayo njalo kuyimicabango yakhe, wayejayele ukunika uPaddington udumo."
Indodakazi yami yayisisifa, njalo kwakumele ngiyivalelise efonini
Esanda kuyehla indodakazi yakhe igijinyiswe esibhedlela esithiwa yiNice's Hospital Louis Pasteur 2, lapho odokotela abasebenze nzima ukuthi bamsilise kodwa kungela lathemba.

"Ngabesengifonelwa nguNad engitshela ukuthi indodakazi yami izakufa phakathi kwemizuzu emibili elandelayo njalo kwakumele ngiyivalelise.
Ngayivalelisa sibili.
Ngathi, "Tashi, ngiyakuthanda kakhulu, sithandwa.
Sizabe sesisonke khathesi.
Sizabe sesisonke.
Imithi kade bemunike yona bodokotela ukuthi inhliziyo yakhe iqhubeke itshaya ibilokhu iphela amandla kancane kancane njalo kade isiphuma emzimbeni wakhe.
Kade esefile kudala, yikho konke besokuphelile.
Akula kade ngizakwenza ngaphandle kokuhlala lokumelela ngikwazi ukuthi yikho okwenzakalayo lokhu.
Bengingakwanisi ukulila, ukuhlaba umkhosi kumbe ukukhala ngoba bengilabemuli labanye abantu.
Bekumele ngizibambe."
Ekucineni umama uEdnan-Laperouse osephakathi kokukhala ngokulahlekelwa yindodakazi yakhe sokumele agadhe indizamutshina labanye abantu - abangela ngitsho lolwazi ngalokhu okwenzakala kuye.
"Akula okwaziyo," watsho njalo.
"Bengilokhu ngiyehlise ikhanda ngapha inyembezi zisiwa isikhathi sonke.
Kunzima ukukuchasisa, kodwa ngithe sengiphakathi kwendizamutshina yikho lapho engicabange ukuthi kumele ngizwele uNad kakhulu.
Wayefuna uthando lwami lokuzwisisa.
Ngangikwazi ukuthi wayemuthanda kakhulu."
Abafazi abaphakathi kobuhlungu bafaka amakhadi ebhirijini ukuthi bazame ukuvimbela ukuzibulala kwabantu
Abafazi ababili abafelwe lamalunga ezimuli zabo ngokuzibulala, bazama ukuncedisa ukuthi bavimbele abanye abantu bengazibulali.
USharon Davis loKelly Humphreys, bebefaka amakhadhi ebhirijini leWelsh alemilayezo ekhuthazayo lenombolo zamafoni ezokuthi abantu bafone nxa befuna uncedo.
Indodana kamama uDavis okuthiwa nguTyler, wayeleminyaka engu13 lapho eze eqalise ukuhlaselwa yikudana kakhulu njalo eseleminyaka engu18 wazibulala.
"Kangifuni ukuthi noma ngumzali uphi azizwe ngendlela engihlala ngizizwa ngayo suku lunye ngalunye," watsho njalo umama lo.
Umama uDavis oleminyaka engu45 ohlala eLydney, wathi umntanakhe wayezakuba ngumpheki omuhle njalo owayebobotheka.
"Umuntu wonke wayemazi ngokubobotheka.
Babehlala besithi ukubobotheka kwakhe, kwenza ukuthi abantu bahlaliseke."
Lanxa kunjalo, watshiya umsebenzi engakafi ngoba "isimo ayekuso sasesimbi."
Ngo2014, umnewabo kaTyler owayeleminyaka engu11 ngaleso sikhathi, nguye owabonayo isidumbu sikamfowabo esezibulele.
Umama uDavis wathi: "Ngihlala ngikhathazeka ngicabanga ukuthi akumuphambanisanga yini lokhu."
Umama uDavis ulungisa amakhadi lawa "ukuthi ancede abantu babekwazi ukuthi kulabanye abantu ongakwanisa ukuthi uhambe kubo ukhulume labo kungabe ngumngane wakho.
Ungahlali uthule - kumele ukhulume."
Umama uHumphreys osengumngane kamama uDavis okweminyaka, laye walahlekelwa nguMark umkakhe oweminyaka engu15, kungela sikhathi umama kamkakhe efile.
"Wayengakhulumi ukuthi uyakhathazeka kumbe udanile, wayengakhulumi lutho," watsho njalo.
"Sokusele amalanga amalutshwana ukuthi sifike kuKristimasi, saqalisa ukubona ukuntshintsha ebuntwini bakhe.
Ngelanga leKristimasi wayesephelile - abantwana beze bevule izipho zabo wayehluleka lokubakhangela emehlweni, kumbe ukwenza enye into."
Wathi ukufa kwakhe kwabayethusa kakhulu kodwa kwakumele bazame ukukuyamukela: "Kuyaphambanisa imuli kakhulu.
Kusitshiya sidanile.
Kodwa kumele siqhubekele phambili sisilwa."
Nxa uphakathi kobunzima kokuthi umelane lempilo, uyakwanisa ukufonela amaSamaritans ungabhadhaliswi ku116 123 (eUK laseIreland), iemail yabo jo@samaritans.org kumbe uhambe kupeji yethu eyeSamaritans website elapha.

IPyongyang kayikakhulumi lutho ngokusobala.
Abanengi ababaleka bevela eNyakatho Korea bacine sebephiwe imvumo yokuba yizakhamizi zaseNingizimu Korea.
ISeoul ithi abaseNyakatho Korea abedlula abangu-30 000 sebechaphe umngcele ngokungekho emthethweni selokhu kwaphela Impi yaseKorea ngo-1953.
Abanengi babaleka besedlula ngaseChina, elomngcele omude kakhulu leNyakatho Korea njalo kulula ukuchapha khona kulokusebenzisa indawo evikelwe kakhulu yeDemilitarised Zone (DMZ) ephakathi kwamazwe eKorea amabili.
IChina ibheka ababakelayo laba njengabazohlala elizweni ngokungekho emthethweni kulokubathi yiziphepheli njalo ihlala ibabuyisela kibo ngenkani.
Ubudlelwano phakathi kweNyakatho leNingizimu - kahle-kahle ezilokhu zisilwa - buthuthuke ngokucacileyo ezinyangeni ezisanda kudlula.

Sengicaphukile."
Abeseqhubekela phambili.
Ngabona kulicebo elilengqondo."

Ukuthi impi yezentengiselwano ye-US-China ingabanhle njani ngeBeijing
Ukuphahluka kwempi yezentengiselwano phakathi kwe-US leChina kwakuvala indlebe, njalo lanxa impi yakhona isesekhatshana lokuthi iphele, isikhala phakathi kwamazwe womabili singanceda iBeijing ngokuhamba kwesikhathi, kutsho izazi.
UDonald Trump, uMongameli wase-US, nguye owaqala ukudubula isixwayiso sokuqala ekuqaliseni komnyaka ngokubhadalisa umthelo izinto ezithengiswa kakhulu ngabeChina okugoqela amaphaneli asebenza ngelanga, insimbi le-aluminiyamu.
Ukukhwela okukhulu okusobala kwenzakale kuleliviki lemithelo emitsha ithinta izinto ezidula okwamadola angamabhiliyoni angu-200 (amaphawundi angamabhiliyoni angu-150), okutsho ukubhadalisa umthelo ingxenye yezinto zonke ezingena e-US zivela eChina.
Ngaso sonke isikhathi iBeijing iphindisela ngokufananayo, khathesi isanda kufaka imithelo yamaphesenti amahlanu kusiya kwalitshumi ezintweni ezivela eMelika ezamadola angamabhiliyoni angu-60.
IChina isifunge ukwenza ngokufanana le-US kukho konke, njalo umkhonomi wesibili omkhulu kulayo yonke emhlabeni ukhanya ungasoze uphangise ukucwayiza.
Ukwenza ukuthi iWashington yehle phansi kutsho ukuvuma lokho ekutshoyo, kodwa ukukhothamela i-US ngokusobala kungaba ngokuyangisa kakhulu kuXi Jinping, uMongameli waseChina.
Lanxa kunjalo, izazi zithi iBeijing ingawadlala kuhle amakhasi ayo, ukuncindezela kwempi yezentengiselwano kungasekela kuhle iChina ngokuhamba kwesikhathi ngokwehlisa ukweyamana kwezomnotho kwamazwe womabili.
"Iqiniso lokuthi isinqumo sokuphangisa kwezombusazwe kungaba seWashington kumbe eBeijing singabangela izimo eziqalisa ukwenza ukuthi ezingokomnotho zibe zimbi kuloba yiliphi ilizwe ngeqiniso kulengozi kakhulu ukwedlula lokho izibukeli ebezikubona ngaphambili," kwatsho u-Abigail Grace, osebenza labachwayisisayo bekhangele kakhulu i-Asia eCenter for New American Security, odla ingqondo.
ISyria ‘isikulungele’ ukuthi iziphepheli ziphenduke elizweni, kusho Umthungameli wogatsha lukahulumende lokusebenzelana lamanye amazwe.
ISyria ithi isikulungele kuphenduka kweziphepheli ngokuzithandela njalo icela uncedo ekwakheni kutsha ilizwe ngemva kokubhidlizwa yimpi okweminyaka eyisikhombisa.
Ekhuluma emhlanganweni weNhlanganiso yokumanyana kwamazwe omhlaba, Umthungameli wogatsha lukahulumende lokusebenzelana lamanye amazwe uWalid al-Moualem uthe umumo wezinto elizweni uqhubeka usiba ncono.
"Namuhla isimo sesincono njalo sesivikelekile sibonga inqhubelaphambili eyenziweyo ekuzivikeleni kubomalwecatsha,” utsho njalo.
Uhulumende uqhubekela phambili evuselela indawo ezabhidlizwa ngomalwecatsha ukuze izimo zibuyele kulokho ezaziyikho ngaphambili.
Zonke izinto sezimingomumo ukuthi iziphepheli ziphenduke ngokuzithandela elizweni lapho okwakudingeke ukuthi zibaleke ngenxa yabomalwecatsha kanye lezomnotho ezazisenza ukuphila kube nzima.
INhlanganiso yokumanyana kwamazwe omhlaba icabangela ukuthi abantu beSyria abedlula 5.5 miliyoni babaleka elizweni kusukela impi iqalisa ngomnyaka ka2011.
Ezinye izigidi eziyisithupha zabantu abasahlala elizweni badinga uncedo ukuze baphile.
UAl-Moualem uthe uhulumende waseSyria uyalwamukela uncedo ekwakheni kutsha lelilizwe elibhidlikileyo.
Kodwa ugcizelele ukuthi kasoze amukele uncedo olubuya lemithetho yalabo abuluphayo kumbe oluvela emazweni aphathisa kumvukela eSyria.
IEurope iqhubeke ileRyder Cup ngemva kokunqoba eParis
Iqembu leEurope linqobe emidlalweni eye2018 Ryder Cup ngokunqoba iqembu leUSA ngemihlomelo eyi16.5 - 10.5, eLe Golf National, phandle kweParis, eFrance.
IUS isinqotshwe kwezikhathi eziyisithupha ezilandeleneyo eEurope njalo kayizake inqobe kuRyder Cup eEurope kusukela ngo1993.
IEurope yathatha futhi umqhele njengoba iqembu labo elikhokhelwa nguThomas Bjorn owesiDanish, lifikise imihlomelo engu14.5 kade ifunakala ukuthi banqobe iUnited States.
Ingcitshi eyeUS, uPhil Mickelson kade eyehluleka emdlalweni yakhe yonke, utshaye ibhora lakhe lawela emanzini epar-3 egodini lesi16, okwenze ukuthi anqotshwe nguFrancesco Molinari.
Umdlali lo owegolf oweItaly uMolinari, uphumelele kumidlalo yakhe yonke okumenze ukuthi abe ngumdlali oyi-1 kubadlali abayi-4 ofikise i5-0-0, kuze kuqale indlela entsha yomdlalo lo ngo-1979.
Umdlali waseAmerica uJordan Spieth, bamnqobile ku5 lo 4, ngomunye umdlali ongakabi lodumo oweqembu leEurope, uThorbjorn Olesen oweDenmark.
Ingcitshi elizweni lonke kumdlalo lo uDustin Johnson unqontshwe ku2 lo 1 loIan Poulter oweEngland ongabe edlale umdalo wakhe wokucina oweRyder Cup.
Enye ingcitshi esenqobe okwesitshiyagalombili amaRyder Cups, uSpaniard Sergio Garcia ube ngumnqobi odlale kuhle kakhulu kumdlalo lo oweEurope obe lemihlomelo efika 25.5 kumidlalo yakhe yonke.
"Angijayelanga ukukhala kodwa namhla ngikhalile.
Umnyaka lo kade kungamanga kuhle.
Yikho ngimbonga uThomas ngokungiphakamisa njalo ngokungithemba.
Ngiyathokoza ngenxa yokuthi sinqobile.
Sikwenzela iqembu lokhu njalo ngiyajabula ukuthi lami ngincedile," ukhulumile lokhu ekhala uGarcia, ngemva kokunqoba eEurope.
Usetshiyele omunye welizwe lakhe isipho uJohn Ram, ngoba unqobe ingcitshi eyegolf oweUSA uTiger Woods nge2 lo 1, bedlala bodwa ngeSonto.
"Khathesi ngizizwa ngiziqhenya kakhulu ngokunqoba uTiger Woods, yindoda engakhula ngiyibukela," watsho njalo uRahm oleminyaka engu23 yokuzalwa.
UWoods unqotshwe kumidlalo yakhe yonke emine eFrance, njalo khathesi umbiko wakhe usume kanje 13-21-3 kumidlalo yakhe yonke eyeRyder Cup.
Kuyinto esingazange siyibone leyi ukuthi ingcitshi yemidlalo yesikhathi sonke idukiswe kanje yona yake yanqoba ka14 emidlalweni emikhulu, elandela uJack Nicklaus.
Iqembu leUSA liyehluleke ukuhlohla amabhora abo ngaphandle kukaPatrick Reed, loJustin Thomas kanye loTony Finau, abadlale umdlalo owaphezulu owegolf kumudlalo wonke.
Umkhokheli weqembu leUS uJim Furyk, ukhulumile ngemva komdlalo odanisayo weqembu lakhe uthe, "Ngiyaziqhenya ngamadoda lawa, balwile.
Kuke kwaba lesikhathi ekuseni lapho esike sayethusela iEurope.
Silwile.
Siyamuhlonipha uThomas.
Ngumkhokheli omuhle.
Abadlali bakhe bonke abayi-12, badlale kuhle.
Sizaqalisa kutsha, ngizasebenza lePGA eyeAmerica kanye lekhomithi eyeRyder Cup yethu njalo siqhubeke phambili.
Ngiyawathanda amadoda angu-12 lawa, njalo ngiyaziqhenya ukuba ngumkhokheli wabo.
Kumele ubahloniphe.
Basinqobile."
Isimo seRed Tide Okwakhathesi: Ubunengi bayo buyehla ePinellas, eManatee laseSarasota
Umbiko osanda kuphuma ovela kuKhomishini yeFlorida Fish and Wildlife utshengisa ukwehla kobunengi beRed Tide ezingxenyeni zasendaweni yaseTampa Bay.
NgokweFWC, izimo zokwanda okuyiziqayiqa ziyabikwa ezindaweni zasezabelweni zePinellas, eManatee, eSarasota, eCharlotte leCollier - okutshengisa ubunengi obehlayo.
Ukwanda kweRed Tide kufinyelela aphose abe ngamamayila angu-130 (amakhilomitha angu-209) asokhunjini ukusukela ezabelweni ezisenyakatho Pinellas kusiya kweziseningizimu Lee.
Iziqayiqa ziyatholakala okungaba okwamamayila angu-10 (amakhilomitha angu-16) usuka okhunjini lweSabelo seHillsborough, kodwa yizindawo ezilutshwana nxa kulinganiswa lezeviki edlulileyo.
IRed Tide ibonakele futhi eSabalweni sePasco.
Ubunengi obuphakathi laphakathi emanzini aseduze kumbe khatshana lasokhunjini lwesabelo sePinellas bubikiwe ngeviki edlulileyo, ubunengi obuphansi kusiya kobuphezulu khatshana lasokhunjini lweSabelo seHillsborough, ubunengi obungasemuva kusiya kobuphezulu eSabelweni seManatee, ubunengi obungasemuva kusiya kobuphezulu eduze kumbe khatshana lasokhunjini kweSabelo seSarasota, ubunengi obungasemuva kusiya kobuphezulu eSabelweni seCharlotte, ubunengi obungasemuva kusiya kobunengi emanzini aseduze kumbe khatshana lasokhunjini lweSabelo seLee, kanye lobunengi obuphansi eSabelweni seCollier.
Ukuphambaniseka ekuphefumuleni kuqhubeka kubikwa ezabelweni zePinellas, eManatee, eSarasota, eLee laseCollier.
Akuzange kubikwe ukuphambaniseka ekuphefumuleni eNyakatho-ntshonalanga Florida evikini edlulileyo.
